Subhv tāṃ bhavānīṃ bhavānītakleśanāśaviśāradām 
Subhv śāradāṃ śāradām bhodasitaṃsihāsanāṃ numaḥ 
Subhv anapekṣitaguruvacanā sarvāngranthīnvibhedayati samyak 
Subhv prakaṭayati pararahasyaṃ vimarśaśaktirnijā jayati 
Subhv dikkālādyanavacchinnānantacinmātramūrtaye 
Subhv svānubhūtyekamānāya namaḥ śāntāya tejase 
Subhv jagatsisṛkṣāpralayakriyāvidhau
Subhv prayatnamunmeṣanimeṣavibhramam 
Subhv vadanti yasyekṣaṇalolapakṣmaṇāṃ
Subhv parāya tasmai parameṣṭhine namaḥ 
Subhv namastribhuvanotpattisthitisaṃhārahetave 
Subhv viṣṇavepārasaṃsārapārottaraṇasetave 
Subhv surāsuraśiroratnakāntivicchuritāṅghraye 
Subhv namastribhuvaneśāya haraye siṃharūpiṇe 
Subhv namastasmai varāhāya helayoddharate mahīm 
Subhv khuramadhyagato yasya meruḥ khurakhurāyate 
Subhv namastuṅgaśiraścumbicandracāmaracārave 
Subhv trailokyanagarārambhamūlastambhāya śaṃbhave 
Subhv abhipretārthasiddhyarthaṃ pūjito yaḥ surairapi 
Subhv sarvavighnacchide tasmai gaṇādhipataye namaḥ 
Subhv nitambālasagāminyaḥ pīnonnatapayodharāḥ 
Subhv manmathāya namastasmai yasyāyatanamaṅganāḥ 
Subhv anantamāmadheyāya sarvākaravidhāyine 
Subhv samastamantravācyāya viśvaikapataye namaḥ 
Subhv oṃ namaḥ paramārthaikarūpāya paramātmane 
Subhv svecchāvabhāsitāsatyabhedabhinnāya śaṃbhave 
Subhv kulaśailadalaṃ pūrṇasuvarṇagirikarṇikam 
Subhv namodhitiṣṭhatenantanālaṃ kamalaviṣṭaram 
Subhv karṇikādiṣviva svarṇamarṇavādiṣvivodakam 
Subhv bhediṣvabhedi yattasmai parasmai mahase namaḥ 
Subhv namo vāṅmanasātītamahimne parameṣṭhine 
Subhv triguṇāṣṭaguṇānantaguṇannirguṇamūrtaye 
Subhv namaḥ śivāya niḥśeṣakleśapraśamaśāline 
Subhv triguṇagranthidurbhedabhavabandhavibhedine 
Subhv samastalakṣaṇāyoga eva yasyopalakṣaṇam 
Subhv tasmai namostu devāya kasmaicidapi śaṃbhave 
Subhv saṃsāraikanimittāya saṃsāraikavirodhine 
Subhv namaḥ saṃsārarūpāya niḥsaṃsārāya śaṃbhave 
Subhv yathā tathāpi yaḥ pūjyo yatra tatrāpi yorcitaḥ 
Subhv yopi vā sopi vā yosau devastasmai namostu te 
Subhv sadasattvena bhāvānāṃ yuktā yā dvitayī sthitiḥ 
Subhv tāmullaṅghya tṛtīyasmai namaścitrāya śaṃbhave 
Subhv namaḥ svatantracicchaktimudritasvavibhūtaye 
Subhv avyaktavyaktarūpāya kasmaicinmantramūrtaye 
Subhv āsannāya sudūrāya guptāya prakaṭātmane 
Subhv sulabhāyātidurgāya namaścitrāya śaṃbhave 
Subhv carācarajagatsphārasphurattāmātradharmiṇe 
Subhv durvijñeyarahasyāya yuktairapyātmane namaḥ 
Subhv viṣṇurvā tripurāntako bhavatu vā brahmā surendrothavā
Subhv bhānurvā śaśalakṣaṇotha bhagavānbuddhotha siddhothavā 
Subhv rāgadveṣaviṣārtimoharahitaḥ sattvānukampodyato
Subhv yaḥ sarvaiḥ saha saṃskṛto guṇaguṇaistasmai namaḥ sarvadā 
Subhv ślokoyaṃ svāmidattasya tatsmṛtyai kāvyalakṣitaḥ 
Subhv yokarotkavināmāṅkaṃ cakrapāṇiyayābhidham 
Subhv bhavabījāṅkurajaladā rāgādyāḥ kṣayamupāgatā yasya 
Subhv brahmā vā viṣṇurvā haro jino vā namastasmai 
Subhv kastūrītilakaṃ lalāṭaphalake vakṣaḥsthale kaustubhaṃ
Subhv nāsāgre navamauktikaṃ karatale veṇuṃ kare kaṅkaṇam 
Subhv sarvāṅge haricandanaṃ suvimalaṃ kaṇṭhe ca muktāvalīṃ
Subhv bibhratstrīpariveṣṭito vijayate gopālacūḍāmaṇiḥ 
Subhv aviratāmbujasaṃgatisaṃgaladbahalakesarasaṃvaliteva vaḥ 
Subhv lalitavastuvidhānasukhollasattanuruhā tanurātmabhuvovatāt 
Subhv lakṣmīkapolasaṃkrāntakāntapattralatojjvalāḥ 
Subhv dordrumāḥ pāntu vaḥ śaurerghanacchāyā mahāphalāḥ 
Subhv pātu vo medinīdolā balendudyutitaskarī 
Subhv daṃṣṭrā mahāvarāhasya pātalagṛhadīpakā 
Subhv madamayamadamayaduragaṃ yamunāmavatīrya vīryaśālī yaḥ 
Subhv mama ratimamaratiraskṛtiśamanapuraḥ sa kriyātkṛṣṇaḥ 
Subhv sa pātu vo yasya hatāvaśeṣās
Subhv tattulyavarṇāñjanarañjiteṣu 
Subhv vālaṇyayukteṣvapi vitrasanti
Subhv daityāḥ svakāntānayanotpaleṣu 
Subhv caṇḍacāṇūradordaṇḍamaṇḍalīkhaṇḍamaṇḍitam 
Subhv avyādvo bālaveṣasya viṣṇorgopatanorvapuḥ 
Subhv govardhanoddharaṇahṛṣṭasamastagopa
Subhv nānāstutiśravaṇalajjitamānasasya 
Subhv smṛtvā varāhavapurindukalāprakāśa
Subhv daṃṣṭroddhṛtakṣiti hareravatu smitaṃ vaḥ 
Subhv manthakṣmādharaghūrṇitārṇavapayaḥ pūrāntarālollasal
Subhv lakṣmīkandalakomalāṅgadalanaprādurbhavatsaṃbhramāḥ 
Subhv harṣotkaṇṭakitatvaco madhuripordevāsurākarṣaṇa
Subhv vyāpāroparamāya pāntu jagatīmābaddhavīpsā giraḥ 
Subhv pṛṣṭhabhrāmyadamandamandaragirigrāvāgrakaṇḍūyanān
Subhv nidrāloḥ kamaṭhākṛterbhagavataḥ śvāsānilāḥ pāntu vaḥ 
Subhv yatsaṃskārakalānuvartanavaśādvelānibhenāmbhaso
Subhv yātāyātamatandritaṃ jalanidhernādyāpi viśrāmyati 
Subhv kiṃcitkuñcitalocanasya pibataḥ paryāptamekaṃ stenaṃ
Subhv sadyaḥprasrutadughavindumaparaṃ hastena saṃmārjataḥ 
Subhv mātraikāṅgulilālitasya cibuke smerānanasyānanā
Subhv cchaureḥ kṣīrakaṇāvalīva patitā dantadyutiḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv kālindīpulinodareṣu musalī yāvadgataḥ krīḍituṃ
Subhv tāvatkarburikāpayaḥ piba hare vardhiṣyate te śikhā 
Subhv itthaṃ bālatayā pratāraṇaparāḥ śrutvā yaśodāgiraḥ
Subhv pāyādvaḥ svaśikhāṃ spṛśanpramuditaḥ kṣīrerdhapīte hariḥ 
Subhv ānandena yaśodayā samadanaṃ gopāṅganābhiściraṃ
Subhv sāśaṅkaṃ balavidviṣā sakusumaṃ siddhaiḥ pṛthivyākulam 
Subhv serṣyaṃ gopakumārakaiḥ sakaruṇaṃ pauraiḥ suraiḥ sasmitaṃ
Subhv yo dṛṣṭaḥ sa punātu vo madhuripuḥ protkṣipragovardhanaḥ 
Subhv kṛṣṇenāmba gatena rantumadhunā mṛdbhakṣitā svecchayā
Subhv satyaṃ kṛṣṇa ka evamāha musalī mithyāmba paśyānanam 
Subhv vyādehīti vikāsitetha vadane mātā samastaṃ jagad
Subhv dṛṣṭvā yasya jagāma vismayavaśaṃ pāyātsa vaḥ keśavaḥ 
Subhv kiṃ yuktaṃ bata māmananyamanasaṃ vakṣaḥsthalasthāyinīṃ
Subhv bhaktāmapyavadhūya kartum adhunā kāntāsahasraṃ tava 
Subhv ityuktvā phaṇabhṛtphaṇāmaṇigatāṃ svāmeva matvā tanuṃ
Subhv nidrāchedakaraṃ hareravatu vo lakṣmyā vilakṣasmitam 
Subhv svaprāsāditadarśanāmanunayanprāneśvarīmādarā
Subhv daṃsesminpatitairapāṅgavalitairyadbodhitopyaśrubhiḥ 
Subhv pratyāyyastvamato mayā nanu hare koyaṃ kramavyatyayaḥ
Subhv pātu tvāṃ vrajayoṣitetyabhihitaṃ lajjākar śārṅgiṇaḥ 
Subhv bhaktiprahvavilokanapraṇayiṇī nīlotpalaspardhinī
Subhv dhyānālambanatāṃ samādhiniratairnīte hitaprāptaye 
Subhv lāvaṇyasya mahānidhī rasikatāṃ lakṣmīdṛśostanvatī
Subhv yuṣmākaṃ kurutāṃ bhavārtiharaṇaṃ netre tanurvā hareḥ 
Subhv yena dhvastamanobhavena balijitkāyaḥ purāstrīkṛto
Subhv yaścodvṛttabhujaṃgarahāravalayo gaṅgāṃ ca yodhārayat 
Subhv yasyāhuḥ śaśimacchiro hara iti stutyaṃ ca nāmāmarāḥ
Subhv pāpātsa svayamandhakakṣayakarastvāṃ sarvadomādhavaḥ 
Subhv kiṃcinnirmucyamāne gagana iva mukhe nāṭyanidrāpayodair
Subhv nyakkurvāṇe svabhāsā phaṇipatiśirasāṃ ratnadīpāṃśujālam 
Subhv pāyāstāṃ vo muroreḥ śaśitapanamaye locane yadvibhāsā
Subhv lakṣmyā kastasthamardhaṃ vikasati kamalasyārdhamabhyeti nidrām 
Subhv mallaiḥ śailendrakalpaḥ śiśurakhilajanaiḥ puṣpacāpoṅganābhir
Subhv gopaistu prākṛtātmā divi kuliśabhṛtā viśvakāyoprameyaḥ 
Subhv kruddhaḥ kaṃsena kālo bhayacakitadṛśā yogibhirdhyeyamūrtir
Subhv dṛṣṭo raṅgāvatāre hariramarajanānandakṛtpātu yuṣmān 
Subhv bhindannarātihṛdayāni hareḥ punātu
Subhv niḥśvāsavātamukharīkṛtakoṭaro vaḥ 
Subhv saṃkrāntakukṣikuharāspadasaptasindhu
Subhv saṃghaṭṭaghorataraghoṣa ivāśu śaṅkhaḥ 
Subhv pāyātsa vaḥ kumudakundamṛṇālagauraḥ
Subhv śaṅkho hareḥ karatalāmbarapūrṇacandraḥ 
Subhv nādena yasya suraśatruvilāsinīnāṃ
Subhv kāñcyo bhavanti śithilā jaghanasthalīṣu 
Subhv dṛṣṭasya yasya hariṇā raṇamūrdhni mūrtir
Subhv udbhūtaduḥsahamahaḥprasarā samantāt 
Subhv tallocanasthitaravipratibimbagarbhe
Subhv vābhāti cakramaricakranudestu tadvaḥ 
Subhv udvṛttadaityapṛtanāpatikaṇṭhapīṭha
Subhv cchedocchaladbahalaśoṇitaśoṇadhāram 
Subhv cakraṃ kriyādabhimatāni harerudāra
Subhv digdāhadāruṇanabhaḥśriyamudvahadvaḥ 
Subhv yasyodyadbāṇavāhudrumagahanavanacchedagoṣṭhīkuṭhāraṃ
Subhv cakraṃ niṣkrāntatīvrānalabahalakaṇākīrṇadhāraṃ vicintya 
Subhv jātagrāsāvasāyo divasakṛtisalanmāṃsalāṃśupravāhe
Subhv muhyatyadyāpi rāhuḥ sa dahatu duritānyāśu daityāntako vaḥ 
Subhv daityāsthipañjaravidāraṇalabdharandhra
Subhv raktāmbunirjarasariddhanajātapaṅkāḥ 
Subhv bālendukoṭikuṭilāḥ śukacañcubhāso
Subhv rakṣantu siṃhavapuṣo nakharā harervaḥ 
Subhv ādityāḥ kiṃ daśaite pralayabhayakṛtaḥ svīkṛtākāśadeśāḥ
Subhv kiṃ volkāmaṇḍalāni tribhuvanadahanāyodyatānīti bhītaiḥ 
Subhv pāyāsurnārasiṃhaṃ vapuramaragaṇairbibhrataḥ śārṅgapāṇer
Subhv dṛṣṭvā dṛptāsurorastaladaraṇagaladraktaraktā nakhā vaḥ 
Subhv merūrukesaramudāradigantapattram
Subhv āmūlalambicalaśeṣaśarīranālam 
Subhv yenoddhṛtaṃ kuvalayaṃ salilātsalīlam
Subhv uttaṃsakārthamiva pātu sa vo varāhaḥ 
Subhv na mṛdnīyānmṛdvī kathamiva mahī potranikaṣair
Subhv mukhāgnijvālābhiḥ kanakagirirīyānna vilayam 
Subhv na śuṣyeyuḥ śvāsaiḥ salilanidhayaḥ sapta ca kathaṃ
Subhv varāho vaḥ pāyāditi vipulacintāparikaraḥ 
Subhv svāmī sanbhuvanatrayasya vikṛtiṃ nītosi kiṃ yācñayā
Subhv yadvā viśvasṛjā tvayaiva na kṛtaṃ taddīyatāṃ te kutaḥ 
Subhv dānaṃ śreṣṭhatamāya tubhyamatulaṃ bandhāya no muktaye
Subhv vijñapto balinā niruttaratayā hrīto hariḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv līne śrotraikadeśe nabhasi nayanayostejasi kvāpi yāte
Subhv śvāsagrāsopayukte maruti jalanidhau pāyurandhrārdhapīte 
Subhv potraprāntaikaromāntaravivaragatāṃ mṛgyataḥ śārṅgapāṇeḥ
Subhv kroḍākārasya pṛthvīmakalitaviṣayaṃ vaibhavaṃ vaḥ punātu 
Subhv kvedānīṃ darpitāste ghanamadamadirāmodino digdhipendrā
Subhv he mero mandarāndre malaya himagire sādhu vaḥ kṣmādharatvam 
Subhv śeṣa ślāghyosi dīrghaiḥ pṛthubhuvanabharoccaṇḍaśauṇḍaiḥ śirobhiḥ
Subhv śaṃsansotprāsamuccairiti dharaṇibhṛtaḥ pātu yuṣmānvarāhaḥ 
Subhv āvyādvo vāmano yasya kaustubhapratibimbitā 
Subhv kautukālokinī jātā jāṭharīva jagattrayī 
Subhv ekasthaṃ jīviteśe tvayi sakalajagatsāramālokayāmaḥ
Subhv śyāme cakṣustavāsminvapuṣi niviśate nālpapuṇyasya puṃsaḥ 
Subhv kasyānyatrāmṛtesminratirativipulā dṛṣṭirevāmṛtaṃ te
Subhv daityairityucyamāno munibhirapi hariḥ straiṇarūpovatādvaḥ 
Subhv bhrāmyanmahāgirinigharṣaṇalabdhapṛṣṭha
Subhv kaṇḍūyanakṣaṇasukhāyitagāḍhanidraḥ 
Subhv suṣvāpa dīrghataraghargharaghoraghoṣaḥ
Subhv śvāsābhibhūtajaladhiḥ kamaṭhaḥ sa vovyātu 
Subhv sa dhūrjaṭijaṭājūṭo jāyatāṃ vijayāya vaḥ 
Subhv yasyaikapalitabhrāntiṃ karotpadyāpi jāhnavī 
Subhv sa pātu vo yasya jaṭākalāpe
Subhv sthitaḥ śaśāṅkaḥ sphuṭahāragauraḥ 
Subhv nīlotpalānāmiva nālapuñje
Subhv nidrāyamāṇaḥ śaradīva haṃsaḥ 
Subhv diśyātsa śītakiraṇābharaṇaḥ śivaṃ vo
Subhv yasyottamāṅgabhuvi visphuradūrmipakṣā 
Subhv haṃsīva nirmalaśaśāṅkakalāmṛṇāla
Subhv kandārthinī surasarinnabhasaḥ papāta 
Subhv śreyāṃsi vo diśatu yasya sitābhraśubhrā
Subhv vibhrājate surasaridvaramaulimālā 
Subhv ūrdhvekṣaṇajvalanatāpavilīyamāna
Subhv candrāmṛtapravitatāmṛtavāhinīva 
Subhv cyutāmindorlekhāṃ ratikalahabhagnaṃ ca valayaṃ
Subhv śanairekīkṛtya prahasitamukhī śailatanayā 
Subhv avocadyaṃ paśyotyavatu sa śivaḥ sā ca girijā
Subhv sa ca krīḍācandro daśanakiraṇāpūritatanuḥ 
Subhv eṣā te hara kā sugātri katamā mūrdhni sthitā kiṃ jaṭā
Subhv haṃsaḥ kiṃ bhajate jaṭāṃ nahi śaśī candro jalaṃ sevate 
Subhv mugdho bhūtiriyaṃ kutotra salilaṃ bhūtistaraṅgāyate
Subhv evaṃ yo vinigūhate tripathagāṃ pāyātsa vaḥ śaṃkaraḥ 
Subhv āśleṣādharavimbacumbanasukhālāpasmitānyāsatāṃ
Subhv dūre tāvadidaṃ mitho na sulabhaṃ jātaṃ mukhālokanam 
Subhv itthaṃ vyarthakṛtaikadehaghaṭanopanyāsayorāvayoḥ
Subhv keyaṃ premaviḍambanetyavatu vaḥ smerordhanārīśvaraḥ 
Subhv mātarjīva kimetadañjalipuṭe tātena gopāyyate
Subhv vatsa svādu phalaṃ prayacchati na me gatvā gṛhāṇa svayam 
Subhv mātraivaṃ prahite gṛhe vighaṭayatyākṛṣya saṃdhyāñjaliṃ
Subhv śaṃbhorbhinnasamādhiruddharabhaso hāsodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv ekaṃ cantacchadasya sphurati japavaśādardhamanyatprakopād
Subhv ekaḥ pāṇiḥ praṇantuṃ śirasi kṛtapadaḥ kṣeptumanyastameva 
Subhv ekaṃ dhyānānnimīlatyaparamaviṣahaṃ vīkṣituṃ cakṣuritthaṃ
Subhv tulyānicchāpi vāmā tanuravatu sa vo yasya saṃdhyāvasāne 
Subhv śailarājatanayāstanayagmavyāpṛtāsyayugalasya gṛhasya 
Subhv śeṣavakrakamalāni malaṃ vo dugdhapānavidhurāṇi harantu 
Subhv karajālamapūrvaceṣṭitaṃ vastadabhīṣṭapradamastu tigmabhāsaaḥ 
Subhv kriyate bhavabandhanādvimuktiḥ praṇatānāmupasevitena yena 
Subhv yuṣmākamambaramaṇe prathame mayūkhās
Subhv te maṅgalaṃ vidadhatūdayarāgabhājaḥ 
Subhv kurvanti ye divasajanmamahotsaveṣu
Subhv sindūrapāṭalamukhīriva dikpuraṃdhrīḥ 
Subhv ābāhūdgatamaṇḍalāgrarucayaḥ saṃnaddhavakṣaḥsthalāḥ
Subhv soṣmāṇo vraṇino vipakṣahṛdaypronmāthinaḥ karkaśāḥ 
Subhv utsṛṣṭāmbaradṛṣṭavigrahabharā yasya smarāgresarā
Subhv yodhā vāravadhūstanāśca na dadhuḥ kṣobhaṃ sa vovyājjinaḥ 
Subhv kiṃ syādbhāsvānna bhānoramṛtaghanarasasyandinaḥ santi pādāḥ
Subhv kiṃ vā rākāśaśāṅko nahi tuhinaruciḥ kutracinniṣkalaṅkaḥ 
Subhv sākṣāccintāmaṇiḥ kiṃ vipulaphalamaṇeḥ saukumāryaṃ kutastyaṃ
Subhv saṃdehānmugdhadhībhiḥ prathamamiti muneḥ pātu dṛṣṭaṃ vapurvaḥ 
Subhv ciramāviṣkṛtaprītibhītayaḥ pāntu vo dviṣām 
Subhv valayajyāravonmiśrāścaṇḍyāḥ kodaṇḍakṛṣṭayaḥ 
Subhv diśyānmahāsuraśiraḥsarasīpsitāni
Subhv preṅkhannakhāvalimayūkhamṛṇālanālam 
Subhv caṇḍyāścalaccaṭulanūpuracañcarīka
Subhv jhāṃkārahāri caraṇāmburuhadvayam vaḥ 
Subhv savrīḍā dayitānane sakaruṇā mātaṅgacarmāmbare
Subhv satrāsā bhujage savismayarasā candremṛtasyandini 
Subhv serṣyā jahnusutāvalokanavidhau dīnā kapālodare
Subhv pārvatyā navasaṃgamapraṇayinī dṛṣṭiḥ śivāyastu vaḥ 
Subhv uttiṣṭhantyā ratānte bharamuragapatau pāṇinaikena kṛtvā
Subhv dhṛtvā cānyena vāso vigalitakabarībhāramaṃsaṃ vahantyāḥ 
Subhv bhūyastatkālakāntidviguṇitasurataprītinā śauriṇā vaḥ
Subhv śayyāmāliṅgya nītaṃ vapuralasalasadbāhu lakṣmyāḥ punātu 
Subhv pāyādgajendravadanaḥ sa imāṃ trilokīṃ
Subhv yasyodgatena gagane mahatā kareṇa 
Subhv mūlāvalagnasitadantabisāṅkureṇa
Subhv nālāyitaṃ tapanabimbasaroruhasya 
Subhv sānandaṃ nandihastāhatamurajaravāhvatakaumārabarhi
Subhv trāsānnāsāgrarandhraṃ viśati phaṇipatau bhogasaṃkocabhāji 
Subhv gaṇḍoḍḍīnālimālāmukharitakakubhastāṇḍave śūlapāṇer
Subhv vaināyakyaściraṃ vo vadanavidhutayaḥ pāntu sītkāravatyaḥ 
Subhv dhanurmālā maurvī kvaṇadalikulaṃ lakṣyamabalā
Subhv mano bhedyaṃ śabdaprabhṛtaya ime pañca viśikhāḥ 
Subhv iyāñjetuṃ yasya tribhuvanamadehasya vibhavaḥ
Subhv sa kāmaḥ kāmānvo diśatu dayitāpāṅgavasatiḥ 
Subhv brahmā dakṣaḥ kubero yamavaruṇamarudvahnicandrendrarudrāḥ
Subhv śailā nadyaḥ samudrā grahagaṇamanujā daityagandharvanāgāḥ 
Subhv dvīḥā nakṣatratārāravivasumunayo vyoma bhūraścinau ca
Subhv saṃlīnā yasya sarve vapuṣi sa bhagavāpātu vo viśvarūpaḥ 
Subhv mugdhe muñca viṣādamatra balajitkampo gurustyajyatāṃ
Subhv sadbhāvaṃ bhaja puṇḍarīkanayane mānyānimānmānaya 
Subhv lakṣmīṃ bodhayataḥ svayaṃvaravidhau dhanvantarervākchalā
Subhv danyatra pratiṣedhamātmani vidhiṃ śṛṇvanhariḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv diśyātsukhaṃ naraharirbhuvanaikavīro
Subhv yasyāhave ditisutoddalanodyatasya 
Subhv krodhoddhataṃ mukhamavekṣitumakṣamatvaṃ
Subhv jānebhavannijanakheṣvapi yannatāste 
Subhv svasti svāgatamarthyahaṃ vada vibho kiṃ dīyatāṃ medinī
Subhv kā mātrā mama vikramatrayapadaṃ dattaṃ gṛhītāṃ mayā 
Subhv mā dehītyuśanāḥ kuto harirayaṃ pātraṃ kimasmātparaṃ
Subhv yo hītthaṃ balinārcito makhamukhe pāyātsa vo vāmanaḥ 
Subhv cakra brūhi vibho gade jaya hare kambo samājñāpaya
Subhv bho bho nandaka jīva pannagariyo kiṃ nātha bhinno mayā 
Subhv ko daityaḥ katamo hiraṇyakaśipuḥ satyaṃ bhavadbhyaḥ śape
Subhv kenāstreṇa nakhairiti pravadato viṣṇormukhaṃ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv cintācakriṇi hanta cakriṇi bhiyā kubjāsanebjāsane
Subhv naśyaddhāmani tigmadhāmani dhṛtāśaṅke śaśāṅke bhṛśam 
Subhv bhraśyaccetasi ca pracetasi śucā tānte kṛtānte ca yo
Subhv vyagrobhūtkaṭukālakūṭakavalīkārāya pāyātsa vaḥ 
Subhv nityaṃ narāvṛti nijānubhavaikamānam
Subhv ānandadhāma jagadaṅkurabījamekam 
Subhv digdeśakālakalanādisamastahasta
Subhv mardāsahaṃ diśatu śarma mahanmaho vaḥ 
Subhv vyomnīva nīradabharaḥ sarasīva vīci
Subhv vyūhaḥ sahasramahasīva sudhāṃśudhām 
Subhv yasminnidaṃ jagadudeti ca līyate ca
Subhv tacchāmbhavaṃ bhavatu vaibhavamṛrddhaye vaḥ 
Subhv lokatrayasthitilayodayakelikāraḥ
Subhv kāryeṇa yo hariharadruhiṇatvameti 
Subhv devaḥ sa viśvajanavāṅmanasātivṛtti
Subhv śaktiḥ śivaṃ diśatu śaśvadanaśvaraṃ vaḥ 
Subhv sarvaḥ kilāyamavaśaḥ puruṣāṇukarma
Subhv kāyādikāraṇagaṇo yadanugraheṇa 
Subhv viśva prapañcaracanācaturatvameti
Subhv sa trāyatāṃ tribhuvanaikamaheśvaro vaḥ 
Subhv yaḥ kandukairiva puraṃdara padmasadma
Subhv padmāpatiprabhṛtibhiḥ prabhuraprameyaḥ 
Subhv khelatyalaṅghyamahimā sa himādrikanyā
Subhv kāntaḥ kṛtāntadalano laghayatvadhaṃ vaḥ 
Subhv muktirhi nāma paramaḥ puruṣārtha ekas
Subhv tāmantarāyamavayanti yadantarajñāḥ 
Subhv kiṃ bhūyasā bhavatu saiva sudhāmayūkha
Subhv lekhāśikhābharaṇabhaktirabhaṅgurā vaḥ 
Subhv śrīkaṇṭhasya sakṛttikārtabharaṇī mūrtiḥ sadārohiṇī
Subhv jyeṣṭhā bhadrapadā punarvasuyutā citrā viśākhānvitā 
Subhv diśyādakṣatahastamūlaghaṭitāṣāḍhā maghālaṅkṛtā
Subhv śreyo vaiśravaṇānvitā bhagavato nakṣatrapālīva vaḥ 
Subhv trātā bhītibhṛtāṃ patiścidacitāṃ kleśaṃ sataṃ śaṃsatāṃ
Subhv hantā bhaktimatāṃ satāṃ svasamatāṃ kartāpakartāsatām 
Subhv devaḥ sevakabhuktimuktiracanābhūrbhūrbhuvaḥsvastrayī
Subhv nirmāṇasthitisaṃhṛtiprakaṭitakrīḍo mṛḍaḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv rājā rājārcitāṅghreranupacitakalo yasya cūḍāmaṇitvaṃ
Subhv nāgā gāgātmajārdhaṃ na bhasitadhavalaṃ yadvapurbhūṣayanti 
Subhv mā rāmārāgiṇī bhūnmatiriti yamināṃ yena vodāhi māraḥ
Subhv sa ptāḥ saptāśvanunnāruṇakiraṇanibhāḥ pātu bibhrattrinetraḥ 
Subhv rādhāmohanamandiraṃ jagamiṣoścandrāvalīmandirād
Subhv rādho kṣemamiti priyasya vacanaṃ śrutvāha candrāvalī 
Subhv kṣemaṃ kaṃsa tataḥ priyaḥ prakupitaḥ kaṃsaḥ kva dṛṣṭastvayā
Subhv rādhā kveti tayoḥ prisannamanasorhāsodgamaḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv ākṛṣṭe yudhi kārmuke samavadadvāmaḥ karo dakṣiṇaṃ
Subhv re re dakṣiṇahasta bhojanamahādānādi te kurvataḥ 
Subhv paścādgantumayuktamityatha punaḥ sopyabravīdadravaṃ
Subhv praṣṭuṃ rāghavamāśu rāvaṇaśirovṛndāni bhindāni kim 
Subhv dṛṣṭaḥ kvāpi sa keśavo vrajavadhūmādāya kāṃcidgataḥ
Subhv sarvā eva hi vañcitāḥ khula vayaṃ sonveṣaṇīyo yadi 
Subhv dve dve gacchata ityudīrya sahasā rādhāṃ gṛhītvā kare
Subhv gopīveṣadharo nikuñjabhavanaṃ prāpto hariḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv mātastarṇakarakṣaṇāya yamunākacchaṃ na gacchāmyahaṃ
Subhv kasmādvatsa pinaṣṭi pīvarakucadvandvena gopījanaḥ 
Subhv bhrūbhaṅgairvinivāritopi bahuśo jalpanyaśodāgrato
Subhv gopībhiḥ karapadmamudritamukhaḥ pāyātsa vaḥ keśavaḥ 
Subhv saṃdhyāṃ yatpraṇipatya lokapurato baddhāñjaliryācase
Subhv dhatse yacca nadīṃ vilajja śirasā tannāma soḍhaṃ mayā 
Subhv śrīryātāmṛtamanthane yadi hariṃ kasmādviṣaṃ bhakṣitaṃ
Subhv mā strīlaṃpaṭa māṃ spṛśeti gadito gauryā haraḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv kastvaṃ śūlī mṛgaya bhiṣajaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaḥ priyehaṃ
Subhv kekāmekāṃ vada paśupatirnaiva dṛśye viṣāṇe 
Subhv mugdhe sthāṇuḥ sa carati kathaṃ jīviteśaḥ śivāyā
Subhv gacchāṭavyāmiti hatavacāḥ pātu vaścandracūḍaḥ 
Subhv koyaṃ dvāri hariḥ prayāhyupavanaḥ śākhāmṛgasyātra kiṃ
Subhv kṛṣṇohaṃ dayite bibhemi sutarāṃ kṛṣṇādahaṃ vānarāt 
Subhv mugdhehaṃ madhusūdanaḥ piba latāṃ tāmeva tanmīvale
Subhv itthaṃ nirvacanīkṛto dayitayā hrīto hariḥ pātu vaḥ 
Subhv nirlajja hare kimidaṃ pramadānugataḥ sadā paribhramasi 
Subhv mugdhe tvatsaṃparkātpramado bhavatīti kiṃ citram 
Subhv śaṭha varṇayāmi bhavato nārīṇāmuparibhūyasī prītiḥ 
Subhv pralapasi kimasaṃbaddhaṃ kasyāriṣu vidyate prema 
Subhv vyāmohayasi kimevaṃ rāmāsaktiṃ bravīmi bhavadīyām 
Subhv jyeṣṭhe bhrātari rāme na kriyatāṃ kathamivāsaktiḥ 
Subhv kiṃ māmevaṃ bhramayasi śocāmi vyasanameva bhavadīyam 
Subhv niṣkāraṇakupitāyāṃ tvayi kathaya kimalpakaṃ vyasanam 
Subhv vakravacanairamībhirgopavadhūmiti naruttarīkṛtya 
Subhv maṇḍalitagurupayodharamupagūḍhaṃ pātu vaḥ śaureḥ 
Subhv ayi saṃprasīda pārvati śivopi tava pādayornipatitoham 
Subhv śiva iti kathaṃ hi jalpasi sarudhiragajacarmasaṃvītaḥ 
Subhv śiva iti yadi tava gadite dviguṇo roṣo bhavāmyahaṃ sthāṇuḥ 
Subhv sthānurasi satyametaccetasi bhavato na kiṃcidapi 
Subhv tyaja ruṣamavehi mānini māmīśvaramarcitaḥ tribhuvanasya 
Subhv tryambaka yadīśvarastvaṃ nagnaḥ kiṃ dhūlidhūsaritaḥ 
Subhv saṃprati kimatra vakṣyasi paśupatireṣosmi pāṇḍurakapole 
Subhv paśupatireva na gaṇayasi yuktāyuktāni yasmāttvam 
Subhv mugdhe bhramasi kimevaṃ satyamimaṃ māṃ bhavaṃ vijānīhi 
Subhv satyaṃ bhavosi śaṭha he yenātivicitrarūposi 
Subhv paṇḍitabādastava yadi lokehaṃ tryambako vidita eṣaḥ 
Subhv ambā hyekāpi na te prajalpasi tvaṃ kutastisraḥ 
Subhv vādo mahānihaiva hi tathā vijānīhyanaṅgadahanaṃ mām 
Subhv dagdhamidamaṅgamaṅgaṃ tvayā mamaivedṛśaiścaritaiḥ 
Subhv saṃdhyāpraṇāmadoṣādyonunayati taṃ vijitya pārvatyā 
Subhv āliṅgitaśca sarabhasamurasā vai haratu duritaṃ vaḥ 
Subhv bhava niḥsnehastvaṃ me na bhavāmyevaṃ yathā tvayā gaditam 
Subhv niḥsnehatābhilāṣastava devi kutaḥ samutpannaḥ 
Subhv kusṛtibhiralametābhiḥ kimarthamuparisthitā nadīyaṃ te 
Subhv kā narakapālamālā mamoparisthā gṛhāṇaitāḥ 
Subhv janamanurāgiṇamevaṃ saṃtāpayasi vyalīkakaraṇena 
Subhv tava narakapālapaṅktibhiravaśyamevopari stheyam 
Subhv kiṃ kupitosi tyaja ruṣamapanayatāṃ vigrahaṃ mayā hi bhavān 
Subhv saha vigraho bhavatyā na jātu vighāṭiṣyatesmākam 
Subhv gaṅgāvigrahakaluṣāmiti śivavacanairniruttarāṃ gaurīm 
Subhv parihāsya yonuninye sa karotu śivaḥ śivaṃ bhavatām 
Subhv vijaye kuśalastryakṣo na krīḍitumahamanena saha śaktā 
Subhv vijaye kuśalosmi na tu tryakṣokṣadvayamidaṃ pāṇau 
Subhv kiṃ me durodareṇa prayātu yadi gaṇapatirna tebhimataḥ 
Subhv kaḥ pradveṣṭi vināyakamahilokaḥ kiṃ na jānāsi 
Subhv vasurahitena krīḍā bhavatā saha kīdṛśī na jihreṣi 
Subhv kiṃ vasubhinnamatomūnsurāsurāneva paśya puraḥ 
Subhv candragrahaṇena vinā nāsmi rame kiṃ pravartayasyevam 
Subhv devyai yadi rucitamidaṃ nandinnāhvayatāṃ rāhuḥ 
Subhv hā rāhau nikaṭasthe sitadaṃṣṭre bhayakṛti ratiḥ kasya 
Subhv yadi necchasi tattyaktaḥ saṃpratyevaiṣa hārāhiḥ 
Subhv āropayasi mudhā kiṃ nāhamabhijñā tvadaṅkasya 
Subhv divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ sthitvaivaṃ yuktamabhidhātum 
Subhv itthaṃ paśupatipeśalapāśakalīlāprayuktavakrokteḥ 
Subhv harṣavaśataralatārakamānanamavyādbhavānyā vaḥ 
Subhv aṅgulyā kaḥ kavāṭe praharati kuṭilo mādhavaḥ kiṃ vasanto
Subhv no cakrī kiṃ kulālo nahi dharaṇidharaḥ kiṃ praṇīndro dvijihvaḥ 
Subhv mugdhe ghorāhimāthī kimuta khagapatirno hariḥ kiṃ kapīndra
Subhv itthaṃ lakṣmyā kṛtosau pratihatavacanaḥ pātulakṣmīdhavo vaḥ 
Subhv khedaḥ kiṃ khalu dayite na vetsi ravimaṇḍalaṃ jagadviditam 
Subhv na krodhaḥ kartavyo jalacaramūrdhvaṃ na jātu paśyāmaḥ 
Subhv kopastyaktuṃ yogyo yasya pipāsā na saṃbhavati 
Subhv saṃtyaja mānini mānaṃ kiṃ mānenādhunā mamānena 
Subhv kiṃ tena kila kāvyena mṛdyamānasya yasya tāḥ 
Subhv udadheriva nāyānti rasāmṛtaparamparāḥ 
Subhv kiṃ kavestasya kāvyena kiṃ kāṇḍena dhanuṣmataḥ 
Subhv parasya hṛdaye lagnaṃ na ghūrṇayati yacchiraḥ 
Subhv apragalbhapadanyāsā jananīrāgahetavaḥ 
Subhv santyeke bahulālāpāḥ kavayo bālakā iva 
Subhv kiṃ tena kāvyamadhunā plāvitā rasanirjharaiḥ 
Subhv jaḍātmānopi no yasya bhavantyaṅkuritān tarāḥ 
Subhv navortho jātiragrāmyā śleṣokliṣṭaḥ sphuto rasaḥ 
Subhv vikaṭākṣarabandhaśca kṛtsnamekatra duṣkaram 
Subhv mukhamātreṇa kāvyasya karotyahṛdayo janaḥ 
Subhv chāyāmachāmapi śyāmāṃ rāhustārāpateriva 
Subhv boddhāromatsaragrastā vibhavaḥ smayadūṣitāḥ 
Subhv abodhopahatāścānye jīrnamaṅge subhāṣitam 
Subhv padadvayasya saṃdhānaṃ kartumapratibhāḥ khalāḥ 
Subhv tathāpi parakāvyeṣu duṣkareṣvapyasaṃbhramāḥ 
Subhv kva doṣotra mayā labhya iti saṃcintya cetasā 
Subhv khalaḥ kāvyeṣu sādhūnāṃ śravaṇāya pravartate 
Subhv upapattibhiramlānā nopadeśaiḥ kadarthitāḥ 
Subhv svasaṃvedanasaṃvedyasārāḥ sahṛdayoktayaḥ 
Subhv keṣāṃcidvāci śukavatpareṣāṃ hṛdi mūkavat 
Subhv kasyāpyā hṛdayādvaktre valgu valganti sūktayaḥ 
Subhv bahūni naraśīrṣāṇi lomaśāni bṛhanti ca 
Subhv grīvāsu pratibaddhāni kiṃcitteṣu sakarṇakam 
Subhv sādhvīva bhāratī bhāti sūktisadvratacāriṇī 
Subhv grāmyārthavastusaṃsparśabahiraṅgā mahākaveḥ 
Subhv te vandyāste mahātmānasteṣāṃ loke sthiraṃ yaśaḥ 
Subhv yairnibaddhāni kāvyānī ye vā kāvyeṣu kīrtitāḥ 
Subhv prasannāḥ kāntihāriṇyo nānāśleṣavicakṣaṇāḥ 
Subhv bhavanti kasyacitpuṇyairmukhe vāco gṛhe striyaḥ 
Subhv kavīnāṃ mahatāṃ sūktairgūḍhārthāntarasūcibhiḥ 
Subhv vidhyamānaśrutermā bhūhurjanasya kathaṃ vyathā 
Subhv yāsyati sajjanahastaṃ ramayiṣyati taṃ bhavecca nirdoṣā 
Subhv utpāditayāpi kavistāmyati kathayā duhitreva 
Subhv avasarapaṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ subhāṣitatvaṃ prayātpasūktamapi 
Subhv kṣudhi kadaśanamapi nitarāṃ bhoktuḥ saṃpadyate svādu 
Subhv durjanahutāśataptaṃ kāvyasuvarṇaṃ viśuddhimupayāti 
Subhv darśayitavyaṃ tasmānmatsarimanasaḥ prayatnena 
Subhv gaṇayanti nāpaśabdaṃ na vṛttabhaṅgaṃ kṣatiṃ na cārthasya 
Subhv rasikatvenākulitā veśyāpatayaḥ kukavayaśca 
Subhv vipulahṛdayābhiyogye khidyati kāvye jaḍo na maurkhye sve 
Subhv nindati kañcukameva prāyaḥ śuṣkastanā nārī 
Subhv khyātiṃ gamayati sujanaḥ sukavirvidadhāti kevalaṃ kāvyam 
Subhv puṣṇāti kamalamambho lakṣmyā tu ravirniyojayati 
Subhv vyākhyātumeva kecitkuśalāḥ śāstraṃ prayoktumalamanye 
Subhv upanāmayati karonnaṃ rasāṃstu jihbaiva jānāti 
Subhv jivita iva kaṇṭhagate sūkte duḥkhāsikā kavestāvat 
Subhv nayanavikāsavidhāyī sacetanābhyāgamo yāvat 
Subhv pratīyamānaṃ punaranyadeva
Subhv vastvasti vāṇīṣu mahākavīnām 
Subhv yattatprasiddhāvayavātirikta
Subhv mābhāti lāvaṇyamivāṅganāsu 
Subhv kaverabhiprāyamaśabdagocaraṃ
Subhv sphurantamārdreṣu padeṣu kevalam 
Subhv vadadbhiraṅgaiḥ kṛtaromavikriyair
Subhv janasya tūṣṇīṃbhavatoyamañjaliḥ 
Subhv sahṛdayāḥ kavigumphanikāsu ye
Subhv katipayāsta ime na viśṛṅkhalāḥ 
Subhv rasamayīṣu latāsviva ṣaṭpadā
Subhv hṛdayasārajuṣo na mukhaspṛśaḥ 
Subhv khyātā narādhipatayaḥ kavisaṃśrayeṇa
Subhv rājāśrayeṇa ca gatāḥ kavayaḥ prasiddhim 
Subhv rājñā samosti na kaveḥ paramopakārī
Subhv rājño na cāsti kavinā sadṛśaḥ sahāyaḥ 
Subhv cetaḥprasādajananaḥ vibuddhottamānām
Subhv ānandi sarvarasayuktamatiprasannam 
Subhv kāvyaṃ khalasya na karoti hṛdi pratiṣṭhāṃ
Subhv pīyūṣapānamiva vaktravivarti rāhoḥ 
Subhv baddhā yadarpaṇarasena vimardapūrvam
Subhv arthānkathaṃ jhaṭiti tānprakṛtānna dadyuḥ 
Subhv caurā ivātimṛdavo mahatāṃ kavīnām
Subhv arthāntarāṇyapi haṭhādvitaranti śabdāḥ 
Subhv tatkiṃ kāvyamanalpapītamadhuvatkuryānna yaddhṛdgataṃ
Subhv mātsaryāvṛtacetasāṃ rasavaśādapyudgatiṃ lomasu 
Subhv kampaṃ mūrdhni kapolayugmamaruṇaṃ bāṣpāvile locane
Subhv adhyāropitavastukīrtanaparaṃ vācaḥ karālambanam 
Subhv ye tāvatsvaguṇopabṛṃhitadhiyasteṣāmaraṇyaṃ jagad
Subhv yepyete kṛtamatsarāḥ paraguṇaṃ svapnepi necchanti te 
Subhv anyeṣāmanurāgiṇāṃ kvacidapi snigdhaṃ mano nirvṛtā
Subhv vitthaṃ yāntu tapovanāni mahatāṃ sūktāni manyedhunā 
Subhv yā sādhūniva sādhuvādamukharānmātsaryamūkānapi
Subhv proccairno kurute satāṃ matimatāṃ dṛṣṭirna sā vāstavī 
Subhv yā yātāḥ śrutigocaraṃ ca sahasā harṣollasatkaṃdharās
Subhv tiryañcopi na muktaśaṣpakavalāstāḥ kiṃ kavīnāṃ giraḥ 
Subhv svecchābhaṅgurabhāgyameghataḍitaḥ śakyā na roddhuṃ śriyaḥ
Subhv prāṇānāṃ satataṃ prayāṇapaṭahaśraddhā na viśrāmyati 
Subhv trāṇaṃ yetra yaśomaye vapuṣi vaḥ kurvanti kāvyāmṛtais
Subhv tānārādhyapade vidhatta sukavīnnirgarvamurvīśvarāḥ 
Subhv he rājānastyajata sukavipremabandhe virodhaṃ
Subhv śuddhā kīrtiḥ sphurati bhavatāṃ nūnametatprasādāt 
Subhv tuṣṭairbaddhaṃ tadalaghu raghusvāminaḥ saccaritraṃ
Subhv ruṣṭairnītastribhuvanajayī hāsyamārgaṃ daśāsyaḥ 
Subhv namo namaḥ kāvyarasāya tasmai
Subhv niṣiktamantaḥ pṛṣatāpi yasya 
Subhv suvarṇatāṃ vaktramupaiti sādhor
Subhv durvarṇatāṃ yāti ca durjanasya 
Subhv ajñātapāṇḍityarahasyamudrā
Subhv ye kāvyamārge dadhatebhimānam 
Subhv te gāruḍīyānanadhītya mantrān
Subhv hālāhalāsvādanamārabhante 
Subhv sarasvatīmāturabhūcciraṃ na yaḥ
Subhv kavitvapāṇḍityaghanastanaṃdhayaḥ 
Subhv kathaṃ sa sarvāṅgamanāptasauṣṭhavo
Subhv dināddinaṃ prauḍhiviśeṣamaśnute 
Subhv vitīrṇaśikṣā iva hṛtpadastha
Subhv sarasvatīvāhanarājahaṃsaiḥ 
Subhv ye kṣīranīrapravibhāgadakṣā
Subhv vivekinaste kavayo jayanti 
Subhv kāvyāmṛtaṃ durjanarāhunītaṃ
Subhv prāpyaṃ bhavenno sumonajanasya 
Subhv saccakramavyājavirājamānat
Subhv aikṣṇyaprakarṣaṃ yadi nāma na syāt 
Subhv vinā na sāhityavidāparatra
Subhv guṇaḥ kathaṃcitprathate kavīnām 
Subhv ālambate tatkṣaṇamambhasīva
Subhv vistāramanyatra na tailabinduḥ 
Subhv atyarthavakratvamanarthakaṃ yā
Subhv śūnyā tu sarvānyaguṇairvyanakti 
Subhv aspṛśyatādūṣitayā tayā kiṃ
Subhv tucchaśvapucchacchaṭayeva vācā 
Subhv nīcastanotvaśru nitāntakārṣṇyaṃ
Subhv puṣṇātu sādharmyabhṛdañjanena 
Subhv vinā tu jāyeta kathaṃ tadīya
Subhv kṣodena sārasvatadṛkprasādaḥ 
Subhv arthosticenna padaśuddhirathāsti sāpi
Subhv no rītirasti yadi sā ghaṭanā kutastyā 
Subhv sāpyasti cenna navavakragatistadetad
Subhv vyarthaṃ vinā rasamaho gahanaṃ kavitvam 
Subhv ślāghyaiva vakrimagatirghanadārḍhyabandhos
Subhv tasyāḥ kavipravarasūktidhanurlatāyāḥ 
Subhv karṇāntikapraṇayabhāji guṇe yadīye
Subhv cetāṃsi matsaravatāṃ jhaṭiti truṭanti 
Subhv yātāste rasasārasaṃgrahavidhiṃ niṣpīḍya niṣpīḍya ye
Subhv vāktatvekṣulatāṃ purā katipaye tattvaspṛśaścakrire 
Subhv jāyantedya yathāyathaṃ tu kavayaste tatra saṃtanvate
Subhv yenuprāsakaṭhoracitrayamakaśleṣādiśalkoccayam 
Subhv paraślokānstokānanudivasamabhyasya nanu ye
Subhv catuṣpādīṃ kuryurbahava iha te santi kavayaḥ 
Subhv avicchinnodgacchajjaladhilaharīrītisuhṛdaḥ
Subhv suhṛdyā vaiśadyaṃ dadhati kila keṣāmcana giraḥ 
Subhv hemno bhāraśatāni vā madamucāṃ vṛndāni vā dantināṃ
Subhv śrīharṣeṇa samarpitāni guṇine bāṇāya kutrādya tat 
Subhv yā bāṇena tu tasya sūktivisarairuṭṭaṅkitāḥ kīrtayas
Subhv tāḥ kalpapralayepi yānti na manāṅmanye parimlānatām 
Subhv dhanyāḥ śūcīni surabhīṇi guṇombhitāni
Subhv vāgvīrudhaḥ svavadanopavanodgatāyāḥ 
Subhv uccitya sūktikusumāni satāṃvivikta
Subhv varṇāni karṇapulineṣvavataṃsayanti 
Subhv tenantavāṅmayamahārṇavadṛṣṭapārāḥ
Subhv sāṃyātrikā iva mahākavayo jayanti 
Subhv yatsūktipelavalavaṅgalavairvaimi
Subhv santaḥ sadaḥ suvadanānyadhivāsayanti 
Subhv trailokyabhūṣaṇamaṇirguṇivargabandhur
Subhv ekaścakāsti kavitā savitā dvitīyaḥ 
Subhv śaṃsanti yasya mahimātiśayaṃ śirobhiḥ
Subhv pādagrahaṃ vidadhataḥ pṛthivībhṛtopi 
Subhv śabdārthamātramapi ye na vidanti tepi
Subhv yāṃ mūrchanāmiva mṛgāḥ śravaṇaiḥ pibantaḥ 
Subhv saṃruddhasarvakaraṇaprasarā bhavanti
Subhv citrasthitā iva kavīndragiraṃ numastām 
Subhv asthāne gamitā layaṃ hatadhiyāṃ vāgdevatā kalpate
Subhv dhikkārāya parābhavāya mahate tāpāya pāpāya vā 
Subhv sthāne tu vyayitā satāṃ prabhavati prakhyātaye bhūtaye
Subhv cetonirvṛtaye paropakṛtaye prānte śivāvāptaye 
Subhv valmīkaprabhaveṇa rāmanṛpatirvyāsena dharmātmajo
Subhv vyākhyātaḥ kila kālidāsakavinā śrīvikramāṅko nṛpaḥ 
Subhv bhojaścittapabihlaṇaprabhṛtibhiḥ karṇopi vidyāpateḥ
Subhv khyātiṃ yānti nireśvarāḥ kavivaraiḥ sphārairna bherīravaiḥ 
Subhv bhujataruvanacchāyāṃ yesāṃ niṣevya mahaujasāṃ
Subhv jaladhiraśanā medinyāsīdasāvakutobhayā 
Subhv smṛtimapi na te yānti kṣmāpā vinā yadanugrahaṃ
Subhv prakṛtimahate kurmastasmai namaḥ kavikarmaṇe 
Subhv yepyāsannibhakumbhaśāyitapadā yepi śriyaṃ lebhire
Subhv yeṣāmapyavasanpurā yuvatayo geheṣvahaścandrikāḥ 
Subhv tāṃllokoyamavaiti lokatilakānsvapnepyajātāniva
Subhv bhrātaḥ satkavikṛtya kiṃ stutiśatairandhaṃ jagattvāṃ vinā 
Subhv sphāreṇa saurabhabhareṇa kimeṇanābhes
Subhv taddhānasāramapi sāramasārameva 
Subhv sraksaumanasyapi na puṣyati saumanasyaṃ
Subhv prasyandate yadi madhudravamuktidevī 
Subhv prayacchati camatkṛtiṃ viracanāvidhau cetasaḥ
Subhv sabhāsu paṭhito bhavatyasamasādhuvādāptaye 
Subhv prathāmupagatastanotyatitarāmudāraṃ yaśo
Subhv na puṣyati manorathaṃ kamiva kāvyacintāmaṇiḥ 
Subhv yaḥ satpadasthamiva kāvyamadhu prasannaṃ
Subhv muṣṇanparasya tanute nijapadmamadhye 
Subhv asthānadoṣajaniteva pipīlakālī
Subhv kālī vibhāti likhitākṣarapaṅktirasya 
Subhv yaḥ syātkevalalakṣyalakṣaṇarato no tarkasaṃparkabhṛn
Subhv nālaṃkāravicāracārudhiṣaṇaḥ kāvyajñaśikṣojjhitaḥ 
Subhv tasmāccedrasaśāli kāvyamudayedekāntataḥ sundaraṃ
Subhv prāsādo dhavalastadā kṣitipateḥ kākasya kārṣṇyādbhavet 
Subhv svaprajñayā kuñcikayeva kaṃcit
Subhv sārasvataṃ vakrimabhaṅgibhājam 
Subhv kavīśvaraḥ kopi padārthakośa
Subhv muddhāṭya viśvābharaṇaṃ karoti 
Subhv daivīrgiraḥ kepi kṛtārthayanti
Subhv tāḥ kuṇṭhayantyeva punarvimūḍhāḥ 
Subhv yā vipruṣaḥ śuktimukheṣu daivyas
Subhv tā eva muktā na tu cātakeṣu 
Subhv pariśramajñaṃ janamantareṇa
Subhv maunavrataṃ bibhrati vāgminopi 
Subhv vācaṃyamāḥ santi vinā vasantaḥ
Subhv puṃskokilāḥ pañcamacañcavopi 
Subhv vyālāśca rāhuśca sudhāprasādāj
Subhv jihvāśironigrahamugramāpuḥ 
Subhv itīva bhītāḥ piśunā bhavanti
Subhv parāṅmukhāḥ kāvyarasāmṛteṣu 
Subhv sākūtaṃ nijasaṃvidekaviṣayaṃ tattvaṃ sacetā bruvan
Subhv nagre nūnamabodhamohitadhiyāṃ hāsyatvamāyāsyati 
Subhv tadyuktaṃ viduṣo janasya jaḍavajjoṣaṃ nu nāmāsituṃ
Subhv jātyandhaṃ pratirūpavarṇanavidhau koyaṃ vṛthaivodyamaḥ 
Subhv jayanti jitamatsarāḥ parahitārthamabhyudyatāḥ
Subhv parābhyudayasusthitāḥ paravipattikhedākulāḥ 
Subhv mahāpuruṣasatkathāśravaṇajātakautūhalāḥ
Subhv samastaduritārṇavaprakaṭasetavaḥ sādhavaḥ 
Subhv paraparivāde mūkaḥ paranārīdarśanepi jātyandhaḥ 
Subhv paṅguḥ paradhanaharaṇe sa jayati loke mahāpuruṣaḥ 
Subhv saṃpatsu mahatāṃ ceto bhavatyutpalakomalam 
Subhv āpatsu ca mahāśailaśilāsaṃghātakarkaśam 
Subhv kusumastabakasyeva dvayī mṛttirmanasvinaḥ 
Subhv mūrdhni vā sarvalokasya śīryate vana eva vā 
Subhv upakāreṇa dūyante na sahantenukampitām 
Subhv āpatsvapi durārādhyā nityaduḥkhā manasvinaḥ 
Subhv jalasekena vardhante taravo nāśmasaṃcayāḥ 
Subhv bhavyo hi dravyatāmeti kriyāṃ prāpya tathāvidhām 
Subhv avṛttibhayamantyānāṃ madhyānāṃ maraṇādbhayam 
Subhv uttamānāṃ tu sattvānāmavamānātparaṃ bhayam 
Subhv tāpaṃ hanti sukhaṃ sūte jīvayatyujjvalaṃ yaśaḥ 
Subhv amṛtasya prakāroyaṃ durlabhaḥ sādhusaṃgamaḥ 
Subhv rasāyanamayī śītā paramānandadāyinī 
Subhv nānandayati kaṃ nāma sādhusaṃgaticandrikā 
Subhv sādhusaṅgatarorjātaṃ vivekakusumaṃ śubham 
Subhv rakṣanti ye mahātmāno bhājanaṃ te phalaśriyaḥ 
Subhv śūnyamākīrṇatāmeti mṛtyurapyutsavāyate 
Subhv āpatsaṃpadivābhāti vidvajjanasamāgame 
Subhv himamāpatsarojinyā mohanīhāramārutaḥ 
Subhv jayatyeko jagatyasminsādhuḥ sādhusamāgamaḥ 
Subhv paraṃ vivardhanaṃ buddherajñānataruśātanam 
Subhv samutsāraṇamādhīnāṃ viddhi sādhusamāgamam 
Subhv yaḥ snātaḥ śītasitayā sādhusaṃgatigaṅgayā 
Subhv kiṃ tasya dānaiḥ kiṃ tīrthaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ kimadhvaraiḥ 
Subhv hṛdayāni satāmeva kaṭhinānīti me matiḥ 
Subhv khalavāgviśikhaistīkṣṇairbhidyante na manāgyataḥ 
Subhv āḥ kimarthamidaṃ cetaḥ satāmambhodhidurbharam 
Subhv iti krudheva durvedhāḥ paraduḥkhairapūrayat 
Subhv kāco maṇirmaṇiḥ kāco yeṣāṃ tenye hi dehinaḥ 
Subhv santi te sudhiyo yeṣāṃ kācaḥ kāco maṇirmaṇiḥ 
Subhv doṣānapi guṇīkartuṃ doṣīkartuṃ guṇānapi 
Subhv śakto vādī na tattathyaṃ doṣā guṇā guṇāḥ 
Subhv guṇarāśimahābhāranirbharāpūritāntarāḥ 
Subhv santo gauravamāyānti yadi tatra kimadbhutam 
Subhv svātmanyeva layaṃ yātu tādṛśo guṇināṃ guṇaḥ 
Subhv svayaṃ prakhyāpyamānopi yastṛṇāya na manyate 
Subhv guṇavajjanasaṃparkādyāti svalpopi gauravam 
Subhv puṣpamālānuṣaṅgeṇa tṛṇaṃ śirasi dhāryate 
Subhv suvṛttasyaikarūpasya paraprītyai dhṛtonnateḥ 
Subhv sādhoḥ stanayugasyeva patanaṃ kasya tuṣṭaye 
Subhv udeti savitā rakto rakta evāstameti ca 
Subhv saṃpatau ca vipatau ca mahatāmekarūpatā 
Subhv pātena kanduka ivotpatatyāryaḥ patannapi 
Subhv tathā tvanāryaḥ patati mṛtpiṇḍapatanaṃ yathā 
Subhv pātitopi karāghātairutpatatyeva kandukaḥ 
Subhv prāyeṇa hi suvṛttānāmasthāyinyo vipattayaḥ 
Subhv ghyutopyudgacchati punaḥ prajñāvānna tu mūḍhadhīḥ 
Subhv kandukaḥ patanotthāyī na tu kāntākucadvayī 
Subhv apekṣante na ca snehaṃ na pātraṃ na daśāntaram 
Subhv sadā lokahite yuktā ratnadīpā ivottamāḥ 
Subhv nirguṇeṣvapi sattveṣu dayāṃ kurvanti sādhavaḥ 
Subhv nahi saṃharate jyotsnāṃ candraścaṇḍālaveśmani 
Subhv nālokaḥ kriyate sūrye bhūḥ pratīpaṃ na dhāryate 
Subhv nahi pratyupakārāṇāmapekṣā satsu vidyate 
Subhv apakurvannapi prāyaḥ prāpnoti mahataḥ śubham 
Subhv dahantamapyaurvamagniṃ saṃtarapayati vāridhiḥ  Qsv kasyāpi
Subhv satpakṣā ṛjavaḥ śuddhāḥ saphalā guṇasevinaḥ dṛṣṭvāpi dṛśyate dṛśyaṃ śrutvāpi śrūyate punaḥ 
Subhv satyaṃ na sādhuvṛttasya dṛśyate punaruktatā 
Subhv satpakṣā ṛjavaḥ śuddhāḥ saphalā guṇasevinaḥ 
Subhv tulyairapi guṇaiścitraṃ santaḥ santaḥ śarāḥ śarāḥ 
Subhv lābhapraṇayino nīcā mānakāmā manasvinaḥ 
Subhv madguḥ sarasi matsyārthī haṃsasyeṣṭā prasannatā 
Subhv paraduḥkhaṃ samākarṇya svabhāvasaralo janaḥ 
Subhv upakārāsamarthatvātprāpnoti hṛdaye vyathām 
Subhv te vandyāste kṛtinaḥ ślāghyā teṣāṃ hi janmanotpattiḥ 
Subhv yairujjhitātmakāryaiḥ suhṛdāmarthā hi sādhyante 
Subhv aśaṭhamalolamajihmaṃ tyāginamanurāgiṇaṃ viśeṣajñam 
Subhv yadi nāśrayati naraṃ śrīḥ śrīreva hi vañcitā tatra 
Subhv ārogyaṃ vidvattā sajjanamaittrī mahākule janma 
Subhv svādhīnatā ca puṃsāṃ mahadaiśvaryaṃ vināpyarthaiḥ 
Subhv svalpāpi sādhusaṃpadbhogyā mahatāṃ na pṛthvyapi khalaśrīḥ 
Subhv sārasameva payastṛṣamapaharati na vāridherjātu 
Subhv na bhavati bhavati ca na ciraṃ bhavati ciraṃ celphalo visaṃvadati 
Subhv manyuḥ satpuruṣāṇāṃ tulyaḥ snehena nīcānām 
Subhv doṣo guṇāya guṇināṃ mahadapi doṣāya doṣiṇāṃ sukṛtam 
Subhv tṛṇamiva dugdhāya gavāṃ dugdhamiva viṣāya sarpāṇām 
Subhv viṣamagatā api na budhāḥ paribhavamiśrāṃ śriyaṃ hi vāñchanti 
Subhv na pibanti bhaumamambhaḥ sarajasamiti cātakā ete 
Subhv yogyatayaiva vināśaṃ prāyonāryeṣu yānti guṇavantaḥ 
Subhv sphuṭavacanā eva śukāḥ pañjarabandhaṃ niṣevante 
Subhv sakṛdapi dṛṣṭvā puruṣaṃ prājñāstulayanti sāraphalgutvam 
Subhv hastatulayāpi nipuṇāḥ palaparimāṇaṃ vijānanti 
Subhv sujano na yāti vairaṃ parahitanirato vināśakālepi 
Subhv chedepi candanataruḥ surabhayati mukhaṃ kuṭhārasya 
Subhv nirguṇamapyanuraktaṃ prāyo na samāśritaṃ jahati santaḥ 
Subhv sahavṛddhikṣayabhājaṃ vahati śaśāṅkaḥ kalaṅkamapi 
Subhv antyāvasthopi budhaḥ svaguṇaṃ na jahāti jātiśuddhatayā 
Subhv na śvetabhāvamujjhati śaṅkhaḥ śikhibhuktamuktopi 
Subhv doṣamapi guṇavati jane dṛṣṭvā guṇarāgiṇo na khidyante 
Subhv prītyaiva śaśini patitaṃ paśyati lokaḥ kalaṅkamapi 
Subhv sāptapadīnaṃ sakhyaṃ bhavetprakṛtyā viśuddhacittānām 
Subhv kimutānyonyaguṇakathāvisrambhanibaddhabhāvānām 
Subhv spṛhaṇīyāḥ kasya na te sumateḥ saralāśayā mahātmānaḥ 
Subhv trayamapi yeṣāṃ sadṛśaṃ hṛdayaṃ vacanaṃ tathācāraḥ 
Subhv guṇinaḥ samīpavartī pūjyo lokasya guṇavihīnopi 
Subhv vimalekṣaṇaprasaṅkādañjanamāpnoti kāṇākṣi 
Subhv sahasiddhamidaṃ mahatāṃ dhaneṣvanāsthā guṇeṣu kṛpaṇatvam 
Subhv paraduḥkhe kātaratā mahacca dhairyaṃ svaduḥkheṣu 
Subhv atikupitā api sujanā yogena mṛdūbhavanti na tu nīcāḥ 
Subhv hemnaḥ kaṭhinasyāpi dravaṇopāyosti na tṛṇānām 
Subhv upakṛtisāhasikatayā kṣatimapi gaṇayanti no guṇinaḥ 
Subhv janayanti hi prakāśaṃ dīpaśikhāḥ svāṅgadāhena 
Subhv raktatvaṃ kamalānāṃ satpuruṣāṇāṃ paropakāritvam 
Subhv asatāṃ ca nirdayatvaṃ svabhāvasiddhaṃ triṣu tritayam 
Subhv upakartumaprakāśaṃ kṣantuṃ nyūneṣvayācitaṃ dātum 
Subhv abhisaṃdhātuṃ ca guṇaiḥ śateṣu kecidvijānanti 
Subhv guṇini guṇajño ramate nāguṇaśīlasya guṇini paritoṣaḥ 
Subhv alireti vanātkamalaṃ na dardurastānnivāsopi 
Subhv ādau tu mandamandāni madhye samarasāni ca 
Subhv ante snehāyamānāni saṃgatāni budhaiḥ saha 
Subhv iyamunnatasattvaśālināṃ
Subhv mahatāṃ kāpi kaṭhoracittatā 
Subhv upakṛtya bhavanti dūrataḥ
Subhv parataḥ pratyupakāraśaṅkayā 
Subhv upakāriṇi vītamatsare vā
Subhv sadayatvaṃ yadi tatra kotirekaḥ 
Subhv ahite sahasāparāddhalabdhe
Subhv saghṛṇaṃ yasya manaḥ satāṃ sa dhuryaḥ 
Subhv ādimadhyanidhaneṣu sauhṛdaṃ
Subhv sajjane bhavati netare jane 
Subhv chedatāḍananigharṣatāpanair
Subhv nānyabhāvamupayāti kāñcanam 
Subhv dīpāḥ sthitaṃ vastu vibhāvayanti
Subhv kulapradīpāstu bhavanti kecit 
Subhv ciravyatītānapi pūrvajānye
Subhv prakāśayanti svaguṇaprakarṣāt 
Subhv tuṅgātmanāḥ tuṅgatarāḥ samarthā
Subhv manorujaṃ dhvaṃsayituṃ na nīcāḥ 
Subhv dhārādharā eva dharādharāṇāṃ
Subhv nidāghadāvaughaharā na nadyaḥ 
Subhv guṇā guṇajñeṣu guṇībhavanti
Subhv te nirguṇaṃ prāpya bhavanti doṣāḥ 
Subhv susvādutoyaprabhavā hi nadyaḥ
Subhv samudramāsādya bhavantyapeyāḥ 
Subhv tṛṇāni nonmūlayati prabhañjano
Subhv mṛdūni nīcaiḥ praṇatāni sarvaśaḥ 
Subhv samucchritāneva tarūnprabādhate
Subhv mahānmahatsveva karoti vikriyām 
Subhv cirāya satsaṃgamaśuddhamānaso
Subhv na yātyasatsaṃgatamātmavānnaraḥ 
Subhv manoharendīvarakhaṇḍagocaro
Subhv na jātu bhṛṅgaḥ kuṇape nilīyate 
Subhv api vibhavavihīnaḥ pracyuto vā svadeśān
Subhv nahi khalajanasevāṃ prārthayatyunnatātmā 
Subhv tanu tṛṇamupabhuṅkte na kṣudhārtopi siṃhaḥ
Subhv pibati rudhiramuṣṇaṃ prāyaśaḥ kuñjarāṇām 
Subhv vitte tyāgaḥ kṣamā śaktau duḥkhe dainyavihīnatā 
Subhv nirdambhatā sadācāre svabhāvoyaṃ mahātmanām 
Subhv sukhalavadaśāharṣaklaivye khalaḥ khalu khelate
Subhv skhalati bhajate leśakleśe viṣādaviṣūcikām 
Subhv bhavati na satāṃ darpoddāmā na dainyamayī matir
Subhv durabhibhavatā gambhīrāṇāṃ sukheṣvasukheṣu ca 
Subhv svāmye peśalatā guṇe praṇayitā harṣe nirutsekatā
Subhv mantre saṃvṛtatā śrute sumatitā vittodaye tyāgitā 
Subhv sādhau sādaratā khale vimukhatā pāpe paraṃ bhīrutā
Subhv duḥkhe kleśasahiṣṇutā ca mahatāṃ kalyāṇamākāṅkṣati 
Subhv vipadi dhairyamathābhyudaye kṣamā
Subhv sadasi vākpaṭutā yudhi vikramaḥ 
Subhv yaśasi cābhiratirvyasanaṃ śrute
Subhv prakṛtisiddhamidaṃ hi mahātmanām 
Subhv idaṃ hi māhātmyaviśeṣasūcakaṃ
Subhv vadanti cihnaṃ mahatāṃ manīṣiṇaḥ 
Subhv mano yadeṣāṃ sukhaduḥkhasaṃbhave
Subhv prayāti no harṣaviṣādavaśyatām 
Subhv subhāṣitaiḥ prītiranunnatiḥ śriyā
Subhv parārthaniṣpattipaṭīyasī kriyā 
Subhv guṇeṣvatṛptirguṇavatsu cādaro
Subhv nigūḍhametaccaritaṃ mahātmanām 
Subhv satyaṃ guṇā guṇavatāṃ vidhivaiparītyād
Subhv yatnārjitā api kalau viphalā bhavanti 
Subhv sāphalyamasti sutarāmidameva teṣāṃ
Subhv yattāpayanti hṛdayāni punaḥ khalānām 
Subhv yadvañcanāhitamatirbahu cāṭugarbhaṃ
Subhv kāryonmukhaḥ khalajanaḥ kṛtakaṃ bravīti 
Subhv tatsādhavo na na vidanti vidanti kiṃ tu
Subhv kartuṃ vṛthā praṇayamasya na pārayanti 
Subhv pāpaṃ samācarati vītaghṛṇo jaghanyaḥ
Subhv prāpyāpadaṃ saghṛṇa eva tu madhyabuddhiḥ 
Subhv prāṇātyayepi na tu sādhujanaḥ suvṛttaṃ
Subhv velāṃ samudra iva laṅghayituṃ samarthaḥ 
Subhv śuddhiḥ sa eva kulajaśca sa eva dhīraḥ
Subhv ślāghyo vipatsvapi na muñcati yaḥ svabhāvam 
Subhv taptaṃ yathā dinakarasya marīcijālair
Subhv dehaṃ tyajedapi himaṃ na tu śītalatvam 
Subhv yāñcāpadaṃ maraṇaduḥkhamivānubhāvya
Subhv dattena kiṃ khalu bhavatyatibhūyasāpi 
Subhv kalpadrumānparihasanta iveha santaḥ
Subhv saṃkalpitairatidadatyakadarthitaṃ yat 
Subhv te sādhavo bhuvanamaṇḍalamaulibhūtā
Subhv ye sādhutāṃ nirupakāriṣu darśayanti 
Subhv ātmaprayojanavaśīkṛtakhinnadehaḥ
Subhv pūrvopakāriṣu khalopi hi sānukampaḥ 
Subhv nāntarvicintayati kiṃcidapi pratīpam
Subhv akopitopi sujanaḥ piśunena pāpam 
Subhv arkadviṣopi hi mukhe patitāgrabhāgās
Subhv tārāpateramṛtameva karāḥ kiranti 
Subhv ākopitopi kulajo na vadatyavācyaṃ
Subhv niṣpīḍito madhurameva vametkilekṣuḥ 
Subhv nīco jano guṇaśatairapi sevyamāno
Subhv hāseṣu tadvadati yatkalaheṣu vācyam 
Subhv nidantu nītinipuṇā athavā stuvantu
Subhv lakṣmīḥ parāpatatu gacchatu vā yatheccham 
Subhv adyaiva vā maraṇamastu yugāntare vā
Subhv nyāyyātpathaḥ pracalayanti padaṃ na dhīrāḥ 
Subhv hetoḥ kutopyasadṛśāḥ sujanā garīyaḥ
Subhv kāryaṃ nisargaguravaḥ sphuṭamārabhante 
Subhv utthāya kiṃ kalaśatopi na sindhunātham
Subhv udvīcimālamapibadbhagavānagastyaḥ 
Subhv priyā nyāyyā vṛttirmalinamasubhaṅgepyasukaraṃ
Subhv hyasanto nābhyarthyāḥ suhṛdapi na yācyokṛśadhanaḥ 
Subhv vipadyuccaiḥ stheyaṃ padamanuvidheyaṃ ca mahatāṃ
Subhv satāṃ kenoddiṣṭaṃ viṣamamasidhārāvratamidam 
Subhv pradānaṃ succhannaṃ gṛhamupagate saṃbhramavidhir
Subhv anutseko lakṣmyāpyanabhibhavanīyāḥ parakathāḥ 
Subhv priyaṃ kṛtvā maunaṃ sadasi kathanaṃ cāpyupakṛteḥ
Subhv śrutetyantāsaktiḥ puruṣamabhijātaṃ kathayati 
Subhv kasyādeśātkṣapayati tamaḥ saptasaptiḥ prajānāṃ
Subhv chāyāhetoḥ pathi viṭapināmañjaliḥ kena baddhaḥ 
Subhv abhyarthyante jalalavamucaḥ kena vā vṛṣṭihetor
Subhv jātyaivaite parahitavidhau sādhavo baddhakakṣyā 
Subhv svaphalanicayaḥ śākhābhaṅgaṃ karoti vanaspater
Subhv gamanamalasaṃ barhāṭopi karoti śikhaṇḍinaḥ 
Subhv caturagamano yo jātyāśvaḥ sa gauriva vāhyate
Subhv guṇavati jane prāyeṇaite guṇāḥ khalu vairiṇaḥ 
Subhv khyātiṃ yatra guṇā na yānti guṇinastatrādaraḥ syātkutaḥ
Subhv kiṃ kuryādbahuśikṣitopi puruṣaḥ pāṣāṇabhūte jane 
Subhv premārūḍhavilāsinīmadavaśavyāvṛttakaṇṭhasvanaḥ
Subhv sītkāro hi manoharopi badhire kiṃ nāma kuryādguṇam 
Subhv kṣudrāḥ santi sahasraśaḥ svabharaṇavyāpāramātronmukhāḥ
Subhv svārtho yasya parārtha eva sa pumānekaḥ satāmagraṇīḥ 
Subhv duṣpūrodarapūraṇāya pibati srotaḥpatiṃ vāḍavo
Subhv jīmūtastu nidāghatāpitajagatsaṃtāpavicchittaye 
Subhv namratvenonnamantaḥ paraguṇanutibhiḥ svānguṇānkhyāpayantaḥ
Subhv puṣṇantaḥ svīyamarthaṃ satatakṛtamahārambhayatnāḥ parārthe 
Subhv kṣāntyaivākṣeparūkṣākṣaramukharamukhādurmukhānduḥkhayantaḥ
Subhv santaḥ sāścaryacaryā jagati bahumatāḥ kasya nābhyarthanīyāḥ 
Subhv sajjanā eva sādhūnāṃ prathayanti guṇotkaram 
Subhv puṣpāṇāṃ saurabhaṃ prāyastanvate dikṣu mārutāḥ 
Subhv sādhureva pravīṇaḥ syātsadguṇāmṛtacarvaṇe 
Subhv navacūtāṅkurāsvādakuśalaḥ kokilaḥ kila 
Subhv prāyaḥ santyupadeśārhā dhīmanto na jaḍāśayāḥ 
Subhv tilāḥ kusumasaugandhyagrāhiṇo na yavāḥ kvacit 
Subhv manasvihṛdayaṃ dhatte raukṣyeṇaiva prasannatām 
Subhv bhasmanā makuraḥ prāyaḥ prasādaṃ labhatetarām 
Subhv uttamaḥ kleśavikṣobhaṃ kṣamaḥ soḍhuṃ nahītaraḥ 
Subhv maṇireva mahāśāṇagharṣaṇaṃ na tu mṛtkaṇaḥ 
Subhv jaḍe prabhavati prāyo duḥkhaṃ bibhrati sādhavaḥ 
Subhv sitāṃśāvudite padmāḥ saṃkocātaṅkadhāriṇaḥ 
Subhv guṇānāmantaraṃ prāyastajjño jānāti netaraḥ 
Subhv mālatīmallikāmodaṃ ghrāṇaṃ vetti na locanam 
Subhv svabhāvaṃ naiva muñcanti santaḥ saṃsargatosatām 
Subhv na tyajanti rutaṃ mañju kākasaṃparkataḥ pikāḥ 
Subhv saṃpattau komalaṃ cittaṃ sādhorāpadi karkaśam 
Subhv sukumāraṃ madhau pattraṃ taroḥ syātkaṭhinaṃ śucau 
Subhv svabhāvaṃ na jahātyantaḥ sādhurāpadgatopi san 
Subhv karpūraḥ pāvakapluṣṭaḥ saurabhaṃ bhajatetarām 
Subhv apyāpatsamayaḥ sādhoḥ prayāti ślāghanīyatām 
Subhv vidhorvidhuṃtudāskandavipatkālopi sundaraḥ 
Subhv dṛṣṭadurjanadaurātmyaḥ sajjane rajyate janaḥ 
Subhv āruhya parvataṃ pānthaḥ nirvṛtimetyalam 
Subhv kṣaṇakṣayiṇi sāpāye bhoge rajyanti nottamāḥ 
Subhv saṃtyajyāmbhojakiṃjalkaṃ haṃsāḥ prāśnanti śaivalam 
Subhv adhamaṃ bādhate bhūyo duḥkhāvego na tūttamam 
Subhv pāṇipādaṃ rujatyāśu śītasparśo na cakṣuṣī 
Subhv guṇavānsucirasthāyī daivenāpi na sahyate 
Subhv tiṣṭhatyekāṃ niśāṃ candraḥ śrīmānsaṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ 
Subhv sarvatra guṇavāndeśe cakāsti prathatetarām 
Subhv maṇirmūrdhni gale bāhau pādapīṭhepi śobhate 
Subhv uttamaṃ suciraṃ naiva vipadobhibhavantyalam 
Subhv rāhugrasanasaṃbhūtā kṣaṇaṃ vicchāyatā vidhoḥ 
Subhv saṃtuṣyatyuttamaḥ stutyā dhanena mahatādhamaḥ 
Subhv prasīdanti japairdevā balibhirbhūtavigrahāḥ 
Subhv na kadācitsatāṃ cetaḥ prasaratyaghakarmasu 
Subhv jaleṣu drutamapyantaḥ sarpirāśyānatāṃ vrajet 
Subhv narāḥ saṃskārārhā jagati kila kecitsukṛtinaḥ
Subhv samānāyāṃ jātāvapi vayasi satyāmapi dhiyi 
Subhv ayaṃ dṛṣṭāntotra sphuṭaparicayādabhyasanataḥ
Subhv śukaḥ ślokānvaktuṃ prabhavati na kākaḥ kvacidapi 
Subhv dhanamapi paradattaṃ duḥkamaucityabhājāṃ
Subhv bhavati hṛdi tadevānandakārītareṣām 
Subhv malayajarasabindurbādhate netramantar
Subhv janayati ca sa evāhlādamanyatra gātre 
Subhv sadvaṃśajasya paritāpanudaḥ suvṛtta
Subhv śuddhātmanaḥ sakalalokavibhūṣaṇasya 
Subhv chidraṃ prajātamapi sādhujanasya daivān
Subhv muktāmaṇeriva guṇāya bhavatyavaśyam 
Subhv gehaṃ durgatabandhurbhirgurugṛhaṃ chātrairahaṃkāribhir
Subhv haṭṭaṃ pattanavañcakairmunijanaiḥ śāponmukhairāśramān 
Subhv siṃhādyaiśca vanaṃ khalairnṛpasabhāṃ cauraurdigantānapi
Subhv saṃkīrṇānyavalokya satyasaralaḥ sādhuḥ kva viśrāmyati 
Subhv sābhimānamasaṃbhāvyamaucityacyutamapriyam 
Subhv duḥkhāvamānadīnaṃ vā na vadanti guṇonnatāḥ 
Subhv bhavati subhagatvamadhikaṃ vistāritaparaguṇasya sujanasya 
Subhv vahati vikāsitakumudo dviguṇaruciṃ himakaroddyotaḥ 
Subhv guṇināmapi nijarūpapratipattiḥ parata eva saṃbhavati 
Subhv svamahimadarśanamakṣṇormakuratale jāyate yasmāt 
Subhv kotibhāraḥ samarthānāṃ kiṃ dūraṃ vyavasāyinām 
Subhv ko videśaḥ savidyānāṃ kaḥ paraḥ priyavādinām 
Subhv aśvaḥ śastraṃ śāstraṃ vīṇā vāṇī naraśca nārī ca 
Subhv puruṣaviśeṣaṃ prāptā bhavanti yogyā ayogyāśca 
Subhv utsāhasaṃpannamadīrghasūtraṃ
Subhv kriyāvidhijñaṃ vyasaneṣvasaktam 
Subhv śūraṃ kṛtajñaṃ dṛḍhasauhṛdaṃ ca
Subhv lakṣmīḥ svayaṃ vāñchati vāsahetoḥ 
Subhv kadarthitasyāpi mahāśayasya
Subhv na śakyate sargaguṇaḥ pramārṣṭum 
Subhv adhomukhasyāpi kṛtasya vahner
Subhv nādhaḥ śikhā yānti kadācideva 
Subhv nyāyaḥ khalaiḥ parihṛtaścalitaśca dharmaḥ
Subhv kālaḥ kaliḥ kaluṣa eva paraṃ pravṛttaḥ 
Subhv prāyeṇa durjanajanaḥ prabhāviṣṇureva
Subhv niścakrikaḥ paribhavāspadameva sādhuḥ 
Subhv vrate vivādaṃ vimatiṃ viveke
Subhv satyetiśaṅkāṃ vinaye vikāram 
Subhv guṇevamānaṃ kuśale niṣedhaṃ
Subhv dharme virodhaṃ na karoti sādhuḥ 
Subhv vandyaḥ sa puṃsaṃ tridaśābhinandyaḥ
Subhv kāruṇyapuṇyopacayakriyābhiḥ 
Subhv saṃsārasāratvamupaitai yasya
Subhv paropakārābharaṇaṃ śarīram 
Subhv abhedenopāste kumudamudare vā sthitavato
Subhv vipakṣādambhojādupagatavato vā madhulihaḥ 
Subhv aparyāptaḥ kopi svaparaparicaryāparicaya
Subhv prabandhaḥ sādhūnāmayamanabhisaṃdhānamadhuraḥ 
Subhv yairvātūlo bhavati purataḥ kathyamānairjanānāṃ
Subhv kāmapyantarvidadhati rujaṃ yepyanudgīryamāṇāḥ 
Subhv tebhiprāyāḥ kimapi hṛdaye kaṇṭhalagnaḥ sphuranto
Subhv yasyākhyeyāstamiha suhṛdaṃ puṇyavanto labhante 
Subhv udanvacchinnā bhūḥ sa ca nidhirapāṃ yojanaśataṃ
Subhv sadā pānthaḥ pūṣā gaganaparimāṇaṃ kathayati 
Subhv iti prāyo bhāvāḥ sphuradavadhimudrāmukulitāḥ
Subhv satāṃ prajñonmeṣaḥ punarayamasīmā vijayate 
Subhv sāgasepi na kupyanti kṛpayā copakurvate 
Subhv bodhaṃ svasyaiva necchanti te viśvoddharaṇakṣamāḥ 
Subhv pātraṃ pavitrayati naiva guṇānkṣiṇoti
Subhv snehaṃ na saṃharati nāpi malaṃ prasūte 
Subhv doṣāvasānaruciraścalatāṃ na dhatte
Subhv satsaṃgamaḥ sukṛtasadmani kopi dīpaḥ 
Subhv aṇurapi maṇiḥ prāṇatrāṇakṣamo viṣabhakṣiṇāṃ
Subhv śiśurapi ruṣā siṃhīsūnaḥ samāhvayate gajān 
Subhv tanurapi taruskandhodbhūto dahatyanalo vanaṃ
Subhv prakṛtimahatāṃ jātyaṃ tejo na mūrtimapekṣate 
Subhv namaḥ khalebhyaḥ ka ivāthavā na tā
Subhv nalaṃ namasyediha yo jijīviṣuḥ 
Subhv vinaiva ye doṣamṛṣiprakāṇḍavan
Subhv nayanti śāpena rasātalaṃ narān 
Subhv viṣadharatopyativiṣamaḥ khala iti na mṛṣā vadanti vidvāṃsaḥ 
Subhv yadayaṃ nakuladveṣī sakuladveṣī sadā piśunaḥ 
Subhv atimaline kartavye bhavati khalānāmatīva nipuṇā dhīḥ 
Subhv timire hi kauśikānāṃ rūpaṃ pratipadyate dṛṣṭiḥ 
Subhv vidhvastaparaguṇānāṃ bhavati khalānāmatīva malinatvam 
Subhv antaritaśaśirucāmapi salilamucāṃ malinimābhyadhikaḥ 
Subhv hasta iva bhūtimalino laṅghayati yathā yathā khalaḥ sūjanam 
Subhv darpaṇamiva taṃ kurute tathā tathā nirmalacchāyam 
Subhv jīvanagrahaṇe namrā gṛhītvā punarutthitāḥ 
Subhv kiṃ kaniṣṭhā uta jyeṣṭhā ghaṭīyantrasya durjanāḥ 
Subhv sadā khaṇḍanayogyāya tuṣapūrṇāśayāya ca 
Subhv namostu bahubījāya khalāyolūkhalāya ca 
Subhv jihvādūṣitasatpātraḥ piṇḍārthī kalahotkaṭaḥ 
Subhv tulyatāmaśucirnityaṃ bibharti piśunaḥ śunaḥ 
Subhv aho bata khalaḥ puṇyairmūrkhopyaśrutapaṇḍitaḥ 
Subhv svaguṇodīraṇe śeṣaḥ paranindāsu vākpatiḥ 
Subhv khalaḥ sujanapaiśunye sarvatokṣi śiromukhaḥ 
Subhv sarvataḥ śrutimāṃlloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati 
Subhv satsādhuvāde mūrkhasya mātsaryagalarogiṇaḥ 
Subhv jihvā kaṅkamukhenāpi kṛṣṭā naiva pravartate 
Subhv māyāmayaḥ prakṛtyaiva rāgadveṣamadākulaḥ 
Subhv mahatāmapi mohāya saṃsāra iva durjanaḥ 
Subhv khacitramapi māyāvī racayatyeva līlayā 
Subhv laghuśca mahatāṃ madhye tasmātkhala iti smṛtaḥ 
Subhv khalena dhanamattena nīcena prabhaviṣṇunā 
Subhv piśunena padasthena hā praje kva gamiṣyasi 
Subhv kṛtaśatamasatsu naṣṭaṃ subhāṣitaśataṃ ca naṣṭamabudheṣu 
Subhv vacanaśatamavacanakare buddhiśatamacetane naṣṭam 
Subhv naṣṭamapātre dānaṃ naṣṭaṃ hitamaphalabuddhyavajñāne 
Subhv naṣṭo guṇoguṇajñe naṣṭaṃ dākṣiṇyamakṛtajñe 
Subhv dūrāducchritapāṇirārdranayanaḥ protsāritārdhāsano
Subhv gāḍhāliṅganatatparaḥ priyakathāpraśneṣu saktottaraḥ 
Subhv antargūḍhaviṣo bahirmadhumayaścātīva māyāmayaḥ
Subhv ko nāmāyamapūrvanāṭakavidhiryaḥ śikṣito durjanaiḥ 
Subhv ye śramaṃ hartumīhante mahatāṃ cirasaṃbhṛtam 
Subhv vandyāstesaralātmāno durjanāḥ sajjanā iva 
Subhv aho kuṭilabuddhīnāṃ durgrāhamasatāṃ manaḥ 
Subhv anyadvacasi kaṇṭhenyadanyadoṣṭhapuṭe sthitam 
Subhv khaleṣu satsu niryātā vayamarjayituṃ guṇān 
Subhv iyaṃ sā taskaragrāme ratnakrayaviḍambanā 
Subhv vardhete spardhayevobhau saṃpadā śataśākhayā 
Subhv aṅkurovaskarodbhūtaḥ puruṣaścākulodbhavaḥ 
Subhv dahyamānāḥ sutīkṣṇena nīcāḥ parayaśogninā 
Subhv aśaktāstatpadaṃ gantuṃ tato nindāṃ pracakrire 
Subhv yatsmṛtvaiva parāṃ yānti santaḥ saṃtāpasaṃtatim 
Subhv tadasanto hasantopi helayaiva hi kurvate 
Subhv guṇadoṣāvaśāstrajñaḥ kathaṃ vibhajate janaḥ 
Subhv kimandhasyādhikārosti rūpabhedopalabdhiṣu 
Subhv prāyaḥ prakāśatāṃ yāti malinaḥ sādhubādhayā 
Subhv nāgrasiṣyata cedarkaṃ kojñāsyatsiṃhikāsutam 
Subhv prāyaḥ paropatāpāya durjanaḥ satatodyataḥ 
Subhv avaśyakaraṇīyatvānna kāraṇamapekṣate 
Subhv stokenonnatimāyāti stokenāyātyadhogatim 
Subhv aho susadṛśī vṛttistulākoṭeḥ khalasya ca 
Subhv aho prakṛtisādṛśyaṃ śleṣmaṇo durjanasya ca 
Subhv madhuraiḥ kopamāyāti kaṭukairupaśāmyati 
Subhv yathā gajapatiḥ śrāntaśchāyārthī vṛkṣamāśritaḥ 
Subhv viśramya taṃ drumaṃ hanti tathā nīcaḥ svamāśrayam 
Subhv durjanaḥ parihartavyo vidyayālaṃkṛtopi san 
Subhv maṇinā bhūṣitaḥ sarpo bhavetkiṃ na bhayaṃkaraḥ 
Subhv cārutā paradārārthaṃ dhanaṃ lokopataptaye 
Subhv prabhūtvaṃ sādhunāśāya khale khalatarā guṇāḥ 
Subhv paropaghātavijñānamātralābhopajīvinām 
Subhv dāśānāmiva dhūrtānāṃ jālāya guṇasaṃgrahaḥ 
Subhv durjanenocyamānāni vacāṃsi madhurāṇyapi 
Subhv akālakusumānīva trāsaṃ saṃjanayanti me 
Subhv na lajjate sajjanavarjanīyayā
Subhv bhujaṃgavakrakriyayāpi durjanaḥ 
Subhv dhiyaṃ kumāyāsamayābhicāriṇīṃ
Subhv vidagdhatāmeva hi manyate khalaḥ 
Subhv vṛtiṃ svāṃ bahu manyate hṛdi śucaṃ dhattenukampoktibhir
Subhv vyaktaṃ nindati yogyatāṃ mitamatiḥ kurvanstutīrātmanaḥ 
Subhv garhyopāyaniṣevaṇaṃ kathayati sthāsnuṃ vadanvyāpadaṃ
Subhv śrutvā duḥkhamaruṃtudāṃ vitanute pīḍāṃ janaḥ prākṛtaḥ 
Subhv pākaścenna śubhasya medya tadasau prāgeva nādātkimu
Subhv svārthaścenna mayāsya kiṃ na bhajate dīnānsvabandhūnayam 
Subhv matto randhrudṛśosya bhīryadi na tallubdhaḥ kimeṣa tyajed
Subhv ityantaḥ puruṣodhaṃaḥ kalayati prāyaḥ kṛtopakriyaḥ 
Subhv sāścaryaṃ yudhi śauryamapratihataṃ tatkaṇḍitākhaṇḍalaṃ
Subhv pāñcottānakaraḥ kṛta sabhagavāndānena lakṣmīpatiḥ 
Subhv aiśvaryaṃ svakarāptasaptabhuvanaṃ labdhābdhipāraṃ yaśaḥ
Subhv sarvaṃ durjanasaṃgamena sahasā spaṣṭaṃ vinaṣṭaṃ baleḥ 
Subhv śamayati yaśaḥ kleśaṃ sūte diśatyaśivāṃ gatiṃ
Subhv janayati janodvegāyāsaṃ nayatyupahāsyatām 
Subhv bhramayati matiṃ mānaṃ hanti kṣiṇoti ca jīvitaṃ
Subhv kṣipati sakalaṃ kalyāṇānāṃ kulaṃ khalasaṃgamaḥ 
Subhv avinayabhuvāmajñānānāṃ śamāya bhavannapi
Subhv prakṛtikuṭilādvidyābhyāsaḥ khalatvavivṛddhaye 
Subhv phaṇibhayabhṛtāmastu cchedakṣamastamasāmasau
Subhv viṣadharaphaṇāratnāloko bhayaṃ tu bhṛśāyate 
Subhv karoti pūjyamānopi lokavyasanadīkṣitaḥ 
Subhv darśane darśane trāsaṃ gṛhāhiriva durjanaḥ 
Subhv satyadharmacyutātpuṃsaḥ kruddhādāśīviṣādiva 
Subhv nāstikopi hyudvijate janaḥ kiṃ punarāstikaḥ 
Subhv yeṣāṃ prāṇivadhaḥ krīḍā narma marmacchido giraḥ 
Subhv kāryaṃ paropatāpitvaṃ te mṛtyorapi mṛtyavaḥ 
Subhv aho bata mahatkaṣṭaṃ viparītamidaṃ jagat 
Subhv yenāpatrpate sādhurasādhustena tuṣyati 
Subhv na tathecchantyakalyāṇāḥ pareṣāṃ vedituṃ guṇān 
Subhv yathaiṣāṃ jñātumicchanti nairguṇyaṃ pāpacetasaḥ 
Subhv varjanīyo matimatāṃ durjanaḥ sakhyavairayoḥ 
Subhv śvā bhavatyupaghāyāya laḍannapi daśannapi 
Subhv ato hāsyataraṃ loke kiṃcidanyanna vidyate 
Subhv yatra durjana ityāha durjanaḥ sajjanaṃ janam 
Subhv apakāramasaṃprāpya tuṣyetsādhurasādhutaḥ 
Subhv naiṣa lābho bhujaṃgena veṣṭito yanna daśyate 
Subhv labdhaḥ stabdhonṛjurmūrkhaḥ prabhurekāntadāruṇaḥ 
Subhv bahūneṣa khalaḥ sādhūnmārayitvā mariṣyati 
Subhv kā khalena saha spardhā sajjanasyābhimāninaḥ 
Subhv bhāṣaṇaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ sādhudūṣaṇaṃ yasya bhūṣaṇam 
Subhv mukhenaikena vidhyanti pādamekasya kaṇṭakāḥ 
Subhv dūrānmukhasahasreṇa sarvaprāṇaharāḥ khalāḥ 
Subhv nirmāya khalajihvāgraṃ sarvaprāṇaharaṃ nṛṇām 
Subhv cakāra kiṃ vṛthā śastraviṣavahnīnprajāpatiḥ 
Subhv yathā paropakāreṣu nityaṃ jāgarti sajjanaḥ 
Subhv tathā parāpakāreṣu jāgarti satataṃ khalaḥ 
Subhv bibheti piśunānnīcaḥ prakāśanapaṭīyasaḥ 
Subhv na punarmūḍhahṛdayo nindanīyātsvakarmaṇaḥ 
Subhv vṛthājvalitakopāgneḥ paruṣākṣaravādinaḥ 
Subhv durjanasyauṣadhaṃ nāsti kiṃcidanyadanuttarāt 
Subhv khalānāṃ kaṇṭakānāṃ ca dvidhaivāsti pratikriyā 
Subhv upānanmukhabhaṅgo vā dūrato vāpi varjanam 
Subhv jīvannapi na tatkartuṃ śaknoti sujanastathā 
Subhv durjano yanmṛtaḥ kuryātparebhyohitamuttaram 
Subhv yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ tattaddeyaṃ guṇavate kila 
Subhv ata eva khalo doṣānsādhubhyaḥ saṃprayacchati 
Subhv rogoṇḍajoṅkurognirviṣamaśvataro ghuṇāḥ krimayaḥ 
Subhv prakṛtikṛtaghnaśca naraḥ svāśrayamavināśya naidhante 
Subhv na vinā paravādena ramate durjano janaḥ 
Subhv śvā hi sarvarasānbhuktvā vināmedhyaṃ na tṛpyati 
Subhv varamatyantaviphalaḥ sukhasevyo hi sajjanaḥ 
Subhv na tu prāṇaharastīkṣṇaḥ śaravatsaphalaḥ khalaḥ 
Subhv svabhāvenaiva niśitaḥ kṛtapakṣagrahopi san 
Subhv śaravadguṇanirmuktaḥ khalaḥ kasya na bhedakaḥ 
Subhv durjanaḥ sujanīkartuṃ yatnenāpi na śakyate 
Subhv saṃskāreṇāpi laśunaṃ kaḥ sugandhīkariṣyati 
Subhv nīcaḥ samutthitovaśyamanavāpya parāśrayam 
Subhv chidreṇa ratimāpnoti dṛṣṭāntotra kaṭībhavaḥ 
Subhv paravāde daśavadanaḥ pararandhranirīkṣaṇe sahasrākṣaḥ 
Subhv sadvṛttavṛttiharaṇe bāhusahasrārjuno nīcaḥ 
Subhv durjanadūṣitamanasāṃ puṃsāṃ sujanepi nāsti viśvāsaḥ 
Subhv bālaḥ pāyasadagdhodadhyapi phūtkṛtya bhakṣayati 
Subhv ādau lajjayati kṛtaṃ madhye paribhavati riktamavasāne 
Subhv khalasaṃgatasya kathayata yadi susthitamasti kiṃcidapi 
Subhv paramarmadivyadarśiṣu jātyaivocitanigūḍhavaireṣu 
Subhv kaḥ khalu khaleṣu śaṅkāṃ ślathayiṣyati dambhānirateṣu 
Subhv ajñaḥ sukhamārādhyaḥ sukhataramārādhyate viśeṣajñaḥ 
Subhv jñānalavadurvidagdhaṃ brahmāpi naraṃ na rañjayati 
Subhv asthānābhiniveśī prāyo jaḍe eva bhavati no vidvān 
Subhv bālādanyaḥ kombhasi jighṛkṣatīndoḥ sphurabimbam 
Subhv labdhodayopi hi khalaḥ prathamaṃ svajanaṃ nayati paritāpam 
Subhv udgacchandavadahano janmabhuvaṃ dāru nirdahati 
Subhv alpaśrutalava eva prāyaḥ prakaṭayati vāgvibhavamuccaiḥ 
Subhv sarvatra kunaṭa eva hi nāṭakamadhikaṃ viḍambayati 
Subhv prakhalā eva guṇāvatāmākramya dhuraṃ puraḥ prakarṣanti 
Subhv tṛṇakāṣṭhameva jaladherupariplavate na ratnāni 
Subhv mahatāṃ yadeva mūrdhasu tadeva nīcāstṛṇāya manyante 
Subhv liṅgaṃ praṇamanti budhāḥ kākaḥ punarāsanīkurate 
Subhv saha vasatāmapyasatāṃ jalaruhajalavadbhavatyasaṃśleṣaḥ 
Subhv dūrepi satāṃ vasatāṃ prītiḥ kumudenduvadbhavati 
Subhv pariśuddhāmapi vṛttiṃ samāśrito durjanaḥ parānvyathate 
Subhv pavanāśinopi bhujagāḥ paropatāpaṃ na muñcanti 
Subhv sādhayati yatprayojanamajñastattasya kākatālīyam 
Subhv daivātkathamapyakṣaramutkirati ghuṇopi kāṣṭheṣu 
Subhv prāyaḥ khalaprakṛtayo nāparibhūtā hitāya kalpante 
Subhv puṣpyatyadhikamaśoko gaṇikācaraṇaprahāreṇa 
Subhv paramarmaghaṭṭanādiṣu khalasya yatkauśalaṃ na tatkṛtye 
Subhv yatsāmarthyamupahatau viṣasya tannopakārāya 
Subhv atisatkṛtāapi śaṭhāḥ sahabhuvamujjhanti jātu na prakṛtim 
Subhv śirasā mahāśvareṇāpi nanu dhṛto vakra eva śaśī 
Subhv vāyuriva khalajanoyaṃ prāyaḥ pararūpameti saṃparkāt 
Subhv santastu ravikarā iva sadasadyogepyasaṃśliṣṭāḥ 
Subhv prerayati paramanāryaḥ śakridaridropi jagadabhidrohe 
Subhv tejayati khaṅgadhārāṃ svayamasamarthā śilā chettum 
Subhv dūrepi parasyāgasi paṭurjano nātmanaḥ samīpepi 
Subhv svaṃ vraṇamakṣi na paśyati śaśini kalaṅkaṃ nirūpayati 
Subhv sādhuṣvevātitarāmaruṃtudāḥ svāṃ vivṛṇvate vṛttim 
Subhv vyādhā nighnanti mṛgānmṛtamapi na tu siṃhamādadate 
Subhv avikāriṇamapi sajjanamaniśamanāryaḥ prabādhatetyartham 
Subhv kamalinyā kimiha kṛtaṃ himasya yattāṃ sadā dahati 
Subhv svaguṇāniva paradoṣānvaktuṃ na satopi śakruvanti budhāḥ 
Subhv svaguṇāniva paradoṣānasatopi khalāstu kathayanti 
Subhv kṛtvāpi yena lajjāmupaiti sādhuḥ paroditenāpi 
Subhv tadakṛtvaiva khalajanaḥ svayamudgiratīti dhiglaghutām 
Subhv āptvāpyātmavināśaṃ gaṇayati na khalaḥ paravyasanakaṣṭam 
Subhv prāyaḥ sahasranāśe samaramukhe nṛtyati kabandhaḥ 
Subhv prakṛtikhalatvādasatāṃ doṣa iva guṇopi bādhate lokān 
Subhv viṣakusumānāṃ gandhaḥ surabhirapi manāṃsi mohayati 
Subhv labdhocchrāyo nīcaḥ prathamataraṃ svāminaṃ parābhavati 
Subhv pathi dhūlirajo hyādāvutthāpakameva saṃvṛṇute 
Subhv mṛgamadakarpūrāgurucandanagandhādhivāsito laśunaḥ 
Subhv na tyajati gandhamaśubhaṃ prakṛtimiva sahotthitāṃ nīcaḥ 
Subhv upakṛtamanena suhṛdayamiti durjaneṣvasti na kvacidapekṣā 
Subhv hotrā saha svamāśrayamudvṛttognirdahatyeva 
Subhv upakṛtireva khalānāṃ doṣasya garīyaso bhavati hetuḥ 
Subhv anukūlācaraṇena hi kupyanti vyādhayotyartham 
Subhv na paraṃ phalati hi kiṃcitkhala evānarthamāvahati yāvat 
Subhv mārayati sapadi viṣatarurāśrayamāṇaṃ śramāpanude 
Subhv svārthanirapekṣa eva hi paropaghātosatāṃ vyasanameva 
Subhv aśanāyodanyā vā viramati phaṇino na dandaśataḥ 
Subhv ekībhāvaṃ gatayorjalapayasormittracetasośvaiva 
Subhv vyatirekakṛtau śaktirhaṃsānāṃ durjanānāṃ ca 
Subhv śalyamapi skhaladantaḥ soḍhuṃ śakyate hālahaladigdham 
Subhv dhīrairna punarakāraṇakupitakhalālīkadurvacanam 
Subhv mṛgamīnasajjanānāṃ tṛṇajalasaṃtoṣavihitavṛttīnām 
Subhv lubdhakadhīvarapiśunā niṣkāraṇavairiṇo jagati 
Subhv prārambhatotivipulaṃ bhṛśakṛśamante vibhedakṛnmalinam 
Subhv mahiṣaviṣāṇamivānṛju puruṣaṃ bhayadaṃ khalaprema 
Subhv pātramapātrīkurute dahati guṇānsnehamāśu nāśayati 
Subhv amale malaṃ prayacchati dīpajvāleva khalamaittrī 
Subhv samarpitāḥ kasya na tena doṣā
Subhv haṭhādguṇā vā na hṛtāḥ khalena 
Subhv tathāpi doṣairna viyujyatesau
Subhv spṛṣṭopi naikena guṇena citram 
Subhv ārādhyamāno bahubhiḥ prakārair
Subhv nārādhyate nāma kimatra citram 
Subhv ayaṃ tvapūrvaḥ pratibhāviśeṣo
Subhv yatsevyamāno riputāmupaiti 
Subhv vidvānupālambhamavāpya doṣān
Subhv nivartatesau paritapyate ca 
Subhv jñātastu doṣo mama sarvatheti
Subhv pāpo janaḥ pāpataraṃ karoti 
Subhv evameva nahi jīvyate khalāt
Subhv tatra kā nṛpativallabhe kathā 
Subhv pūrvameva hi suduḥsaho nalaḥ
Subhv kiṃ punaḥ prabalavāyuneritaḥ 
Subhv amarairamṛtaṃ na pītamabdher
Subhv na ca hālāhalamulvaṇaṃ hareṇa 
Subhv vidhinā nihitaṃ khalasya vāci
Subhv dvayametadbahirekamantaranyat 
Subhv nimittamuddiśya hi yaḥ prakupyati
Subhv dhruvaṃ sa tasyāpagase prasīdati 
Subhv akāraṇadveṣi mano hi yasya vai
Subhv kathaṃ parastaṃ paritoṣayiṣyati 
Subhv itaradeva bahirmukhamucyate
Subhv hṛdi tu yatsphuratītaradeva tat 
Subhv caritametadadhīravitārakaṃ
Subhv dhuri payaḥpratibimbamivāsatām 
Subhv kva piśunasya gatiḥ pratihanyate
Subhv daśati dṛṣṭamapi śrutamapyasau 
Subhv atisuduṣkaramavyatiriktadṛk
Subhv chrutibhirapyatha dṛṣṭiviṣairidam 
Subhv gajaturagaśataiḥ prayāntu mūrkhā
Subhv dhanarahitā vibudhāḥ prayāntu padbhyām 
Subhv giriśikhiragatāpi kākapālī
Subhv pulinagatairna sameti rājahaṃsaiḥ 
Subhv hrepayati priyavacanairādaramupadarśayankhalīkurute 
Subhv utkarṣayaṃśca laghayati mūrkhasuhṛtsarvathā varjyaḥ 
Subhv prakaṭamapi na saṃvṛṇoti doṣaṃ
Subhv guṇalavalampaṭa eṣa sādhuvargaḥ 
Subhv atiparuṣaruṣaṃ vināpi doṣaiḥ
Subhv piśunaśunāṃ ruṣatāṃ prayāti kālaḥ 
Subhv yadā vigṛhṇāti tadā hataṃ yaśaḥ
Subhv karoti maittrīmatha dūṣitā guṇāḥ 
Subhv sthitiṃ samīkṣyobhayathā parīkṣakaḥ
Subhv karotyavajñopahataṃ pṛthagjanam 
Subhv iṣṭo vā sukṛtaśatopalālito vā
Subhv śliṣṭo vā vyasanaśatābhirakṣito vā 
Subhv dauḥśīlyājjanayati naiva jātvasādhur
Subhv visrambhaṃ bhujaga ivāṅkamadhyasuptaḥ 
Subhv rūkṣaṃ virauti parikupyati nirnimittaṃ
Subhv sparśena dūṣayati vārayati praveśam 
Subhv lajjākaraṃ daśati naiva ca tṛpyatīti
Subhv kauleyakasya ca khalasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ 
Subhv pādāhatotha dṛḍhadaṇḍavighaṭṭito vā
Subhv yaṃ daṃṣṭrayā daśati taṃ kila hanti sarpaḥ 
Subhv kopyanya eva piśunodya bhujaṃgadharmā
Subhv karṇe paraṃ spṛśati hantyaparaṃ samūlam 
Subhv yuktaṃ yayā kila nirantaralabdhavṛtter
Subhv asyābhimānatamasaḥ prasaraṃ niroddhum 
Subhv vidvattayā jagati tāmavalambya kecit
Subhv tanvantyahaṃkṛtimaho śataśākhamāndhyam 
Subhv nanvāśrayasthitiriyaṃ tava kālakūṭa
Subhv kenottarottaraviśiṣṭapadopadiṣṭā 
Subhv prāgarṇavasya hṛdaye vṛṣalakṣmaṇotha
Subhv kaṇṭhedhunā vasasi vāci punaḥ khalānām 
Subhv prāyaḥ svabhāvamalino mahatāṃ samīpe
Subhv ṭiṣṭhankhalaḥ prakuruterthijanopaghātam 
Subhv śītārditaiḥ sakalalokasukhāvahopi
Subhv dhūme sthite nahi sukhena niṣevyatogniḥ 
Subhv dhūmaḥ payodharapadaṃ kathamapyavāpya
Subhv varṣāmbubhiḥ śamayati jvalanasya tejaḥ 
Subhv daivādavāpya kaluṣaprakṛtirmahattvaṃ
Subhv prāyaḥ svabandhujanameva tiraskaroti 
Subhv ullāsitākhilakhalasya viśṛṅkhalasya
Subhv prāgjātavismṛtanijādhamakarmavṛtteḥ 
Subhv daivādavāptavibhavasya guṇadviṣosya
Subhv nīcasya gocaragataiḥ sukhamāsyate kaiḥ 
Subhv nāścaryametadadhunā hatadaivayogā
Subhv durccaiḥsthitiryadadhamo na mahānubhāvaḥ 
Subhv rathyākalaṅkaśatasaṃkarasaṃkulopi
Subhv pṛṣṭhe bhavatyavakaro na punarnidhānam 
Subhv prasahya maṇimuddharenmakaravaktradaṃṣṭrāntarāt
Subhv samudramapi saṃtaretpracaladūrmimālākulam 
Subhv bhujagamapi kopitaṃ śirasi puśpavaddhārayen
Subhv na tu pratiniviṣṭamūrkhajanacittamārādhayet 
Subhv labheta sikatāsu tailamapi yatnataḥ pīḍayan
Subhv pibecca mṛgatṛṣṇikāsu salilaṃ pipāsārditaḥ 
Subhv kadācidapi paryaṭacchaśaviṣāṇamāsādayen
Subhv na tu pratiniviṣṭamūrkhajanacittamārādhayet 
Subhv araṇyaruditaṃ kṛtaṃ śavaśarīramudvartitaṃ
Subhv sthalebjamavaropitaṃ suciramūṣare varṣitam 
Subhv śvapucchamavanāmitaṃ badhirakarṇajāpaḥ kṛtaḥ
Subhv kṛtāndhamukhamaṇḍanā yadabudho janaḥ secitaḥ 
Subhv vṛthā dugdhonaḍvānstanabharanatā gauriti ciraṃ
Subhv pariṣvaktaḥ ṣaṇḍho yuvatirita lāvaṇyasahitā 
Subhv kṛtā vaidūryāśā vikacakiraṇe kācaśakale
Subhv mayā mūḍhena tvāṃ kṛpaṇamaguṇajñaṃ praṇamatā 
Subhv svapakṣacchedaṃ vā samucitaphalabhraṃśamathavā
Subhv svamūrterbhaṅgaṃ vā patanamaśucau nāśamathavā 
Subhv śaraḥ prāpnotyetānhṛdayapathasaṃsthopi dhanuṣa
Subhv ṛjorvakrāśleṣādbhavati khalu suvyaktamaśubham 
Subhv guṇāṇāṃ sā śaktirvipadamanubadhnanti yadamī
Subhv prasannastadvedhā mama yadi na tairyogamakarot 
Subhv viṣaṇṇaṃ daurgatyāditi guṇinamālokya viguṇaḥ
Subhv karoti sve gehe dhruvamatisamṛddhyotsavamasau 
Subhv avekṣya svātmānaṃ viguṇamaparānichhati tathā
Subhv phalatyetanno cedvilapati na santīha guṇinaḥ 
Subhv nimārṣṭuṃ śaptuṃ vā paribhavitumudyacchati tato
Subhv pyaho nīce ramyā saguṇavijigīṣā vidhiktā 
Subhv yadi paraguṇā na kṣamyante yatasva tadarjane
Subhv nahi parayaśo nindāvyājairalaṃ parimārjitum 
Subhv viramasi na cedicchādveṣaprasaktamanorathā
Subhv dinakarakarānpāṇicchattrairnudacchramameṣyasi 
Subhv prakṛṣṭe saṃparke bhaṇibhujagayorjanmajanite
Subhv maṇirnāherdoṣānbhajati na ca sarpo maṇiguṇān 
Subhv asādhuḥ sādhurvā bhavati nanu jātyaiva puruṣo
Subhv nasaṅgāddaurjanyaṃ na ca sujanatā kasyacidapi 
Subhv na viṣamamṛtīkartuṃ śakyaṃ prayatnaśatairapi
Subhv tyajati kaṭutāṃ na svāṃ nimbaḥ sthitopi payohrade 
Subhv guṇaparicitāmāryāṃ vāṇīṃ na jalpati durjanaś
Subhv ciramapi balādhmāte lohe kutaḥ kanakākṛtiḥ 
Subhv varamahimukhe krodhāviṣṭe karau viniveśitau
Subhv viṣamapi varaṃ pītvā suptaṃ kṛtāntaniveśane 
Subhv girivarataṭānmuktaścātmā varaṃ śatadhā kṛto
Subhv na tu khalajanāvāptairarthaiḥ kṛtaṃ hitamātmanaḥ 
Subhv varṇasthaṃ gurulāghavaṃ na gaṇathatyāśaṅkate na kvacid
Subhv rūpaṃ naiva parīkṣate na puruṣaṃ vṛtteṣu vārtā kutaḥ 
Subhv kaṣṭaṃ nāyaśaso vibheti mahato naivāpaśabdāntarān
Subhv mṛtyurmūrkhakaviḥ khalaḥ kunṛpatiścauraśca tulyakriyāḥ 
Subhv siṃho vyākaraṇasya karturaharatprāṇānpriyānpāṇiner
Subhv mīṃāṃsākṛtamunmamātha tarasā hastī muniṃ jaiminim 
Subhv chandojñānanidhiṃ jaghāna makaro velātaṭe piṅgalam
Subhv ajñānāhatacetasāmatiruṣāṃ korthastiraścāṃ guṇaiḥ 
Subhv vandyānnindati duḥkhitānupahasatyābādhate bāndhavāñ
Subhv chūrāndveṣṭi dhanacyutānparibhavatyājñāpayatyāśritān 
Subhv guhyāni prakaṭikaroti ghaṭayanyatnena vairāśayaṃ
Subhv brūte śīghramavācyamujjhati guṇāngṛhṇāti doṣānkhalaḥ 
Subhv hasati lasati harṣāttīvraduḥkhe pareṣāṃ
Subhv skhalati galati mohādātmanaḥ kleśaleśe 
Subhv nadati vadati nindyaṃ mānināṃ kiṃ ca nīcaḥ
Subhv paruṣavacanamalpaṃ śrāvito hantumeti 
Subhv yadi satsaṅganirato bhaviṣyasi bhaviṣyasi 
Subhv athāsajjaganoṣṭhīṣu patiṣyasi patiṣyasi 
Subhv karṇe tatkathayanti dundubhiravai rāṣṭre yaduddhoṣitaṃ
Subhv tannamrāṅgatayā vadanti karuṇaṃ yasmātrapāvānbhavet 
Subhv ślāghante tadudīryate yadariṇāpyugraṃ na marmāntakṛ
Subhv dye kecinnanu śāvyamaugdhyanidhayaste bhūbhṛtāṃ rañjakāḥ 
Subhv bhaṇḍastāṇḍavamaṇḍape caṭukathāvīthīṣu kanthākavir
Subhv goṣṭhaśva svagṛhāṅgaṇe śikharibhūgarte khaṭākhuḥ sphuṭam 
Subhv piṇḍīśūratayā viṭaśva paṭutāṃ bhūbhṛdgṛhe gāhate
Subhv gacchanti hradakṛṣṭakacchapatulāṃ citraṃ tatonyatra te 
Subhv jāḍyaṃ hrīmati gaṇyate vratarucau dambhaḥ śucau kaitavaṃ
Subhv śūre nirghṛṇatā ṛjau vimatitā dainyaṃ priyālāpini 
Subhv tejasvinyavaliptatā mukharatā vaktaryaśaktiḥ sthire
Subhv tatko nāma guṇo bhavedguṇavatāṃ yo durjanairnāṅkitaḥ 
Subhv ākhuḥ kailāsaśailaṃ tulayati karaṭastārkṣyamāṃsābhilāṣī
Subhv babhrurlāṅgūlamūlaṃ calayati capalastakṣakāhiṃ jighāṃsuḥ 
Subhv bhekaḥ pāraṃ yiyāaurbhujagamapi mahāghasmarasyāmburāśeḥ
Subhv prāyeṇāsannapātaḥ smarati samucitaṃ karma na kṣudrakarmā 
Subhv aguṇakaṇo guṇorāśirdvayamiha daivātkhalamukhe patitam 
Subhv prasarati tailamivaikaḥ salile ghṛtavajjaḍatvametyanyaḥ 
Subhv śaraṇaṃ kiṃ prapannāni viṣavanmārayanti kim 
Subhv na tyajyante na bhujyante kṛpaṇena dhanāni yat 
Subhv kṛpaṇena samo dātā na bhūto na bhaviṣyati 
Subhv aspṛśanneva vittāni yaḥ parebhyaḥ prayacchati 
Subhv yā vipattirdhanāpāye navā bhogivadānyayoḥ 
Subhv prajñāpakarṣātprāgeva prāptā hi kṛpaṇena sā 
Subhv tyāgopabhogaśūnyena dhanena dhanino yadi 
Subhv bhavāmaḥ kiṃ na tenaiva dhanena dhanino vayam 
Subhv gṛhamadhyanikhātena dhanena ramate yadi 
Subhv sa tu tenānusāreṇa ramate kiṃ na meruṇā 
Subhv kiṃśuke kiṃ śukaḥ kuryātphalitepi bubhukṣitaḥ 
Subhv adātari samṛddhepi kiṃ kuryurupajīvinaḥ 
Subhv dānopabhogabandhyā yā suhṛdhbiryā na bhujyate 
Subhv puṃsāṃ yadi hi sā lakṣmīralakṣmīḥ katama bhavet 
Subhv atisaṃcayakart ṇāṃ vittamanyasya kāraṇām 
Subhv anyaiḥ saṃcīyate yatnādanyaiśca madhu pīyate 
Subhv yaddadāsi viśiṣṭebhyo yadāśnāsi dine dine 
Subhv tatte vittamahaṃ manye śeṣaṃ kasyāpi rakṣasi 
Subhv viḍambanaiva puṃsi śrīḥ parapraṇayapāṃsule 
Subhv kāntiṃ kāmiha kurvīta kuṇau kaṭakakalpanā 
Subhv kṛtvopakāraṃ yastasmādvāñchati pratyupakriyām 
Subhv dīnastṛṣṇāvidheyatvādvāntamapyupaleḍhi saḥ 
Subhv dānaṃ bhogo nāśastisro gatayo bhavanti vittasya 
Subhv yo na dadāti na bhuṅkte tasya tṛtīyā gatirnāśaḥ 
Subhv dānaṃ bhogaṃ ca vinā dhanasattāmātrakeṇa ceddhaninaḥ 
Subhv vayamapi kimiti na dhaninistiṣṭhati naḥ kāñcano meruḥ 
Subhv dhaninopyadānabhogā gaṇyante dhuri mahādaridrāṇām 
Subhv hanti na yataḥ pipāsāmataḥ samudropi marureva 
Subhv abhyupayuktāḥ sadbhirgatāgatairaharahaḥ sunirviṇṇāḥ 
Subhv kṛpaṇajanasaṃnikarṣaṃ saṃprāpyārthāḥ svapantīva 
Subhv upabhogakātarāṇāṃ puruṣāṇāmarthasaṃcayaparāṇām 
Subhv kanyāratnamiva gṛhe tiṣṭhantyarthāḥ parasyārthe 
Subhv te mūrkhatarā loke yeṣāṃ dhanamasti nāsti ca tyāgaḥ 
Subhv kevalamarjunarakṣaṇaviyogaduḥkhānyanubhavanti 
Subhv kṛpaṇasamṛddhīnāmapi bhoktāraḥ santi kecidatinipuṇāḥ 
Subhv jalasaṃpadomburāśeryānti layaṃ śaśvadaurvāgnau 
Subhv prāptānapi na labhante bhogānbhoktuṃ svakarmabhiḥ kṛpaṇāḥ 
Subhv mukharogaḥ kila bhavati drākṣāpāke balibhujāṃ hi 
Subhv na niryiyāsanti kadaryahastād
Subhv dhanāni pāṃsoriva tailaleśāḥ 
Subhv daivātkadācidviniyoktureva
Subhv nirgantumicchantyasubhiḥ sahaiva 
Subhv saṃcitaṃ kratuṣu nopayujyate
Subhv yācitaṃ guṇavate na dīyatye 
Subhv tatkadaryaparirakṣitaṃ dhanaṃ
Subhv caurapārthivagṛheṣu gacchati 
Subhv varamamī taravo vanagocarāḥ
Subhv śakunisārthaviluptaphalaśriyaḥ 
Subhv na tu dhanāḍhyagṛhāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ phaṇa
Subhv nihitaratnabhujaṃgamavṛttayaḥ 
Subhv susaṃvṛtairjīvitavatsurakṣitair
Subhv nijepi dehe kṛtayantraṇasya ca 
Subhv tavānumārgaṃ vrajato bhavāntare
Subhv śaṭhairdhanaiḥ pañcapadī na pūritā 
Subhv aho dhanānāṃ mahatī vidagdhatā
Subhv sukhoṣitānāṃ kṛpaṇasya veśmani 
Subhv vrajanti na tyāgadaśāṃ na bhogyatāṃ
Subhv parāṃ ca kāñcitprathayanti nirvṛtim 
Subhv na śāntāntastṛṣṇāṃ dhanalavaṇavārivyatikaraiḥ
Subhv kṣatacchāyaḥ kāyaściravirasarūkṣāśanatayā 
Subhv anidrā mandāgnirnṛpasalilacaurānalabhayāt
Subhv kadaryāṇāṃ kaṣṭaṃ sphuṭamadhanakaṣṭādapi param 
Subhv ekaikātiśayālavaḥ paraguṇajñānaikavaijñānikāḥ
Subhv santyete dhanikāḥ kalāsu sakalāsvācāryacaryācaṇāḥ 
Subhv apyete sumanogirāṃ niśamanādbibhyatyaho ślāghayā
Subhv dhūte mūrdhani kuṇḍale kaṣaṇataḥ kṣīṇe bhavetāmiti 
Subhv prītiṃ na prakaṭīkaroti suhṛdi dravyavyayāśaṅkayā
Subhv bhītaḥ pratyupakārakāraṇabhayānnākṛṣyate sevayā 
Subhv mithyā jalpati vittamārgaṇabhayātstutyāpi na prīyate
Subhv kīnāśo vibhavavyayavyatikaratrastaḥ kathaṃ prāṇiti 
Subhv matvā sāraṃ guṇānāṃ śirasi yadi śaśī sthāpito daivayogā
Subhv dīśena kṣīṇabimbaṃ sakalamupacayaṃ kiṃ na nītaḥ kṣaṇena 
Subhv mithyaivaṃ khyāpayanto guṇini saralatāṃ lokabhaktyarthamuccair
Subhv āḍhyāḥ kurvanti vittavyayacakitadhiyo mānamarthena śūnyam 
Subhv brahmāṇḍamaṇḍalīmātraṃ kiṃ lobhāya manasvinaḥ 
Subhv śapharīsphuritairnābdheḥ kṣubdhatā jātu jāyate 
Subhv nālpīyasi nibadhnanti padamuddāmacetasaḥ 
Subhv yeṣāṃ bhuvanalābhepi niḥsīmāno manorathāḥ 
Subhv puṃsāmunnatacittānāṃ sukhāvahamidaṃ dvayam 
Subhv sarvasaṅganivṛttirvā vibhūtirvā suvistarā 
Subhv ayaṃ bandhuḥ paro veti gaṇanā laghucetasām 
Subhv puṃsāmudāracittānāṃ vasudhaiva kuṭumbakam 
Subhv jarāmaraṇadaurgatyavyādhayastāvadāsatām 
Subhv janmaiva kiṃ na dhīrasya bhūyo bhūyastrapākaram 
Subhv parivartini saṃsāre mṛtaḥ ko vā na jāyate 
Subhv sa jāto yena jātena yāti vaṃśaḥ samunnatim 
Subhv api nāma sa dṛśyeta puruṣātiśayo bhuvi 
Subhv garvocchūnamukhā yena dhanino nāvalokitāḥ 
Subhv pṛthvī pṛthvī guṇā mānyāḥ santi bhūpā vivekinaḥ 
Subhv parābhavāpadaṃ yānti kasmādunnatabuddhayaḥ 
Subhv adṛṣṭamukhabhaṅgasya yuktamandhasya yācitum 
Subhv aho bata mahatkaṣṭaṃ cakṣuṣmānapi yācate 
Subhv dāridryānalasaṃtāpaḥ śāntaḥ saṃtoṣavāriṇā 
Subhv yācakāśāvighātāntardāhaṃ ko nāma paśyatu 
Subhv paripūrṇaguṇābhogagarimodnāra eva saḥ 
Subhv trijagatspṛhaṇīyesminna rucirdraviṇepi yat 
Subhv vidyayaiva mado yeṣāṃ kārpaṇyaṃ ca dhane sati 
Subhv teṣāṃ daivābhiśaptānāṃ salilādagnirutthitaḥ 
Subhv kiṃ tayā kriyate lakṣmyā yā vadhūriva kevalā 
Subhv yā na veśyeva sāmānyā pathikairapi bhujyate 
Subhv tyāgo guṇo vittavatāṃ vittaṃ tyāgavatāṃ guṇaḥ 
Subhv parasparaviyuktau tu vittatyāgau viḍambanā 
Subhv kusumastabakasyeva dvayī vṛttirmanasvinaḥ 
Subhv mūrdhni vā sarvalokasya śīryate vana eva vā 
Subhv nṛṇāṃ dhuri sa evaiko yaḥ kaścittyāgapāṇinā 
Subhv nirmārṣṭi prārthanāpāṃsudhūsaraṃ mukhamarthinām 
Subhv ākāramātravijñānasaṃpāditamanorathāḥ 
Subhv dhanyāste ye na śṛṇvanti dīnāḥ praṇayināṃ giraḥ 
Subhv buddhiryā sattvarahitā strītvaṃ tatkevalaṃ matam 
Subhv sattvaṃ cānayasaṃpannaṃ tatpaśutvaṃ na pauruṣam 
Subhv kāmaṃ priyānapi prāṇānvimuñcanti manasvinaḥ 
Subhv icchanti na tvamitrebhyo mahatīmapi satkriyām 
Subhv atyadbhutamimaṃ manye svabhāvamamanasvinaḥ 
Subhv yadupakriyamāṇopi prīyate na vilīyate 
Subhv pratyupakurvatpūrvaṃ kṛtopakāramapi lajjayati cetaḥ 
Subhv yastu vihitopakārādupakāraḥ sodhiko mṛtyoḥ 
Subhv pratyupakurvanbahvapi na bhavati pūrvopakāriṇā tulyaḥ 
Subhv ekonukaroti kṛtaṃ niṣkāraṇameva kurutenyaḥ 
Subhv jīvañjīvayati hi yo jñātijanaṃ parijanaṃ ca suhṛdaśca 
Subhv tasya saphalā gṛhaśrīrdhiganupajīvyāṃ dhanasamṛddhim 
Subhv yacchañjalamapi jalado vallabhatāmeti sarvalokasya 
Subhv nityaṃ prasāritakaraḥ savitāmapi bhavatyacakṣuṣyaḥ 
Subhv nāptaṃ yatkenacidapi manorathā api yato nivartante 
Subhv tadyapi na labhyatenyanmanasvinaḥ kimabhimānaphalam 
Subhv ghaṭanaṃ vighaṭanamathavā kāryāṇāṃ bhavati vidhiniyogena 
Subhv ucitenucite karmaṇi vṛttinivṛttī mamāyatte 
Subhv kalpasthāyi na jīvitamaiścaryaṃ nāpyate ca yadabhimatam 
Subhv lokastathāpyakāryaṃ kurute kāryaṃ kimuddiśya 
Subhv dhanabāhulyamahetuḥ kopi nisargeṇa muktakaraḥ 
Subhv prāvṛṣi kasyāmbumucaḥ saṃpattiḥ kimadhikāmbunidheḥ 
Subhv utpāditā svayamiyaṃ yadi tattanūjā
Subhv tātena vā yadi tadā bhaginī khalu śrīḥ 
Subhv yadyanyasaṃgamavatī ca tadā parastrī
Subhv tattyāgabaddhamanasaḥ sudhiyo bhavanti 
Subhv draviṇārjanajaḥ pariśramaḥ
Subhv phalitopyasya janasya nīrasaḥ 
Subhv draviṇārjanamātmatuṣṭaye
Subhv paramāvarjayituṃ guṇārjanam 
Subhv yaḥ praśaṃsati naro naramanyaṃ
Subhv devatāsu varadāsu satīṣu 
Subhv mugdhadhīrdhanalavaspṛhayālus
Subhv taṃ nṛśaṃsamahamādyamavaimi 
Subhv yathā śarīraṃ kila jīvitena
Subhv vinākṛtaṃ kāṣṭhamivāvabhāti 
Subhv tathaiva lajjīvitamapyavaimi
Subhv lokottareṇa sphuritena śūnyam 
Subhv santopi santaḥ kva kirantu tejaḥ
Subhv kva nojjvalantu kva nu na prathantām 
Subhv vidhāya ruddhā nanu vedhasaiva
Subhv brahmāṇḍakośe ghaṭadīpakalpāḥ 
Subhv kadarthitasyāpi hi dhairyavṛtter
Subhv na śakyate sattvaguṇaḥ pramārṣṭum 
Subhv adhomukhasyāpi kṛtasya vahner
Subhv nādhaḥ śikhā yānti kadācideva 
Subhv jātaśca nāma na vinaṅkṣyanti cetyayuktam
Subhv utpāda eva niyameva vināśahetuḥ 
Subhv tulye ca nāma maraṇavyasanopatāpe
Subhv mṛtyurvaraṃ parahitāvahitāśayasya 
Subhv iyatyapyetasminniravadhimahatyadhvani guṇās
Subhv ta evāmī dvitrā jaraṭhajaraṭhā yānti gaṇanām 
Subhv aho grāmyo lokaḥ sa na paramamībhiḥ kṛtadhṛtiḥ
Subhv smayastabdhoyāvatkalayati samagraṃ tṛṇamidam 
Subhv svacittaparicintayaiva paritāpamātmanyamī
Subhv na bibhrati manāsvino yadamunā na tāvatkṣatiḥ 
Subhv aharniśamihaiva ye paramanonuvṛttyā punar
Subhv vahanti vijigīṣutāṃ kimiva tenukampāspadam 
Subhv vipulahṛdayairanyaiḥ kaiścijjagajjanitaṃ purā
Subhv vidhṛtamaparairdattaṃ cānyairvijitya tṛṇaṃ yathā 
Subhv iha hi bhuvanānyanye dhīrāścaturdaśa bhuñjate
Subhv katipayapurasvāmye puṃsāṃ ka eṣa madajvaraḥ 
Subhv abhuktāyāṃ yasyāṃ kṣaṇamapi na yātaṃ nṛpaśatair
Subhv bhuvastasyā lābhe ka iva bahumānaḥ kṣitibhujām 
Subhv tadaṃśasyāpyaṃśe tadavayavaleśepi patayo
Subhv viṣāde kartavye vidadhati jaḍāḥ pratyuta mudam 
Subhv pareṣāṃ cetāṃsi pratidivasamāyāsya bahudhā
Subhv prasādaṃ kiṃ netuṃ viśāsi hṛdaya kleśakalilam 
Subhv prasanne tvayyeva svayamuditacintāmaṇiguṇe
Subhv viviktaḥ saṃkalpaḥ kimabhilaṣitaṃ puṣyati na te 
Subhv vināpyarthairdhīraḥ spṛśati bahumānonnatipadaṃ
Subhv pariṣvaktopyarthaiḥ paribhavapadaṃ yāti kṛpaṇaḥ 
Subhv svabhāvenodbhūtāṃ guṇasamudayāvāptivipulāṃ
Subhv dyutiṃ saiṃhīṃ na śvā dhṛtakanakamālopi labhate 
Subhv bhujyante svagṛhasthitā iva sukhaṃ yasyāthibhiḥ saṃpadaḥ
Subhv paṭvī yasya matistamaḥprahataye dvāveva tau prāṇitaḥ 
Subhv yastvātmaṃbharirunnatepi vibhave hīnaśca vidvattayā
Subhv tasyālekhyamaṇerivākṛtidhṛtaḥ sattāpyasattā nanu 
Subhv ādhārāya dharāvakāśavidhayepyākāśamālokane
Subhv bhāsvānātmamahattvasādhanavidhāvanye guṇāḥ kecana 
Subhv ityasminnupakārakāriṇi sadā varge paraṃ dustyaje
Subhv dainyavrīḍakalaṅkamujjhatu kathaṃ ceto mahācetasām 
Subhv nityaṃ yā gurubhṛtyabandhusujanairna svecchayā bhujyate
Subhv paśyanti spṛhayālavo na ripavo yāṃ vikramāsāditām 
Subhv yasyāḥ sādhuparikṣayeṇa suhṛdāṃ nāśena vā saṃbhavo
Subhv no saṃpadvipadeva sā guṇavatāṃ prītistayā kīdṛśī 
Subhv nyāyyaṃ mārgamanujjhataḥ sukṛtino daivādbhavantyāpado
Subhv yāstāḥ santu balerivādipuruṣāyorvīṃ svayaṃ yacchataḥ 
Subhv śakrasyeva jugupsitaiḥ subahubhirnindyairbhṛśaṃ karmabhir
Subhv devānāmupari prabhutvamapi me mā bhūttrapākāraṇam 
Subhv śayyā śādvalamāsanaṃ śuciśilā sadma dramāṇāmadhaḥ
Subhv śītaṃ nirjharavāri pānamaśanaṃ kandāḥ sahāyā mṛgāḥ 
Subhv ityprārthitasarvalabhyavibhave doṣoyameko vane
Subhv duṣprāpārthini yatparārthaghaṭanāvandhyairvṛthā sthīyate 
Subhv alpīyasāmeva hi janmabhūmes
Subhv tyāgaḥ pramādo viduṣāṃ na sosti 
Subhv sthānādapetā maṇayo vrajanti
Subhv rājñāṃ śiraḥ kākamukhāni bhekāḥ 
Subhv śūrāśca kṛtavidyāśca rūpavatyaśca yoṣitaḥ 
Subhv yatra yatra gamiṣyanti tatra tatra kṛtālayāḥ 
Subhv rudrodriṃ jaladhiṃ harirdiviṣado dūraṃ vihāyaḥ śritā
Subhv bhogīndrāḥ prabalā api prathamataḥ pātālamūle sthitāḥ 
Subhv līnā padmavane sarojanilayā manyerthisārthādbhiyā
Subhv dīnoddhāraparāyaṇāḥ kaliyuge satpūruṣāḥ kevalam 
Subhv prārabhyate na khalu vighnabhayena nīcaiḥ
Subhv prārabhya vighnavihatā viramanti madhyāḥ 
Subhv vighnaiḥ sahasraguṇitairapi hanyamānāḥ
Subhv prārabdhamuttamaguṇā na parityajanti 
Subhv prasaradbhiḥ karairyasya vikasanti na sadguṇāḥ 
Subhv tasya doṣākarasyeyaṃ kathaṃ nityāsti pūrṇatā 
Subhv kṣīṇaḥ kṣīṇaḥ samīpatvaṃ pūrṇaḥ pūrṇotidūratām 
Subhv upaiti mitrādyaccandro yuktaṃ yanmalinaḥ sadā 
Subhv kathaṃ na lajjitastādṛksavitā tejasāṃ nidhiḥ 
Subhv brahmāṇḍakhaṇḍikāṃ prāpya kurvanpādaprasārikām 
Subhv raverevodayaḥ ślāghyaḥ konyeṣāmudayagrahaḥ 
Subhv na tamāṃsi na tejāṃsi yasminnabhyudite sati 
Subhv kimanena na paryāptaṃ kāntatvaṃ śaśalakṣmaṇā 
Subhv susaṃtaptāpi nalinī yadviśvāsamupāgamat 
Subhv karānprasārya raviṇā dakṣiṇāśāvilambinā 
Subhv na kevalamanenātmā divasopi laghūkṛtaḥ 
Subhv vartate yena pātaṅgiḥ ṣaṇmāsāndvau ca vatsarau 
Subhv rāśiḥ sa eva candrasya na yāti divasatrayam 
Subhv śirasā dhāryamāṇopi somaḥ somena śaṃbhunā 
Subhv tathāpi kṛśatāṃ dhatte kaṣṭaḥ khalu parāśrayaḥ 
Qsv pa pājakasya
Subhv patatu vāriṇi yātu digantaraṃ
Subhv viśatu vahnimatho vrajatu kṣitim kathaṃ sa dantarahitaḥ sūryaḥ sūribhirucyate 
Subhv yo mīnarāśiṃ bhuktvaiva meṣaṃ bhoktuṃ samudyataḥ 
Subhv patatu vāriṇi yātu digantaraṃ
Subhv viśatu vahnimatho vrajatu kṣitim 
Subhv ravirasāviyatāsya guṇeṣu kā
Subhv sakalalokacamatkṛtiṣu kṣatiḥ
