Subhv tattāvadeva śaśinaḥ sphuritaṃ mahīyo
Subhv yāvanno tīkṣṇarucimaṇḍalamabhyupaiti 
Subhv abhyudyate sakaladhāmanidhau ca tasmin
Subhv nindoḥ sitābhraśakalasya ca ko viśeṣaḥ 
Subhv sadvṛttayaḥ sadasadarthavivekino ye
Subhv te paśya kīdṛśamamuṃ samudāharanti 
Subhv caurāsatīprabhṛtayo bruvate yadasya
Subhv tadgṛhyate yadi kṛtaṃ tadahaskareṇa 
Subhv ekaiva sāmṛtamayī sutarāmanarghā
Subhv kāpyastyasau śaśadharasya kalā yayaiva 
Subhv āropito guṇavidā parameśvareṇa
Subhv cūḍāmaṇau na gaṇitosya kalaṅkadoṣaḥ 
Subhv udyantyamūni subahūni mahāmahāṃsi
Subhv candropyalaṃ bhuvanamaṇḍalamaṇḍanāya 
Subhv sūryādṛte na tadudeti na cāstameti
Subhv yenoditena dinamastamitena rātriḥ 
Subhv lokānandādviramati na yaḥ kṣīyamāṇopi bhūyaḥ
Subhv svaḥsthe tasminkila dinamukhaṃ nūtanaṃ nābhaviṣyat 
Subhv daivaṃ kīdṛkkathamapi yathā bhartumātmānameva
Subhv vyagraḥ kālaṃ gamayati sakhe sopyayaṃ paśya candraḥ 
Subhv kṣīṇaścandro viśāti taraṇermaṇḍalaṃ māsi māsi
Subhv labdhvā kāṃcitpunarapi kalāṃ dūradūrānuvartī 
Subhv saṃpūrṇaścetkathamapi tathā spardhayodeti bhānor
Subhv no daurjanyādviramati jaḍo nāpi dainyādvyaraṃsīt 
Subhv pādanyāsaṃ kṣitidharagurormūrdhni kṛtvā sumeroḥ
Subhv krāntaṃ yena kṣapitatamasā madhyamaṃ dhāma viṣṇoḥ 
Subhv soyaṃ candraḥ patati gaganādalpaśeṣairmayūkhair
Subhv dūrāroho bhavati mahatāmapyupabhraṃśaniṣṭhaḥ 
Qsv kalaśakasya
Subhv pātaḥ pūṣṇo bhavati mahate nopatāpāya yasmāt
Subhv kālenāstaṃ ka iva na gatā yānti yāsyanti cānye kva tattejastādṛgjvalanamahaso nāśapiśunaṃ
Subhv parābhūtiḥ kvāsau visadṛśatarādrāhuśirasaḥ 
Subhv vidheryogādetatsamucitamidaṃ tu vyathayati
Subhv trapāhīno mitrāttadapi gagane yadviharati 
Subhv pātaḥ pūṣṇo bhavati mahate nopatāpāya yasmāt
Subhv kālenāstaṃ ka iva na gatā yānti yāsyanti cānye 
Subhv etāvattu vyathayati yadālokabāhyaistamobhis
Subhv tasminneva prakṛtimahati vyomni labdhovakāśaḥ 
Subhv ā sargātprativāsaraṃ rasaśatairyā bodhitā poṣitā
Subhv kalpāntāvasaretha saiva pṛthivī svaireva dagdhā karaiḥ 
Subhv kṛtvetthaṃ kimapi svakarma niyateḥ pūrvāparopaplutaṃ
Subhv kaṣṭaṃ sopi dināntavītakiraṇastigmāṃśurastaṃ gataḥ 
Subhv yenonmathya tamāṃsi māṃsalaghanaspardhīni sarvaṃ jagac
Subhv cakṣuṣmatparamārthataḥ kṛtamidaṃ devena tigmatviṣā 
Subhv tasminnastamite vivasvati kiyānkrūro jano durjano
Subhv yadbadhnāti dhṛtiṃ śaśāṅkaśakalāloketha dīpethavā 
Subhv śocyastāvadumāpatiḥ prabhutayā yo mūrdhni gaṅgokṣite
Subhv sacchidraṃ nṛśiraḥkapālamamalaṃ candraṃ ca dhatte samam 
Subhv candraḥ śocyatarastataḥ paribhavepyevaṃvidhe yaḥ sati
Subhv jyotsnāhāsavikāsapāṇḍuravapurmukhyāṃ mudaṃ puṣyati 
Subhv pūrṇaṃ vīcibhujaiḥ svavṛddhirabhasādinnduṃ samāliṅgati
Subhv kṣīṇaṃ dūrata eva muñcati pitā bhūtvā jalānāṃ nidhiḥ 
Subhv prakṣīṇasya tu yena tasya vasunā kṛtvā krameṇodayaṃ
Subhv pūrṇatve ca davīyasi sthitamaho mitrāya tasmai namaḥ 
Subhv dhvāntena grathitairgrahakṣitipaterdevasya dūrasthiteḥ
Subhv saccakrapramadāvahābhyuditatā kairnāma nākāṅkṣitā 
Subhv etenābhyuditena saṃprati punaḥ kaṣṭaṃ tathā ceṣṭitaṃ
Subhv lokastīkṣṇakaroyamityabhimukhaṃ nainaṃ yathā prekṣate 
Subhv dṛṣṭaiva yaṃ karasahasrahṛtāndhakāraṃ
Subhv bhītyāpayāntyanudinaṃ śataśaḥ piśācāḥ 
Subhv kṣīṇe vidhau harivilūnakaroti citraṃ
Subhv gṛhṇāti taṃ dyumaṇimabhrapiśāca ekaḥ 
Subhv tamograstaṃ jagatsarvaṃ trātuṃ bhānuḥ sadodyataḥ 
Subhv taṃ tu trātuṃ tamograstaṃ jagatyekopi na kṣamaḥ 
Subhv rātrau guṇanidheḥ padmātkumudaṃ yadanakṣaram 
Subhv prāptā lakṣmīḥ sa mahimā rājño jaḍanidherdhruvam 
Subhv ābhāti candrarahitā na kadāpi rātriś
Subhv candropi rātrirahito gatakāntireva 
Subhv kiṃ kāraṇaṃ yadanayoḥ pratimāsameko
Subhv jāto nistaratayā parirambhayogaḥ 
Subhv gaganaśayanalīnāṃ rātrimutsṛjya candro
Subhv vrajati dhavalapakṣe kṛṣṇapakṣe tu rātriḥ 
Subhv apasarati yadīndorvyomatalpe prasuptāt
Subhv truṭati tadanayoḥ kiṃ tāvatā dampatitvam 
Subhv āśāḥ prakāśayati yastimirāṇi bhaṅktvā
Subhv bodhaṃ dṛśāṃ diśati bhūriguṇeṣvabhīṣṭaḥ 
Subhv khedāya yasya na paropakṛtiṣvaṭāṭyā
Subhv dhīmānnamasyati na kastaminaṃ praśasyam 
Subhv vicārastathyo vā bhavatu vitatho vā kimaparaṃ
Subhv tathāpyuccairdhāmno bhavati bahujalpo janaravaḥ 
Subhv tulottīrṇasyāpi prathitamahimadhvastatamaso
Subhv ravestādṛktejo na bhavati hi kanyāṃ gata iti 
Subhv uḍugaṇaparivāro nāyakopyoṣadhīnām
Subhv amṛtamayaśarīraḥ kāntiyuktopi candraḥ 
Subhv bhavati vigataraśmirmaṇḍalaṃ prāpya bhānoḥ
Subhv parasadananiviṣṭaḥ ko laghutvaṃ na yāti 
Subhv uccaḥ satphalado yathāyamahamapyetādṛgetāvatā
Subhv spardhāṃ manda madoddhataḥ svajanakenārkeṇa mā mā kṛthāḥ 
Subhv dūrādeva bhavādṛśosya mahasā dhvastāḥ samastāḥ svayaṃ
Subhv naivecchatyayamatyayaṃ guṇisakhaḥ kasyāpi tejonidhiḥ 
Subhv tulyā sukhasthitiramuṣya mameti rājñi
Subhv spardhāṃ nijepi janake janakelihetau 
Subhv mā rājanandana kṛthāḥ sa hi sarvaloka
Subhv dhvāntāntakṛdgiriśahastapavitritātmā 
Subhv mātsaryeṇa jahadgrahānvisadṛśe dhūmadhvaje yogyatāṃ
Subhv jñātvā svāṃ vidadhattviṣaṃ dinapatirhāsyapraśāntyunmukhaḥ 
Subhv daivaṃ vetti na yaḥ śikhī sa parato nāmāstu tatsaṃbhavāḥ
Subhv syurdīpā api yadvaśena jagatāṃ tigmāṃśuvismārakāḥ 
Subhv pādmā ye madanuvratā dadhati te klāntiṃ tuṣārāhatā
Subhv yepyete divasā madekaśaraṇāḥ kārśyaṃ paraṃ yānti te 
Subhv gacchannitthamasau samāśritajanaprītyeva dūrāṃ diśaṃ
Subhv hemante bhagavānaharpatiraho loke gataḥ sevyatām 
Subhv nābhiṣeko na saṃskāraḥ siṃhasya kriyate vane 
Subhv vikramārjitasattvasya svayameva mṛgendratā 
Subhv ekohamasahāyohaṃ kṛśohamaparicchadaḥ 
Subhv svapnepyevaṃvidhā cintā mṛgendrasya na jāyate 
Subhv mattebhakumbhanirbhedakaṭhoranakharāśaniḥ 
Subhv mṛgāririti nāmnaiva laghutvaṃ yāti kesarī 
Subhv patanti naiva mātaṅgakumbhapāṭanalampaṭāḥ 
Subhv valgatsvapi kuraṅgeṣu mṛgārernakharāḥ kharāḥ 
Subhv kiṃ kirmaḥ ka upālabhyo yatredamasamañjasam 
Subhv kākiṇyapi na siṃhasya mūlyaṃ koṭistu dantinaḥ 
Subhv līlādalitadhṛṣṭebhakumbhapīṭhasya nirbhayaiḥ 
Subhv kathaṃ kesariṇaḥ krāntaṃ suptasyāpi mṛgaiḥ padam 
Subhv mattebhakumbhanirbhedarudhirāruṇapāṇinā 
Subhv hariṇā hariṇaḥ spardhāṃ varākaḥ kurute katham 
Subhv tāvadgarjati mātaṅgo vane madabharālasaḥ 
Subhv śirovilagnalāṅgūlo yāvannāyāti kesarī 
Subhv śauryadarpabalādhmātaśvasadgaṇḍāntaśobhinaḥ 
Subhv saṭāmutpāṭya siṃhasya kiṃ narāḥ sukhamāsate 
Subhv kopodekatalāghātanipatanmattadantinaḥ 
Subhv harerhariṇayuddhesya kiyānvyākṣepavistaraḥ 
Subhv yāvadasthiṣu saṃlagnāḥ karāḥ kesariṇaḥ kṣaṇam 
Subhv yūthasya prāṇitaṃ tāvattadaraṇyanivāsinaḥ 
Subhv sagrvagarjadgajagaṇḍamaṇḍalī
Subhv vikhaṇḍanoḍḍāmaravikramakramaḥ 
Subhv anantaviśrāntakuraṅgasaṃgara
Subhv prasaṅgamaṅgīkurute kathaṃ hariḥ 
Subhv siṃhaḥ śiśurapi nipatati madamalinakapolabhittiṣu gajeṣu 
Subhv prakṛtiriyaṃ sattvavatāṃ na khalu vayastejaso hetuḥ 
Subhv ekākini vanavāsinyarājalakṣmaṇyanītiśāstrejñe 
Subhv sattvocchrite mṛgapatau rājeti giraḥ pariṇamanti 
Subhv siṃhaḥ karoti vikramamalijhāṅkārāṅkite kare kariṇaḥ 
Subhv na punarnakhamukhavilikhitabhūdharakuharasthite nakule 
Subhv samadakarikumbhadāraṇamadapaṅkacchuritakesarasaṭasya 
Subhv siṃhasya ka iva vaktre karatalamādhātumutsahate 
Subhv niṣpragraheṣu karipotaśateṣu mohād
Subhv valgatsu bāliśatayā puratopyaṭatsu 
Subhv mattebhakumbhadalanocitacittavṛtteḥ
Subhv siṃhasya locananimīlanameva yuktam 
Subhv dṛṣṭvaiva roṣavaśaghūrṇitakesarāṃsa
Subhv māyāntamantakasamaṃ purato mṛgārim 
Subhv māṃsaṃ cikhādiṣubhiretya patatripūgair
Subhv bhrāntaṃ madāndhagajayūthapamastakeṣu 
Subhv yaḥ kesarī kharanakhakrakacograpāṇi
Subhv nirdāritebhavarakumbhasamudbhavena 
Subhv navyena śoṇitacayena nirastatṛṣṇo
Subhv nityaṃ babhūva dhigahodya tṛṇena sorthī 
Subhv visraṃ vapuḥ paravadhapravaṇā ca buddhis
Subhv tiryaktayaiva kathitaḥ sadasadvivekaḥ 
Subhv itthaṃ na kiṃcidapi sādhu mṛgādhipasya
Subhv tejastu tatsphurati yena jagadvarākam 
Subhv siṃhostu śatrurathavādhipatirmṛgāṇāṃ
Subhv śaṃsāspadaṃ tadapi na dvayameva manye 
Subhv tasya sphuratkarajavajraśirobhighāta
Subhv helānipātitamataṅgajajaṅgamādreḥ 
Subhv preṅkhanmayūkhanakhapātaśikhānikhāta
Subhv vikhyātavāraṇagaṇasya harerguhāyām 
Subhv kroṣṭā nikṛṣṭasaramāsutadṛṣṭinaṣṭa
Subhv dhārṣṭyo niviṣṭa iti kaṣṭamihādya dṛṣṭam 
Subhv mattebhakumbhadalanākulalolavalga
Subhv dantaḥ kvaṇatkarajavajraśikhābhighātaḥ 
Subhv kiṃ kesarī jagati mānanidhistṛṇena
Subhv prāṇātyayepi kurute svaśarīrayātrām 
Subhv viśvasya sthitaye dhanurdharatayā garjantamuccaiḥ pade
Subhv meghaṃ dantimadāntadurlalitadhīrmā siṃha lālaṅghiṣīḥ 
Subhv asmādvajravidāritakṣitibhṛto mā pāti varṣopalair
Subhv jhampālampaṭabhāvabhāvipatanāccintyoṅgabhaṅgaḥ svayam 
Subhv kharanakharanikhātottuṅgamātaṅgakumbha
Subhv sthalavigalitamuktālaṃkṛtakṣmātalasya 
Subhv harati hariṇavṛndaṃ kiṃ harervairamājau
Subhv militamapi samantādekakāryeṇa kṛtsnam 
Subhv anukṛtagaṇḍaśailamadamaṇḍitagaṇḍataṭa
Subhv bhramadalimaṇḍalīniviḍaguṃgumaghoṣajuṣaḥ 
Subhv dalayati helayaiva harirugrakarānkariṇas
Subhv trijagati teja eva guru no vikṛtākṛtitā 
Subhv śailaśreṇiguhāgṛheṣu nivasañjīvannijāḍambarair
Subhv avyājorjitavikramo mṛgapatirvīrendra mā kupyatām 
Subhv asmātkuñjarakumbhasaṃbhavavasāpānaikahevākino
Subhv yallabdhaṃ vyasanākulena manasā svenaiva taccintyatām 
Subhv kaśmīrāngatukāmasya mīraśāhākhyabhūpateḥ 
Subhv śāhābuddīnabhūmīndraḥ prāhiṇoditi lekhakam 
Subhv kimevamaviśāṅkitaḥ śiśukuraṅga lolakramaṃ
Subhv parikramitumīhase virama naiva śūnyaṃ vanam 
Subhv sthitotra gajayṅthanāthamathanocchalacchoṇita
Subhv cchaṭāpaṭalabhāsurotkaṭasaṭābharaḥ kesarī 
Subhv kaṭhoranakharāhatadviradakumbhapīṭhasthalī
Subhv luṭhadrudhirarañjitollalitakesaraḥ kesarī 
Subhv gabhīraravakātarāturatarāturavyāhṛtaiḥ
Subhv patanhariṇakaiḥ samaṃ samarabhūmikāṃ lajjate 
Subhv carata vṛṣabhā jālīmāṃsaṃ yathecchamabhīravaḥ
Subhv pibata nalinīkaccheṣvacchaṃ punarmahiṣāḥ payaḥ 
Subhv vahata kariṇo bhūyaḥ śobhāṃ madena kapolayor
Subhv asahanatayā dūrībhūto vidherta kesarī 
Subhv labdhā ḍambharamambare jaladharaṃ garjantamālokya yad
Subhv dūrāducchalitosi siṃha mahatāṃ tenaiva khinnaṃ manaḥ 
Subhv yattvāsārabhayena saṃprati darīsāṃmukhyamālambase
Subhv taddṛṣṭvaiva vayaṃ hriyā kimaparaṃ pātālamūlaṃ gatāḥ 
Subhv yasyānekamadāndhavāraṇaghaṭākumbhasthalībhedana
Subhv vyāpāraikavinodadurlalitayā kālogamallīlayā 
Subhv udgarjajjalabhāravāmanaghanaspardhī sa evādhunā
Subhv siṃhaḥ pañjarapātapuñjitatanurdhatte daśāmīdṛśīm 
Subhv kṣutkṣāmepi jarākṛśopi śithilaprāṇopi kaṣṭāṃ daśā
Subhv māpannopi vipannadhīdhṛtirapi prāṇeṣu naśyatsvapi 
Subhv darpādhmātakarīndrakumbhadalanapreṅkhannakhāgrāśaniḥ
Subhv kiṃ jīrṇaṃ tṛṇamatti mānamahatāmagresaraḥ kesarī 
Subhv nāsyocchrāyavatī tanurna daśanau no dīrghadīrghaḥ karaḥ
Subhv satyaṃ vāraṇa naiṣa kesariśiśustvāḍambaraiḥ spardhate 
Subhv tejobījamasahyamasya hṛdaye nyastaṃ purā vedhasā
Subhv tādṛktvādṛśameva yena sutarāṃ bhojyaṃ paśuṃ manyate 
Subhv mādyanmātaṅgakumbhasthalabahalavasāvāsanāvisragandha
Subhv vyāsaṅgavyaktamuktāphalaśakalalasatkesarālīkarālaḥ 
Subhv vyādhīvaidhavyavedhāḥ svabhujabalamadagrastatejasvidhāmā
Subhv vibhyatsāraṅgasārthaḥ satatamasahanaḥ kesarī kena dṛṣṭaḥ 
Subhv kaḥ kaḥ kutra na ghurghurāyitaghurīghoro ghuretsūkaraḥ
Subhv kaḥ kaḥ kaṃ kamalākaraṃ vikamalaṃ kartuṃ karī nodyataḥ 
Subhv ke ke kāni vanānyaraṇyamahiṣā nonmūlayeyuryataḥ
Subhv siṃhīsnehavilāsabaddhavasatiḥ pañcānano vartate 
Subhv ā bālyādapi yo vidāritamadonmattebhakumbhasthalī
Subhv sthālīmadhyakavoṣṇaraktarasavanmuktāpulākapriyaḥ 
Subhv hastastasya kathaṃ prasarpatu puraḥ kṛcchrepyavasthāntare
Subhv gartāvartavivartamānaśaśakaprāṇāpahāre hareḥ 
Subhv raktāktayannakharakoṭinibhādibhānāṃ
Subhv yūthāḥ palāśavanatopi palāyya jagmuḥ 
Subhv siṃhasya tasya jarato viṣamā daśā yad
Subhv gomāyavairavayavairapi nāsti vṛttiḥ 
Subhv parjanyaṃ prati garjataḥ pratinidhīnvindhyasya vātoddhatā
Subhv nambhodhīniva dhāvataḥ sarabhasaṃ hatvā raṇe vāraṇān 
Subhv vṛkṣādvṛkṣamupeyuṣolpavapuṣaḥ śākhāmṛgasyopari
Subhv kruddhaḥ sopi bhavānaho bata gataḥ pañcāsya hāsyāṃ daśām 
Subhv huṃkāraiḥ stanitānukāracaturairnyakkāramākārita
Subhv kṣauṇībhṛcchikharaśriyo gajaghaṭā nītvā madāṭopinīḥ 
Subhv siṃhaḥ saṃhatabhāvato daśadiśaḥ kliśyatsu durvāśitair
Subhv gomāyuṣvapi viśvaviśvaviditaprauḍhiḥ kimudyacchate 
Subhv karikalabha vimuñca lolatāṃ
Subhv cara vinayavratamānatānanaḥ 
Subhv mṛgapatinakhakoṭibhaṅguro
Subhv gururupari kṣamate na teṅkuśaḥ 
Subhv keliṃ kuruṣva paribhuṅkṣva saroruhāṇi
Subhv gāhasya śailataṭanirjhariṇīpayāṃsi 
Subhv bhāvānuraktakariṇīkaralālitāṅga
Subhv mātaṅga muñca mṛgarājaraṇābhilāṣam 
Subhv ucchṛṅkhalena nirapekṣatayonmadena
Subhv yenākulīkṛtamidaṃ kariṇā babhūva 
Subhv dattvā padaṃ śirasi hastipakārbhakeṇa
Subhv mandaḥ kathaṃ gamita eṣa vaśaṃ prasahya 
Subhv vindhyādrisānutarupuṣpapatatparāga
Subhv saṃpuñjapūjitakaraḥ kariyūthasevyaḥ 
Subhv yobhūtsa eva nṛnideśakaraḥ karīndro
Subhv jātaḥ kathaṃ kimathavā prabhuratra kālaḥ 
Subhv antaḥsamutthavirahānalatīvratāpa
Subhv saṃtāpitāṅga karipuṅgava muñca śokam 
Subhv dhātrā svahastalikhitāni lalāṭapaṭṭe
Subhv ko vākṣarāṇi parimārjayituṃ samarthaḥ 
Subhv bho bhoḥ karīndra divasāni kiyanti tāvad
Subhv asminmarau samativāhayakutracittvam 
Subhv revājalairnijakareṇukaraprayuktair
Subhv bhūyaḥ śamaṃ gamayitāsi nidāghakāle 
Subhv asmiñjaḍe jagati ko nu bṛhatpramāṇa
Subhv karṇaḥ karī nanu bhavedduritasya pātram 
Subhv ityāgataṃ tamapi yolinamunmamātha
Subhv mātaṅga eva kimataḥ paramucyatesau 
Subhv na gṛhṇāti grāsaṃ navakamalakiṃjalkini jale
Subhv na paṅkairāhlādaṃ vrajati bisabhaṅgārdhaśakalaiḥ 
Subhv lalantīṃ premārdrāmapi viṣahate nānyakariṇīṃ
Subhv smarandāvabhraṣṭāṃ hṛdayadayitāṃ vāraṇapatiḥ 
Subhv latāntānnādatte śaśiśakalaśītaṃ na ca jalaṃ
Subhv bhramadbhṛṅgāsaṅgāḥ pariharati kāntāḥ kamalinīḥ 
Subhv dadhadbhārākāraṃ karamapi karī jātaviraho
Subhv vitanvannucchvāsānkṣaṇamapi vatānte na ramate 
Subhv nadīvaprānbhittvā kisalayavadutpāṭya ca tarūn
Subhv madonmattāñjitvā karacaraṇadantaiḥ pratigajān 
Subhv jarāṃ prāpyānāryāṃ taruṇajanavidveṣajananīṃ
Subhv sa evāyaṃ nāgaḥ sahati kalabhebhyaḥ paribhavam 
Subhv varamiyamaṅkuśakṣatiralakṣitamāpatitā
Subhv vinayavidhitsayā śirasi te gajayūthapate 
Subhv na punarapaścimā karajavajraśikhābhihatiḥ
Subhv prasabhasamutthitasya niśitā vanakesariṇaḥ 
Subhv svādhīnāṃ pravihāya śailakaṭakaprānte kareṇa vane
Subhv yatte nāgarikājane nipatitaṃ sadbhāvaśūnye manaḥ 
Subhv tasyaitaddṛḍharajjubandhanavadhavyāpārakhedātmakaṃ
Subhv he mattadvipu karmaṇaḥ pariṇataṃ rāgānurūpaṃ phalam 
Subhv kvākāro girisannibhaḥ kva ca gatirvegena līlā ca sā
Subhv helākuḍmalitekṣaṇāḥ kva nu dṛśastadvā kva te bṛṃhitam 
Subhv vaprāghātarasaḥ kva te kva ca karaḥ kaṣṭaṃ yadevaṃvidhaṃ
Subhv tvāmāruhya śiśuḥ padā paravaśaṃ saṃcārayatyājñayā 
Subhv pādāghātavighūrṇitā vasumatī trāsālasāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ
Subhv paṅkāṅkāni sarāṃsi gaṇḍakaṣaṇakṣodakṣatāḥ śākhinaḥ 
Subhv prāpyedaṃ karipotakairvidhivaśācchārdūlaśūnyaṃ vanaṃ
Subhv tattannāma kṛtaṃ viśṛṅkhalatayā vaktuṃ na yatpāryate 
Subhv puṇḍrekṣūnapi bhakṣayanghṛtabhṛto māṃsaudanādīnapi
Subhv prāvṛṇvanvividhāḥ kuthā api vahannakṣatramālā api 
Subhv karṇe cāmaramālikāmapi dadhaddantī tathāpi smara
Subhv nvaindhyīnāṃ ghanasallakīvanabhuvāmāste sadā duḥkhitaḥ 
Subhv nīvāraprasavāgramuṣṭikavalairyo vardhitaḥ śaiśavo
Subhv pītaṃ yena sarojapattrapuṭake homāvaśeṣaṃ payam 
Subhv taṃ dṛṣṭvā madamantharālivalayavyālupragaṇḍaṃ gajaṃ
Subhv sotkaṇṭhaṃ sabhayaṃ ca paśyati muhurdūre sthitastāpasaḥ 
Subhv dante nyasya karaṃ pralambitaśirāḥ saṃmīlya netradvayaṃ
Subhv kiṃ tvaṃ vāraṇa tapyase gaṇikayā ko nāma no vañcitaḥ 
Subhv grāsaṃ śāntamanā gṛhāṇa satataṃ śokodhunā tyajyatāṃ
Subhv ye mattā avivekinaścaladhiyaste prāpnuvantyāpadam 
Subhv patyuryatkavalāvaśeṣapatitagrāsena vṛttiḥ kṛtā
Subhv pītaṃ yacca karāvagāhakaluṣaṃ tatpītaśeṣaṃ payaḥ 
Subhv prāṇānpūrvataraṃ vihāya tadidaṃ prāptaṃ kariṇyā phalaṃ
Subhv yadbandhārpaṇakātarasya kariṇaḥ kliṣṭaṃ na dṛṣṭaṃ mukham 
Subhv ghāsagrāsaṃ gṛhāṇa tyaja gajakalabha premabandhaṃ kariṇyāḥ
Subhv pāśagranthivraṇānāmabhimatamadhunā dehi paṅkānulepam 
Subhv dūrībhūtāstavaite śabaravaravadhūvibhramodbhrāntaramyā
Subhv revākulopakaṇṭadrumakusumarajo dhūsarā vindhyapādāḥ 
Subhv lāṅgūlacālanamadhaścaraṇāvapātaṃ
Subhv bhūmau nipatya vadanodaradarśanaṃ ca 
Subhv śvā piṇḍadasya kurute gajapuṅgavastu
Subhv dhīraṃ vilokayati cāṭuśataiśca bhuṅkte 
Subhv yadvindhyaḥ śikharī tadantarapi yatpīlupriyaḥ pippalaḥ
Subhv sotkaṇṭhā rabhasāgamādabhipatadreṇuḥ kareṇuśca yat 
Subhv tatkiṃ bhadratayā smaratyapi karī daivaṃ hi sarvaṃkaṣaṃ
Subhv tanmṛtyorapi duḥsahaṃ tu yadayaṃ mando dhuri sthāpitaḥ 
Subhv madhyevindhyamudūrminārmadanadīvātūlavātāvalī
Subhv heloddhūlitamallikākisalayairyo vṛddhimabhyāgataḥ 
Subhv soyaṃ daivavaśādvaśāvirahitaḥ śūtkārakārī karī
Subhv nirmajjadvajarajjupāśavivaśaḥ kaṣṭaṃ kimāceṣṭām 
Subhv he gandhakuñjara mahāgirikuñjarāji
Subhv madyāpi mā smara salīlanimīlitākṣaḥ 
Subhv muñcābhimānamadhunā bhaja vartamānaṃ
Subhv vakraṃ vidherupari śāsanamaṅkuśaṃ ca 
Subhv svacchasvādujalā vihāya sarito hartuṃ tṛṣaṃ duḥsahāṃ
Subhv mā matta dviradākṣi nikṣipa śaratkṛṣṭe taḍāgāmbuni 
Subhv pītesminsakalepi gacchati na te śāntiṃ pipāsā jale
Subhv grāmasyaikagateramuṣya niyataṃ syājjīvite saṃśayaḥ 
Subhv dūrvākuratṛṇāhārā dhanyāstāta vane mṛgāḥ 
Subhv vibhavonmattacittānāṃ na paśyanti mukhāni yat 
Subhv amṛtā vigataprāṇā sāntaḥśalyākṛtavraṇā 
Subhv abaddhā niścalevāste kūṭasaṃsthe mṛge mṛgī 
Subhv rajjvā diśaḥ pravitatāḥ salilaṃ viṣeṇa
Subhv pāśairmahī hutabhujā jvalitā vanāntāḥ 
Subhv vyādhāḥ padānyanusaranti gṛhītabāṇāḥ
Subhv kaṃ deśamāśrayati yūthapatirmṛgāṇām 
Subhv drutataramito gaccha prāṇaiḥ kuraṅga viyujyase
Subhv kimiti valitagrīvaṃ sthitvā muhurmuhurīkṣase 
Subhv vidadhati hatavyādhānāṃ te manāgapi nārdratāṃ
Subhv kaṭhinamanasāmeṣāmete vilocanavibhramāḥ 
Subhv sthalīnāṃ dagdhānāmupari mṛgatṛṣṇāmanusaraṃs
Subhv tṛṣārtaḥ sāraṅgo viramati na khinnepi manasi 
Subhv ajānānastattvaṃ na sa mṛgayatenyatra sarasī
Subhv mabhūmau pratyāśā na ca phalati vighnaṃ ca kurute 
Subhv he sāraṅga tṛṇānyaśāna salilaiḥ prāṇānpuṣāṇāthavā
Subhv yadvā syāḥ pavanāśanastadapi te sāviṣkṛti prāṇitam 
Subhv yeneyaṃ bhavatocchvasatkuvalayaprastāracārudyutir
Subhv dṛṣṭirvittamadoddhatākṣiṇi mukhe mūrkhasya nāyāsitā 
Subhv alpīyaḥskhalanena yatra patanaṃ kṛcchreṇa yatronnatir
Subhv dvāre vetralatāvitānagahane kaṣṭaḥ praveśakramaḥ 
Subhv he sāraṅga manoramā vanabhuvastyaktvā viśeṣārthinā
Subhv kiṃ bhūbhṛtkaṭakasthitivyasaninā vyarthaṃ khurāḥ śātitāḥ 
Subhv naitāstā malaya kānanabhuvaḥ svacchasravannirjharās
Subhv tṛṣṇā yāsu nivartate tanubhṛtāmālokamātrādapi 
Subhv rūkṣadhvāṅkṣaparigraho bharurayaṃ sphārībhavadbhrāntayas
Subhv tā etā mṛgatṛṣṇikā hariṇa he nedaṃ payo gamyatām 
Subhv tyaktaṃ janmavanaṃ tṛṇāṅkuravatī māteva muktā sthalī
Subhv visrambhasthitihetavo na gaṇitā bandhūpamāḥ pādapāḥ 
Subhv bālāpatyaviyogaduḥkhavidhurā nāpekṣitā sā mṛgī
Subhv mārgantaḥ padavīṃ tathāpyakaruṇā vyādhā na muñcantyamī 
Subhv chittvā pāśamapāsya kūṭaracanāṃ bhaṅktvā balādvāgurāṃ
Subhv paryastāgniśikhākalāpajaṭilānnirgatya dūraṃ vanāt 
Subhv vyādhānāṃ śaragocarādapi javenotplutya dhāvanmṛgaḥ
Subhv kūpāntaḥ patitaḥ karoti vidhure kiṃ vā vidhau pauruṣam 
Subhv svairī bhrāmyasi nātha kāmyasi paradvārāṇi nottāmyasi
Subhv nādyānāmanimittakopakuṭilālāpaṃ mukhaṃ paśyasi 
Subhv muñcasyekamapi kṣaṇaṃ prakaṭitapremāṃ ca na preyasīṃ
Subhv he sāraṅga tavātisundaramidaṃ kenopadiṣṭaṃ vratam 
Subhv svacchandaṃ hariṇena yā viharatā daivātsamāsāditā
Subhv bhaṅgaprasrutadugdhabindubisarā śālernavā mañjarī 
Subhv niḥśvāsānaladagdhakomalatṛṇaprakhyāpitāntarvyathas
Subhv tāmeva prativāsaraṃ muniriva dhyāyanvane śuṣyati 
Subhv sāraṅgo na latāgṛheṣu ramate no paṃsule bhūtale
Subhv no ramyāsu vanopakaṇṭhaharitacchāyāsu śītāsvapi 
Subhv tāmevāyatalocanāmanudinaṃ dhyāyanmuhuḥ preyasīṃ
Subhv śailendrodarakaṃdareṣu gatadhīḥ śṛṅgāriveṣaḥ sthitaḥ 
Subhv śṛṅgeṇāṅgaṃ mṛgāṇāṃ kaṣati paricayaprāptaye niḥspṛhāṇāṃ
Subhv mandasvacchandacārī pariharati bhayādālayaṃ yūthapasya 
Subhv dṛṣṭastiṣṭhatyalakṣyo jhagiti nipatitaistatkuraṅgīkaṭākṣaiḥ
Subhv sāraṅgo duḥkhamāste vidhuravidhivaśādanyayūthapraviṣṭaḥ 
Subhv ādāya māṃsamakhilaṃ stanavarjamaṅgān
Subhv māṃ muñca vāgurika yāhi kuru prasādam 
Subhv adyāpi ghāsakavalagrasanānabhijño
Subhv manmārgavīkṣaṇaparastanayo madīyaḥ 
Subhv puro revā pāre giriratidurārohaśikharaḥ
Subhv saraḥ savye vāme davadahanadāhavyatikaraḥ 
Subhv dhanuṣpāṇiḥ paścācchabarahatako dhāvatitarāṃ
Subhv na yātuṃ na sthātuṃ hariṇāśiśureṣa prabhavati 
Subhv kva krīḍati kva carati kva karoti vṛttiṃ
Subhv vāri kva nāma pibati svapiti kva nāma 
Subhv itthaṃ mṛgaṃ niraparādhamabādhamānaṃ
Subhv vyādhonudhāvati vadhāya dhanurdadhānaḥ 
Subhv candraḥ sudhāṃśurayamatrisuto dvijeśaḥ
Subhv puṇyairavāpi śaraṇāya mayeti toṣam 
Subhv mugdhaiṇaśāva bhaja mā tyaja pāpamenaṃ
Subhv mīnaṃ prabhujya sahasā kṛtameṣabhogam 
Subhv karabha yadi kadācitprabhramandaivayogān
Subhv madhukarakulatastvaṃ prāpayethā madhūni 
Subhv virama virama tebhyaḥ santi śaṣpāṇyaraṇye
Subhv prathamamukharasāste śoṣayantyeva paścāt 
Subhv vikacakumudaiḥ phullāmbhojaiḥ sarobhiralaṃkṛtāṃ
Subhv marakatamaṇiśyāmāṃ śaṣpairvihāya vanasthalīm 
Subhv smarati karabho yadvṛkṣāṇāṃ caranmarudhanvanāṃ
Subhv paricayaratiḥ sā durvārā na sā guṇavairitā 
Subhv karabhadayite yattatpītaṃ sudurlabhamekadā
Subhv madhu vanagataṃ tasyālābhe virauṣi kimutsukā 
Subhv kuru paricitaiḥ pīloḥ pattrairdhṛtiṃ marugocare
Subhv jagati sakale kasyāvāptiḥ sukhasya nirantarā 
Subhv karabhadayite yosau pīlustvayā madhulubdhayā
Subhv vyapagatadhanacchāyastyakto na sādaramīkṣitaḥ 
Subhv calakisalayaḥ sopīdānīṃ prarūḍhanavāṅkuraḥ
Subhv karabhadayitāvṛndairanyaiḥ sukhaṃ paribhujyate 
Subhv karabha kimidaṃ dīrghocchvāsaiḥ kṣiṇoṣi śarīrakaṃ
Subhv virama śaṭhe he kasyātyantaṃ sakhe sukhamāgatam 
Subhv cara kisalayaṃ svasthaḥ pīlorvimuñca madhuspṛhāṃ
Subhv punarapi bhavānkalyāṇānāṃ bhaviṣyati bhājanam 
Subhv karabha rabhasātkroṣṭuṃ vāñchasyaho śravaṇajvaraḥ
Subhv śaraṇamathavānṛjvī dīrghā tavaiva śirodharā 
Subhv pṛthugalabilāvṛttiśrāntoccariṣyati vāṅmukhā
Subhv diyati samaye ko jānīte bhaviṣyati kasya kim 
Subhv tathā saṃtuṣṭaḥ sañjalavṛṇaśamīpīlubadaraiś
Subhv caransvasthoraṇye karabhaśiśukaḥ śokarahitaḥ 
Subhv kṛto madhvāsvādapravaṇahadayo mugdhavidhinā
Subhv yathā nānyadbhuṅkte na pibati na śete na ramate 
Subhv yasyāsīnnavapīlupattrabadaragrāsopi saṃtuṣṭaye
Subhv dīrghādhvanyanugamyate na padavī yasya svayūthyairapi 
Subhv soyaṃ saṃprati yāti bālakarabhaḥ kṣīṇodyamaḥ kṣāmatāṃ
Subhv manye nūnamanena daivahatakenāsvāditaṃ bhrāmaram 
Subhv pīlūnāṃ hi phalaṃ kaṣāyarahitaṃ romanthayitvā marau
Subhv śākhāgraṃ yadakhādi cāru karabhīvaktrārpitaṃ premataḥ 
Subhv tatsmṛtvā karabhena khedavidhuraṃ dīrghaṃ tathā kūjitaṃ
Subhv prāṇānāmabhavattadeva sahasā prasthānatūryaṃ yathā 
Subhv kramelakaṃ nindati komalecchuḥ
Subhv kramelakaḥ kaṇṭakalampaṭastam 
Subhv prītau tayoriṣṭabhujoḥ samāyāṃ
Subhv madhyasthatā naikataropahāsaḥ 
Subhv eka eva khago mānī vane vasati cātakaḥ 
Subhv pipāsito vā mriyate yācate vā puraṃdaram 
Subhv ayi cakitamugdhacātaka marubhuvi dhāvasi mudhā kimudgrīvam 
Subhv grīṣme davāgnivalitastāpicchoyaṃ na vidyutvān 
Subhv pipāsurapyeva jalaṃ śikhaṇḍī
Subhv pratīkṣate prāṇasamāṃ pibantīm 
Subhv nūnaṃ priyāsnehanibaddhadṛṣṭiḥ
Subhv svalpaṃ payaḥ paśyati nimnagāsu 
Subhv atyunnativyasaninaḥ śirasodhunaiṣa
Subhv svasyaiva cātakaśiśuḥ praṇayaṃ vidhattām 
Subhv asyaitadicchati nahi pratatāsu dikṣu
Subhv tāḥ svacchaśītamadhurāḥ kva nu nāma nāpaḥ 
Subhv kekāḥ kalā vanabhuvastilakāyamāno
Subhv ramyaḥ kalāpamahimaiṣa śikhaṇḍinosya 
Subhv durlakṣaṇaṃ nanu vihāyasi vāyasādi
Subhv kṣuṇṇepyayaṃ caṭakatulyagatirna jātaḥ 
Subhv nīlābjapuñjarajasāruṇitānvimucya
Subhv svacchānsudhādhikarasānapi vārirāśīn 
Subhv yaccātakaḥ pibati vāridharodabindūn
Subhv manye tadānatibhayācchirasobhimānī 
Subhv divyāmbupānaniyamastava mohayetkaṃ
Subhv doṣopi saṃvṛtimatāṃ bhajate guṇatvam bhūmisthamambu yadi cātaka pātumiccheḥ
Subhv kaṇṭhavraṇaṃ prakaṭayestadayogyatāṃ ca 
Subhv divyāmbupānaniyamastava mohayetkaṃ
Subhv doṣopi saṃvṛtimatāṃ bhajate guṇatvam 
Subhv kiṃ naiva santi navatāmarasāvataṃsā
Subhv haṃsāvalīvalayino jalasanniveśāḥ 
Subhv kopi graho gururayaṃ bata cātakasya
Subhv pauraṃdarīṃ yadabhivāñchati vāridhārām 
Subhv kiṃ dūreṇa payodharā upari kiṃ nānye raṭantaḥ śrutā
Subhv nindyāḥ pāpatayā svakukṣiṣu gatāḥ kiṃ nāma pakṣāḥ kṣayam 
Subhv ramyaṃ vā gagane na kiṃ viharaṇaṃ kiṃ tūgrakākāvalī
Subhv paryāyapratipattilāghavabhayādbhūmau sthitā barhiṇaḥ 
Subhv no tāṇḍavena nayanāmṛtanirjhareṇa
Subhv kekāraveṇa na ca karṇarasāyanena 
Subhv barheṇa cāpi suracāparucā tavāya
Subhv moturna tuṣyati śikhinvadhamantareṇa 
Subhv cātaka tāta kiyadbhavatā pātakamatulamakāri 
Subhv navajaladādapi cañcupuṭe yattava na patati vāri 
Subhv jalakaṇavitaraṇarahitaḥ prakaṭitadhavalitaveṣaḥ 
Subhv cātaka raṭasi vṛthā kiṃ jaladaḥ śārada eṣaḥ 
Subhv santi kūpāḥ sphuradrūpāḥ paritaḥ saritaḥ śubhāḥ 
Subhv tathāpi cātakasyaikaḥ phalado jaladodayaḥ 
Subhv kekānibhāddhaṭayase paṭucāṭukāni
Subhv cañcatkalāpamapi nṛtyasi rañjanāya 
Subhv he cātaka prayatase jaladaṃ pratītthaṃ
Subhv binduṃ jalasya labhase na ca lajjase ca 
Subhv vāhatvamīśvarasutasya vidhāya barhin
Subhv pramlāyitaḥ sa nijapakṣakalāpa eva 
Subhv nārādhitaḥ sa bhavatā puruṣottamaḥ kiṃ
Subhv yaste tṛṣaṃ praśamayetkacameghavarṣaiḥ 
Subhv vasatotiśayaprītyā mānasocitasaṃsthiteḥ 
Subhv palvalāmbhasi haṃsasya haṃsataiva vikalpyate 
Subhv pibanti madhu padmebhyo bhṛṅgāḥ kesaradhūsarāḥ 
Subhv haṃsāḥ śaivālamaśnanti dhigdaivamasamañjasam 
Subhv yadi nāma daivayogājjagadasarojaṃ kadācidapi jātam 
Subhv avakaranikaraṃ vikirati tatkiṃ kṛkavākuriva haṃsaḥ 
Subhv kaṭu raṭati nikaṭarvatī vācāṭaṣṭiṭṭibhaḥ paṭuryatra 
Subhv apasaraṇameva śaraṇaṃ maunaṃ vā tatra haṃsasya 
Subhv astu yadyapi sarvatra nīraṃ nīrajamaṇḍitam 
Subhv ramate na marālasya mānasaṃ mānasaṃ vinā 
Subhv kṣudhitopi padmakhaṇḍe jahāti rajasāvṛtaṃ hi kiṃjalkam 
Subhv guṇini kṛtapakṣapāto bisaṃ tu bahu manyate haṃsaḥ 
Subhv taralayasi dṛśaṃ kimutsukā
Subhv makulaṣamānasavāsalālite 
Subhv avatara kalahaṃsi vāpikāṃ
Subhv punarapi yāsyasi paṅkajālayam 
Subhv bhṛṅgāṅganājanamanoharahārigīta
Subhv rājīvareṇukraṇakīrṇapaśaṅgatoyām 
Subhv ramyāṃ himācalanadīṃ pravihāya haṃsa
Subhv he he hatāśa vada kāṃ diśamutsukosi 
Subhv he haṃsa melitapayaḥsalilaṃ vivektuṃ
Subhv śaktasya saṃprati matiḥ kva nu tedya yātā 
Subhv kāsāravāriṇi kalāṃ patitāṃ yadindo
Subhv rādātumicchasi bisāṅkuravāñchayā tvam 
Subhv śītāṃśuśekharaśiroruhasaṃśritāni
Subhv puṇyāni pāvitajaganti manoramāṇi 
Subhv bhrāntvā ciraṃ surasaritsalilāni daivāl
Subhv labdhāni hātumiha vāñchasi nāsi haṃsaḥ 
Subhv sthitvā ciraṃ nabhasi niścalatārakeṇa
Subhv mātaṅgasaṅgakaluṣāṃ nalinīṃ nirīkṣya 
Subhv utpannamanyuparighargharaniḥsvanena
Subhv haṃsena sāśru parivṛtya gataṃ na līnam 
Subhv yenojjhitaṃ sahacarīvadanopanītaṃ
Subhv ramyaṃ mṛṇālaśakalaṃ himaśaṅkhaśubhram 
Subhv soyaṃ khago hatavidhe tava ceṣṭitena
Subhv śevālanālalavalampaṭatāṃ vidhatte 
Subhv raṭasi kaṭu kimuccairvāyasa spardhayā me
Subhv vihagahataka viṣṭhāraktavaktrāntarālaḥ 
Subhv vitatadhavalapakṣākṣepavikṣobhitāmbhāḥ
Subhv kamalavanavihārī sārasohaṃ na kākaḥ 
Subhv haṃsodhvagaḥ śramamapohayituṃ dinānte
Subhv kāraṇḍakākabakabhāsavanaṃ praviṣṭaḥ 
Subhv mūkoyamityupahasanti lunanti pakṣān
Subhv nīcāśrayo hi mahatāmavamānabhūmiḥ 
Subhv kva kaṭhinamaho pīloḥ pattraṃ mṛduḥ kva bisāṅkuraḥ
Subhv kva kaṭu lavaṇaṃ kaupaṃ cāmbhaḥ kva tāmarasāsavaḥ 
Subhv kva kusumarajo hṛdyaṃ rūkṣāḥ kva coṣarapāṃsavaḥ
Subhv kva maruviṣayo dhvāṅkṣakṣetraṃ kva haṃsa bhavādṛśāḥ 
Subhv bho rājahaṃsa kimiti tvamihāgatosi
Subhv yosau bakaḥ sa iha haṃsa iti pratītaḥ 
Subhv tadgamyatāṃ tvaritameva tataḥ prabhāte
Subhv yāvadvadanti baka eṣa na mūḍhalokāḥ 
Subhv aye vāpīhaṃsā nijavasatisaṃkocapiśunaṃ
Subhv karudhvaṃ mā ceto viyati bahato vīkṣya vihagān 
Subhv amī te sāraṅgā bhuvanamahanīyavratabhṛto
Subhv nirīhāṇāmeṣāṃ tṛṇamiva bhavantyambunidhayaḥ 
Subhv tarau tīrodbhūte kvacidapi dalācchāditatanuḥ
Subhv pataddhārāsārāṃ gamaya viṣamāṃ prāvṛṣamimām 
Subhv nivṛttāyāṃ tvasyāṃ sarasi sarasotphullanaline
Subhv sa eva tvaṃ haṃsaḥ punarapi vilāsāsta iha te 
Subhv gataṃ tadgāmbhīryaṃ jalamapi vṛtaṃ jālakaśataiḥ
Subhv sakhe haṃsottiṣṭha prathamamamuto dagdhasarasaḥ 
Subhv sa yāvatpaṅkāmbhaḥkaluṣitavapurbhūrivilapan
Subhv na kāko vācāṭaścaraṇayugalaṃ mūrdhni kurute 
Subhv spṛśati na bisaṃ cañcvā bhūyastayā saha khaṇḍitaṃ
Subhv pibati na jalaṃ yāti svaptuṃ na śevalajālakam 
Subhv kamalakalikābhaṅgakrīḍāṃ karoti na sārasaḥ
Subhv kvaṇati karuṇaṃ śokagrastaḥ priyāvirahākulaḥ 
Subhv sarasi bahuśastārāchāyāṃ daśanparivañcataḥ
Subhv kumuda viṭapānveṣī haṃso niśāsvavicakṣaṇaḥ 
Subhv daśati na punastārāśaṅkī divāpi sitotpalaṃ
Subhv kuhakacakito lokaḥ satyepyapāyamapekṣate 
Subhv muktābhāni payāṃsi bhaṅgavilasaddugdhā bisagranthayaḥ
Subhv sphītāstāmarasāsavā viharaṇakrīḍāsahaṃ saikatam 
Subhv santyeva pratideśamatraviṣame he haṃsa paṅkāṅkite
Subhv dhṛṣṭoktruṣṭabake jaratsarasi te koyaṃ nivāsagrahaḥ 
Subhv āpūryeta punaḥ sphuracchapharikāsārormibhirvāribhir
Subhv bhūyopi pravibhajyamānanalinaṃ paśyema toyāśayam 
Subhv ityāśāśatatantubaddhahṛdayo naktaṃdinaṃ dīnadhīḥ
Subhv śuṣyatyātapaśoṣitasya sarasastīre jaratsārasaḥ 
Subhv tāvaddolitapaṅkajacyutarajaḥpiṅkāṅgarāgojjvalp
Subhv yaḥ śṛṇvankalakūjitaṃ madhulihāṃ saṃjātaharṣotsavaḥ 
Subhv kāntācañcupuṭāpavarjitabisagrāsagrahepyakṣamaḥ
Subhv soyaṃ saṃprati haṃsako marugataḥ kaṣṭaṃ tṛṇaṃ vāñchati 
Subhv yāṃ smṛtvā sahasaiva mānasasarastyaktvā viśeṣārthinas
Subhv tāmevotsukacetasaḥ kamalinīṃ dṛṣṭvā bakādhyāsitām 
Subhv līyante vigatābhimānalaghavastatraiva bhūyopi ye
Subhv haṃsāste na bhavanti haṃsadhavalāḥ prāyo bakā eva te 
Subhv yāmāliṅgya bakā raṭanti kaṭukaṃ dīrghocchvasatkaṃdharā
Subhv yasyāmaṃsataṭāvaghaṭṭitajalaṃ valgantyamī madgavaḥ 
Subhv yā śaśvanmalinātmakairapi bakairnaktaṃdinaṃ sevyate
Subhv sā haṃsena manasvinā kamalinī yuktaṃ yadi tyajyate 
Subhv rūpaṃ hāri manoharā sahacarī pānāya pādmaṃ madhu
Subhv krīḍā cāpsu saroruheṣu vasatisteṣāṃ rajo maṇḍanam 
Subhv vṛttiḥ sādhumatā bisena sahṛdaścārusvanāḥ ṣaṭpadāḥ
Subhv sevādainyavimānanāvirahito haṃsaḥ sukhaṃ jīvati 
Subhv matsyā api hi jānanti kṣīranīravivecanam 
Subhv prasiddhaṃ rājahaṃsānāṃ yaśaḥ puṇyairavāpyate 
Subhv kruddholūkanakhaprapātavigalatpakṣā api svāśrayaṃ
Subhv ye nojjhanti purīṣapuṣṭavapuṣastekecidanye dvijāḥ 
Subhv ye tu svargataraṅgiṇībisalatāleśena saṃvardhitā
Subhv gaṅgānīramapi tyajanti kaluṣaṃ te rājahaṃsāḥ kutaḥ 
Subhv samudgirasi vācaḥ kiṃ puṃskokila sukomalāḥ 
Subhv śvabhresmiñjaḍapāṣāṇagurunirghoṣabhairave 
Subhv kākaiḥ saha vivṛddhasya kokilasya kalā giraḥ 
Subhv khalasaṅgepi naiṣṭhuryaṃ kalyāṇaprakṛteḥ kutaḥ 
Subhv śrotrotsavaṃ tava kalaṃ kalakaṇṭha kotra
Subhv nādaṃ śṛṇoti rativigrahasaṃdhidūtam 
Subhv dāvāgnidagdhaghanapādapakoṭarānta
Subhv rāvirbhavatkaṭuravāsu vanasthalīṣu 
Subhv mūkīmūya tameva kokila madhuṃ bandhuṃ pratīkṣasva he
Subhv helollāsitamālatīparimalāmodānukūlānilam 
Subhv yatraitāstava sūktayaḥ saphalatāmāyāntyamī tūllasat
Subhv pāṃsūttambhabhṛto nidāghadivasāḥ saṃtāpasaṃdhāyinaḥ 
Subhv bhrātaḥ kokilakūjitairalamalaṃ nārghanti yasmādguṇās
Subhv tūṣṇīmāḥsva viśīrṇaparṇanicayacchannaḥ kvacitkoṭare 
Subhv udyānadrumavāṭikākaṭuraṭatkākāvalīṃsakulaḥ
Subhv kāloyaṃ śiśirasya saṃprati sakhe nāyaṃ vasantotsavaḥ 
Subhv kvacijjhillīnādaḥ kvacidatulakākolakalahaḥ
Subhv kvacitkaṅkārāvaḥ kvacidapi kapīnāṃ kalakalaḥ 
Subhv kvaciddhoraḥ pherudhvanirayamaho daivaghaṭanā
Subhv kathaṃkāraṃ tāraṃ kvaṇatu cakitaḥ kokilayuvā 
Subhv ketakīkusumaṃ bhṛṅgaḥ pīḍyamānopi sevate 
Subhv doṣāḥ kiṃ nāma kurvanti guṇāpahṛtacetasaḥ 
Subhv kṛtvāpi koṣapānaṃ bhramarayuvā purata eva kamalinyāḥ 
Subhv abhilaṣati bakulakalikāṃ madhulihi maline kutaḥ satyam 
Subhv madanamavalokya niṣphalamanityatāmapi ca bandhujīvānām 
Subhv gurumupagamya bhramaraḥ saṃprati jāto japāsaktaḥ 
Subhv bhramara bhramatā digantarāṇi
Subhv kvacidāsāditamīkṣitaṃ śrutaṃ vā 
Subhv vada satyamapāsya pakṣapātaṃ
Subhv yadi jātīkusumānukāri puṣpam 
Subhv kamalaṃ bhavanaṃ rajoṅgarāgo
Subhv madhu pānaṃ madhurāḥ priyāpralāpāḥ 
Subhv śayanaṃ mṛdu kesaropadhānaṃ
Subhv bhramarasyāmbhasi kā na rājalīlā 
Subhv patitamutpatitaṃ sthitamakriyaṃ
Subhv sakaruṇaṃ kvaṇitaṃ gatamāgatam 
Subhv kamalinīmalinā tuhināhatāṃ
Subhv nahi tadasti vilokya na yatkṛtam 
Subhv kamalinīmalinī dayitaṃ vinā
Subhv na sahate saha tena niṣevitām 
Subhv tamadhunā madhunā nihitaṃ hṛdi
Subhv smarati sā ratisāramaharniśam 
Subhv madaṃ na lipseta śilīmukho yadi
Subhv dvipānna karṇāgranipātamāpnuyāt 
Subhv paropasarpī sukhaleśalipsayā
Subhv naro bhavatyeva parābhavāspadam 
Subhv madhukara bahuśastvayā nirastāḥ
Subhv kusumalatāstṛṇāvatsupuṣpitāgrāḥ 
Subhv phalamanubhava kaṇṭakāvṛtābhyas
Subhv tadidamapatrapa ketakīlatābhyaḥ 
Subhv pulleṣu yaḥ kamalinīkamalodareṣu
Subhv cūteṣu yo vilasitaḥ kalikāntarasthaḥ 
Subhv paśyādya tasya madhupasya śaradvyapāye
Subhv kṛcchreṇa veṇuvivare divasāḥ prayānti 
Subhv puṣpāsavaṃ surabhi gandhirajoṅgarāgaḥ
Subhv pītvā latāsu madhupaḥ kamale niṣaṇṇaḥ 
Subhv baddhodhunā śaśikaraiḥ karuṇaṃ virauti
Subhv saṃtoṣahīnamiha kaṃ na bhajantyanarthāḥ 
Subhv anyāsu tāvadupamardasahāsu bhṛṅga
Subhv lolaṃ vinodaya manaḥ sumanolatāsu 
Subhv nugdhānanāmarajasaṃ kalikāmakāle
Subhv bālāṃ kadarthayasi kiṃ navamālikāyāḥ 
Subhv erāvaṇānanamadāmbukaṇāvapāta
Subhv saṃsaktatāmarasareṇupiśaṅgitāṅgaḥ 
Subhv caṇḍānilāhatatuṣāraviśīrṇapakṣaḥ
Subhv kṣīṇaḥ kṣitau madhukaro vivaśotra śete 
Subhv sotkaḥ paribhramasi kiṃ vyavapātidhairyaḥ
Subhv kūjandvirepha karuṇaṃ kusumāsavārthī 
Subhv anyāsu pādapalatāsu dhṛtiṃ badhāna
Subhv bhagnā hi sā kusumitā sahakāravallī 
Subhv svāmodavāsitasamagradigantarālā
Subhv raktā manoharamukhā sukumāramūrtiḥ 
Subhv sevyā sarojakalikā tu yadaiva jātā
Subhv nītastadaiva vidhinā madhuponyadeśam 
Subhv jātyujjvale madhurakomalavāgnilāsau
Subhv dvau puṣkare madhukarau yugapatpraviṣṭau 
Subhv ekastayormadhubharākulapūrṇadehaḥ
Subhv kaṣṭe vidhau na rajasāpi yuto dvitīyaḥ 
Subhv madhukaragaṇaścūtaṃ tyaktvā gato navamālikāṃ
Subhv punarapi gato raktāśokaṃ kadambataruṃ tataḥ 
Subhv tadapi suciraṃ sthitvā tebhyaḥ prayāti saroruhaṃ
Subhv paricitaguṇadveṣī loko navaṃ navamīhate 
Subhv likhitakamale saundaryeṇa prakāmahṛtātmanā
Subhv kimiva na kṛtaṃ tatra bhrāntvā madhuspṛhayālinā 
Subhv adhigatarasaḥ sobhūttasmānmanāgapi nālpadhīr
Subhv dhuri tu likhitastṛṣṇāndhānāṃ janena vivekinā 
Subhv bhramati bakule mandaṃ kunde na vindati nirvṛtiṃ
Subhv prakṛtisurabhau raktāśoke na yāti viśokatām 
Subhv surabhikusumāmodotkaṇṭhāpanītamanā vane
Subhv vahati tanutāmaṅge bhṛṅgaḥ smarannavamālikām 
Subhv spṛśati śanakaiścumbannaṅgaiḥ karoti nipīḍanaṃ
Subhv caraṇapatanaṃ mudrābhedaṃ vidhātumapīhate 
Subhv samayamucitaṃ cittotsukyātpratīkṣitumakṣamo
Subhv madhukarayuvā puṇyairlabdhvā navāṃ navamālikām 
Subhv himotsannāṃ dṛṣṭvā hatakamalanālāṃ kamalinīṃ
Subhv dvirephāḥ saṃvṛttāḥ sapadi gajagaṇḍapraṇayinaḥ 
Subhv aho dhigbhūtānāṃ prakṛtiriyamapratyayakarī
Subhv na kaścitkṣīṇārthe prathamaguṇagandhaṃ gaṇayati 
Subhv kimāmodabhrāntyā bhramasi suciraṃ bhṛṅga nanu he
Subhv na jānīṣe tattvaṃ pratapatitarāṃ grīṣmasamayaḥ 
Subhv sthitaṃ śūnyaṃ puṣpaiḥ prakaṭaviṭapaṃ paśya vipinaṃ
Subhv gataḥ gaurabhyāḍhyaḥ prakṛtisubhagaścaitravibhavaḥ 
Subhv kenāghrātamudāramasya kusumaṃ kaiścumbitaṃ kesaraṃ
Subhv pītaḥ kena rasosya kena rajasā codvellitaṃ kena vā 
Subhv he he mugdhamadhuvrata vraja javādanyāṃstarūnpuṣpitā
Subhv nuttāletra vṛthaiva pippalatarau kiṃ kiṃcidāsādyate 
Subhv pratyagrotra yathāsukhaṃ madhurasaḥ pātavya ityutsukas
Subhv tṛṣṇāvibhramavipralabdhahrdayastattvāvabodhaṃ vinā 
Subhv nirviṇṇopyaphalaśramo na viramatyālekhyapadmākare
Subhv durbuddhirvyasanī tathāpi madhupastṛṣṇāśayodbhrāmyati 
Subhv yasyāḥ saṃgamavāñchayā na gaṇitā vāpyo vinidrotpalā
Subhv yāmāliṅgya samutsukena manasā yātaḥ parāṃ nirvṛtim 
Subhv bhagnāṃ tāmavalokya candanalatāṃ bhṛṅgeṇa yajjīvyate
Subhv dhairyaṃ nāma tadastu tasya na punaḥ snehānurūpaṃ kṛtam 
Subhv yenāmodini kesarasya mukule pītaṃ madhu svecchayā
Subhv nītā yena niśā śaśāṅkadhavalā padmodare śārade 
Subhv bhrāntaṃ yena madapravāhamaline guṇḍasthale dantināṃ
Subhv soyaṃ bhṛṅgayuvā karīraviṭape badhnātu tuṣṭiṃ kutaḥ 
Subhv mā bhūnnāma sahāmunaiva nidhanaṃ daivātkathaṃcitpunas
Subhv tṛṣṇā vā hatajīvite yadi tadā kiṃ puṣpaśūnyaṃ jagat 
Subhv yenaivonmathitaḥ sa eva dayitaḥ padmākaro nirdayaṃ
Subhv dānāmbhaḥspṛhayānuyātyaliraho lolastameva dvipam 
Subhv sopūrvo rasanāviparyayavidhistatkarṇayoścāpalaṃ
Subhv dṛṣṭiḥ sā madavismṛtasvaparadikkiṃ bhūyasoktena vā 
Subhv sarvaṃ niścitavānasi bhramara he yadvāraṇodyāpyasā
Subhv vantaḥśūnyakaro niṣevyata iti bhrātaḥ ka eṣa grahaḥ 
Subhv re re bhṛṅga madāndhavāraṇacalatkarṇānilāndolana
Subhv kleśaklāntatano mudhaiva bhavatā duḥkhaṃ kimityāsyate 
Subhv utkūjatsamadadvirephavalayapyāluptakośaśriyaḥ
Subhv sāmodāḥ prakaṭāśayāḥ pratipadaṃ santyeva padmākarāḥ 
Subhv gandhāḍhyāṃ navamālikāṃ madhukarastyaktvā gato yūthikāṃ
Subhv tāṃ tyaktvāpi gataḥ sa candanataruṃ tasmātsarojaṃ gataḥ 
Subhv baddhastatra niśākareṇa suciraṃ krandatyasau mandadhīḥ
Subhv saṃtoṣeṇa vinā parābhavaśataṃ prāpnoti lubdho janaḥ 
Subhv rātrirgamiṣyati bhaviṣyati suprabhātaṃ
Subhv bhāsvānudeṣyati hasiṣyati padminī ca 
Subhv evaṃ vicintayati koṣagate dvirephe
Subhv hā hanta hanta nalinīṃ gaja unmamātha 
Subhv bhramanvanānte vanamañjarīṣu
Subhv na ṣaṭpado gandhaphalīmajighrat 
Subhv sā kiṃ na ramyā sa ca kiṃ na rantā
Subhv balīyasī kevalamīśvarecchā 
Subhv aṅke vṛddhimupāgataṃ śiśutayā sarvāṅgamāliṅgitaṃ
Subhv matsyaḥ śrīparirambhanirbharataravyākośakoṣonmukhaiḥ 
Subhv āśāptaiḥ paripīyamānamaniśaṃ niḥspandamindindirair
Subhv dūrādeva nimeṣaśūnyanayanaḥ padmaṃ samudvīkṣate 
Subhv jīvato nigiranmatsyānmunivaddṛśyate bakaḥ 
Subhv mṛnānapi na gṛdhrastu dhigākāramunīndratām 
Subhv nāleneva sthitvā pādenaikena kuñcitagrīvam 
Subhv janayati kumudabhrāntiṃ vṛddhabako bālamatsyānām 
Subhv eṣa bakaḥ sahasaiva vipannaḥ
Subhv śādyamaho kva nu tadgatamasya 
Subhv sādhu kṛtāntaka kaścidapi tvāṃ
Subhv vañcayitum na kutopi samarthaḥ 
Subhv nijakulocitaceṣṭitamātmano
Subhv yadapahāya yiyāsasi haṃsatām 
Subhv baka cara vratameva tathāpi te
Subhv phalati tattadidaṃ yatatāṃ nṛṇām 
Subhv na kolilānāmiva mañcu kūjitaṃ
Subhv na kabdhalāsyāni gatāni haṃsavat 
Subhv na barhiṇānāmiva citrapakṣatā
Subhv guṇastathāpyasti bake bakavratam 
Subhv tadvedagdhyaṃ samuditapayastoyatattvaṃ vivektu
Subhv mālāpāste sa ca mṛdupadanyāsahṛdyo vilāsaḥ 
Subhv āstāṃ tāvadbaka yadi tathā vetsi kiṃcidicchlathāśaṃ
Subhv tūṣṇīmevāsitumayi sakhe tvaṃ kathaṃ me na haṃsaḥ 
Subhv kastvaṃ lohitalocanāsyacaraṇo haṃsaḥ kuto mānasāt
Subhv kiṃ tatrāsti suvarṇapaṅkajavanānyambhaḥ sudhāsaṃnibham 
Subhv muktāśuktirathāsti śaṅkhanicayo vaidūryarohāḥ kvacic
Subhv chambūkāḥ kimu santi neti ca bakairākarṇya hīhīkṛtam 
Subhv tulyavarṇacchadaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ kokilaiḥ saha saṃgataḥ 
Subhv kena vijñāyate kākaḥ svayaṃ yadi na bhāṣate 
Subhv ātmarutādapi virutaṃ kurvāṇāḥ spardhayā saha mayūraiḥ 
Subhv kiṃ jānanti varākāḥ kākāḥ kekāravānkartum 
Subhv kṛṣṇaṃ vapurvahatu cumbatu satphalāni
Subhv ramyeṣu saṃcaratu cūtavanāntareṣu 
Subhv puṃskokilasya caritāni karotu nāma
Subhv kākaḥ kila dhvanividhau nanu kāka eva 
Subhv saṃprāpya kokilakulaiḥ kamanīyakāntiḥ
Subhv kāntasvarairapi balātkhalu saṃnikarṣam 
Subhv vaidhuryabhāji hatavedhasi kiṃ varākaḥ
Subhv kākaḥ karotvanukṛtiṃ na yayau yadeṣām 
Subhv iyaṃ pallī bhillairanucitasamārambharasikaiḥ
Subhv samantādākrāntā viṣaviṣamabāṇapraṇayibhiḥ 
Subhv tarorasya skandhe gamaya samayaṃ kīra nibhṛtaṃ
Subhv na vāṇī kalyāṇī tadihamukhamudraiva śaraṇam 
Subhv kaati mukhagṛhītaṃ bhuktaśeṣaṃ purīṣaṃ
Subhv vilikhati caraṇāgrairdevatānāṃ śirāṃsi 
Subhv vrajati ca hatamānaḥ sādhumūrdhasvaśaṅkaḥ
Subhv kimiva na kurute khaṃ prāpya kāko varākaḥ 
Subhv daurbhāgyaṃ vacasāṃ tanormalinatā ceṣṭāsvaho cāpalaṃ
Subhv śaṅkāyāstadupajñataiva viditā vṛttistvavācyaiva sā 
Subhv itthaṃ dṛṣkṛtaśākhinaḥ phalamiva sphītaṃ tathāpyāturaḥ
Subhv kākaḥ kokilalāñchanacchavirucā kaṣṭaṃ muhurmūrchati 
Subhv nṛtyantaḥ śikhino manoharamamī śravyaṃ paṭhantaḥ śukā
Subhv vīkṣyante na ta eva khalviha ruṣā vāryanta evāthavā 
Subhv pānthastrīgṛhamiṣṭalābhakathanāllabdhānvayenāmunā
Subhv saṃpratyetadanargalaṃ balibhujā māyāvinā bhujyate 
Subhv re re dhvāṅkṣa virūkṣatāstu vacasaḥ kāṇākṣitā kṣamyate
Subhv laulyaṃ nāma taveti kātra gaṇanā bhāṇḍyaṃ vibhūṣaiva te 
Subhv sarvaṃ soḍhamidaṃ svabhāvavihitaṃ vahnerivauṣṇyaṃ hi te
Subhv yattvevaṃ viguṇasya kāpi bhavato grīvā na tatsahyate 
Subhv kākaḥ kokilamunnamayya kurute cūte phalāsvādanaṃ
Subhv bhuṅkte rājaśukaṃ nivārya kuraraḥ krīḍāparo dāḍimam 
Subhv dhūko barhiṇamasya śākhiśikhare śete sajāniḥ sukhaṃ
Subhv hā jātaṃ viparītamadya vipine śyene parokṣaṃ gate 
Subhv kiṃ kekīva śikhaṇḍamaṇḍitatanuḥ kiṃ kīravatpāṭhakaḥ
Subhv kiṃ puṃskokilavatsvanena madhuraḥ kiṃ haṃsavatsadgatiḥ 
Subhv kiṃ sāmānyaśakuntaśāvaka iva krīḍāvinodākaraḥ
Subhv kākaḥ kena guṇena kāñcanamaye vyāpāritaḥ pañjare 
Subhv utpattirmarutāṃ prabhoryugadine prakhyāpyaviśvotsave
Subhv puṇyāhaśrutiṣu prasiddhiradhikā pūrṇaṃ vayaḥ pauruṣam 
Subhv kākutsthena samaṃ sapatnakalaho daivajñatā tādṛśī
Subhv kākastena guṇena kāñcanamaye vyāpāritaḥ pañjare 
Subhv ādyaḥ praveśasamayaḥ sa kaleryugasya
Subhv prāptastiraskṛtabahūdakahaṃsasārthaḥ 
Subhv āhūye sādaratayā tapasontimohni
Subhv kāṇo dvijaḥ pratigṛhaṃ bata yatra pūjyaḥ 
Subhv sūrydanyatra yaccandrepyarthasaṃsparśi tatkṛtam 
Subhv khadyota iti kīṭasya nāma tuṣṭena kenacit 
Subhv ghanasaṃtamasamalīmasadaśadiśi niśi yadvirājasi tadanyat 
Subhv kīṭamaṇe dinamadhunā tarāṇikarāntaritacārusitakiraṇam 
Subhv jarjaratṛṇāgramadahansarṣapakaṇamaprakāyannūnam 
Subhv kīṭatvamātmatantraḥ khadyotaḥ khyāpayanbhāti 
Subhv bhrājiṣṇavo nabhasi bhūrihṛtāndhakāra
Subhv svalpaprabhāḥ svatanumātranibaddhabhāsaḥ 
Subhv khadyotakāḥ prakaṭatīvraguruprabhāvās
Subhv tāvanna saptaturagaḥ samudeti yāvat 
Subhv yuṣmādṛśaḥ kṛpaṇakāḥ krimayopi yasyāṃ
Subhv bhānti sma saṃtamasamayyagamanniśāsau 
Subhv sūryāṃśudīpradaśadigdivasodhunāyaṃ
Subhv bhātyatra nendurapi kīṭamaṇe kimu tvam 
Subhv induḥ prayāsyati vinaṅkṣyati tārakaśrīḥ
Subhv sthāsyanti līḍhatimirā na maṇipradīpāḥ 
Subhv andhaṃ samagramapi kīṭamaṇe bhaviṣya
Subhv dunmeṣameṣyati bhavāniti dūrametat 
Subhv sattvāntaḥ sphuritāya vā kṛtaguṇādyāropatucchāya vā
Subhv tasmai kātaramohanāya mahaso leśāya mā svasti bhūt 
Subhv yacchāyāsphuraṇāruṇena khacatā khadyotanāmnāmunā
Subhv kīṭenāhitayāpi jaṅgamamaṇibhrāntyā viḍambyāmahe 
Subhv pratyagraiḥ parṇanicayaistaruryaireva śobhitaḥ 
Subhv jahāti jīrṇāṃstāneva kiṃ vā citraṃ kujanmanaḥ 
Subhv yathāpallavapuṣpāḍhyā yathāpuṣpaphalarddhayaḥ 
Subhv yathāphalarddhisvārohā hā mātaḥ kvāgamandrumāḥ 
Subhv sādhveva tadvidhāvasya vedhāḥ kliṣṭo na yanmudhā 
Subhv svarūpānanurūpeṇa candanasya phalena kim 
Subhv mayā badaralubdhena vṛkṣāṇāmanabhijñayā
Subhv vane kaṇṭakasādṛśyātkhadiraḥ paryupāsitaḥ 
Subhv mahātarurvā bhavati samūlo vā vinaśyati 
Subhv nāṅkuraprakriyāmeti nyagrodhakaṇikāṅkuraḥ 
Subhv puṣpapattraphalacchāyāmūlavalkaladārubhiḥ 
Subhv dhanyā mahīruhā yeṣāṃ vimukhā yānti nārthinaḥ 
Subhv patatyaṅgāravarṣe vā vāti vā pralayānile 
Subhv tālaḥ stabdhatayārabdhastayaiva saha naśyati 
Subhv chāyāvanto gatavyālāḥ svārohāḥ phaladāyinaḥ 
Subhv mārgadrumā mahāntaśca pareṣāmeva bhūtaye 
Subhv agatīnāṃ khalīkārādduḥkhaṃ naivopajāyate 
Subhv bhavantyaśokāḥ prāyeṇa sāṅkurāḥ pādatāḍitāḥ 
Subhv yadyapi candanaviṭapī vidhinā phalakusumavarjito vihitaḥ 
Subhv nijavapuṣaiva pareṣāṃ tathāpi saṃtāpamapaharati 
Subhv prāpte vasantamāse vṛddhiṃ prāpnoti sakalavanarājinaḥ 
Subhv yanna karīre pattraṃ tatkiṃ doṣo vasantasya 
Subhv phalitaghanaviṭapavighaṭitapaṭudinakaramahasi lasati kalpatarau 
Subhv chāyārthī kaḥ paśurapi bhavati jaradvīrudhāṃ praṇayī 
Subhv phalakusumakisalayojjvalaviṭapaśatāntaritataraṇikiraṇaughe 
Subhv mārgatarau nikaṭasthe kaḥ pathikaḥ klāntimanubhavati 
Subhv dūrīkṛtasvārthalavā janasya
Subhv samudyatā ye bhuvi tāpaśāntyai 
Subhv drumāsta evāgatikā na vidmaḥ
Subhv prajāpaterāśayaleśamatra 
Subhv candane viṣadharānsahāmahe
Subhv vastu sundaramaguptimatkutaḥ 
Subhv rakṣituṃ vada kimātmasauṣṭhavaṃ
Subhv saṃcitāḥ khadira kaṇṭakāstvayā 
Subhv grathita eṣa mithaḥ kṛtaśṛṅkhalo
Subhv viṣadharairadhiruhya mahājaḍaḥ 
Subhv malayajaḥ sumanobhiranāśrito
Subhv yadata eva phalena na yujyate 
Subhv yatkiṃcanānucitamapyucitānubandhi
Subhv kiṃ candanasya na kṛtaṃ kusumaṃ phalaṃ vā 
Subhv lajjāmahe bhṛśamapakrama eva yātus
Subhv tasyāntikaṃ parigṛhītabṛhatkuṭhāraḥ 
Subhv he bālacampakataro taruṇīkapola
Subhv lāvaṇyacumbanasukhocitacārupuṣpa 
Subhv kiṃ puṣpitena vijahīha vikāsahāsa
Subhv muddāmapāmaragaṇā marubhūmireṣā 
Subhv antaḥprataptamarusaikatadahyamāna
Subhv mūlasya campakataroḥ kva vikāsacintā 
Subhv prāyo bhavatyanucitasthitideśabhājāṃ
Subhv śreyaḥ svajīvaparipālanamātrameva 
Subhv daurjanyamātmani paraṃ prathitaṃ vidhātrā
Subhv bhūrjadrumasya viphalatvasamarpaṇena 
Subhv kiṃ carmabhirniśitaśastraśatāvakṛttair
Subhv āśāṃ na pūrayati sorthiparamparāṇām 
Subhv kiṃ kaṇṭakaikarasikena phaladviṣā kiṃ
Subhv vairasyasīmani kimu sthirakautukena 
Subhv chāyāvilāsavimukhena satāṃ kimaṅga
Subhv chātrā khalena khadiradruma eṣa sṛṣṭaḥ 
Subhv labdhaṃ cirādamṛtavatkimamṛtyave syād
Subhv dīrghaṃ rasāyanavadāyuruta pradadyāt 
Subhv etatphalaṃ yadayamadhvagaśāpadagdhaḥ
Subhv stabdhaḥ phalaṃ phalati varṣaśatena tālaḥ 
Subhv he vṛkṣa śobhita mahāphalabhāralakṣmyā
Subhv kṣuttāpaśāntijanakaikajagatprasiddha 
Subhv tvatto mayā kathamapīdamadho nirastam
Subhv ekaṃ phalaṃ śakunikhaṇḍitamalpamāptam 
Subhv atyantaśītalatayā subhagasvabhāva
Subhv satyaṃ na kaścidapi te tarurasti tulyaḥ 
Subhv chāyārthināmapi punarvikaṭadvijihva
Subhv saṅgena candana viṣadrumanirviśeṣaḥ 
Subhv kathamiyati vanānte kaścideko na tādṛg
Subhv varavanataruruccaiḥ puṣpavallīphalāḍhyaḥ 
Subhv jagadasukhavidhāturdagdhadhāturniyogād
Subhv dhavakhadirapalāśāḥ kevalaṃ vṛddhibhājaḥ 
Subhv śākhāsaṃtatisaṃniruddhagaganābhogasya labdhvā taroś
Subhv chāyāṃ yasya bhavidbhireva śamitā gharmāpadonekaśaḥ 
Subhv bhoḥ pānthā nanu dṛśyatāṃ vidhigatistasyaiva kālakṣaya
Subhv prakṣīṇasya taledya taptasikatāṅgāraivaḥ paraṃ dahyate 
Subhv citrairyasya patittribhirdaśadiśo bhrāntvā sametaiḥ sukhaṃ
Subhv viśrāntaṃ śayitaṃ prabhuktamuṣitaṃ skandhe phalaiḥ praśrite 
Subhv tasyaivonmathitasya duṣṭakariṇā mārgadrumasyādhunā
Subhv kārīṣāya kaṣanti śoṣaparuṣāṃ gopālabālāstvacam 
Subhv saṃtoṣaḥ kimaśaktatā kimathavā tasminnasaṃbhāvanā
Subhv śobhaivātha ca kānanisthitiriyaṃ pradveṣa evāthavā 
Subhv āstāṃ khalvanurūpayā saphalayā puṣpaśriyā durvidhe
Subhv saṃbandhonanurūpayāpi na kṛtaḥ kiṃ candanasya tvayā 
Subhv sanmūlaḥ prathinnatirghanalasacchāyaḥ sthitaḥ satpathe
Subhv sevyaḥ sadbhiritīdamākalayatā tālodhvagenāśritaḥ 
Subhv puṃsaḥ śaktiriyatyasau sa tu phaledadyāthavā śvothavā
Subhv kāle kvāpyathavā kadācidathavā netyatra vedhāḥ prabhuḥ 
Subhv yajjātosi catuṣpathe ghanalasacchāyosi kiṃ chāyayā
Subhv saṃyuktaḥ phalitosi kiṃ yadi phalaiḥ pūrṇosi kiṃ saṃnataḥ 
Subhv he sadvṛkṣa sahasva saṃprati sakhe śākhāśikhākarṣaṇa
Subhv kṣobhāmoṭanabhañjanāni janataḥ svaireva duścoṣṭitaiḥ 
Subhv suskandhasya visārisaurabhaguṇākrāntākhilāśasya te
Subhv tanvīcārupayodharāntarakṛtasparśasya gopyākṛteḥ 
Subhv doṣaḥ kopi bhujaṃgasaṃgamakṛtaḥ prodgūta eṣodhunā
Subhv yena tvāṃ parihṛtya candanataro yāntyadhvagā dūrataḥ 
Subhv chinnastaptasuhṛtsa candanataruryūyaṃ palāyyāgatā
Subhv bhogābhyāsasukhāsikāḥ pratidinaṃ tā vismṛtāstatra vaḥ 
Subhv daṃṣṭrākoṭiviṣolkayā pratikṛtaṃ tasya praharturna cet
Subhv kiṃ tenaiva saha svayaṃ na nidhanaṃ yātāḥstha bho bhoginaḥ 
Subhv tvanmūle puruṣāyuṣaṃ gatamidaṃ kālena saṃśaṣyatāṃ
Subhv ksodīyāṃsamapi kṣaṇaṃ paramataḥ śaktiḥ kutaḥ prāṇitum 
Subhv tatsvastyastu vivṛddhimehi mahatīmadyāpi kā nastvarā
Subhv kalyāṇaiḥ phalitāsi tālaviṭapinputreṣu pautreṣu vā 
Subhv chāyāsyaiva ghanāsugandhirayamevāpannatāpacchidā
Subhv magresyaiva guṇagrahaḥ saguṇatā kiṃ candanasyocyatām 
Subhv ā mūlātpunareṣu baddhavṛtibhirvyālaistathā dūṣito
Subhv jāne yena varaṃ dhavotha khadiropyanyothavā na tvayam 
Subhv na ślāṣyāni phalāni pallavakṛtā chāyā na vāñchāpi sā
Subhv no puṣpaṃ sumanoharaṃ na vihagāḥ śabdāmṛtasyandinaḥ 
Subhv kākavrātapurīṣanirbharajaranmūrteraśuddhātmano
Subhv niḥstabdhasya taroradhaḥ kathamaho sṛṣṭosi durvedhasā 
Subhv nāsya svāduphalaṃ na cāru kusumaṃ na snigdhaparṇā latā
Subhv na cchāyā klamahāriṇī na ca kalakvāṇāstathā patriṇaḥ 
Subhv eṣosau khadiradumaḥ kimathavā pānthena dṛṣṭastvayā
Subhv tatkiṃ pāntha kaṭhorakaṇṭakamukhairgātrakṣatārthī bhavān 
Subhv snigdhāḥ pallavinaḥ prakāmaviṭapavyāviddhacaṇḍātapā
Subhv namrāḥ svāduphalā samāśritajanakṣuttāpavicchedinaḥ 
Subhv dagdhāste taravaḥ prayāntu pathikāsteṣveva mārgeṣvamī
Subhv rūkṣāḥ kāṇṭakinaḥ sasarpavivarā bhūyaḥ prarūḍhā drumāḥ 
Subhv chāyā nātmana eva yā kathamasāvanyasya niṣpragrahā
Subhv grīṣmoṣmāpadi śītalastalabhūvi spandonilādeḥ kutaḥ 
Subhv vārtā varṣaśate gate kila phalaṃ bhāvīti vārtaiva sā
Subhv drāghimṇā muṣitāḥ kiyacciramaho tālena bālā vayam 
Subhv kastvaṃ bhoḥ kathayāmi daivahatakaṃ māṃ viddhi śāhoṭakaṃ
Subhv vairāgyādiva vakṣi sādhu viditaṃ kasmādidaṃ kathyate 
Subhv vāmenātra vaṭastamadhvagajanaḥ sarvātmanā sevate
Subhv na cchāyāpi paropakārakṛtaye mārgasthitasyāpi se 
Subhv āmodairmaruto mṛgāḥ kisalayairlambaistvacā tāpasāḥ
Subhv puṣpaiḥ ṣaṭcaraṇāḥ phalaiḥ śakunayo gharmārditāśchāyayā 
Subhv skandhairgandhagajāśca viśramarujāḥ śaśvadvibhaktāstvayā
Subhv prāptastvaṃ druma bodhisattvapadavīṃ satyaṃ kujātāḥ pare 
Subhv bhrāmyadbhṛṅgabharāvanamrakusumacyotanmadhūdgandhiṣu
Subhv cchāyāvatsu taleṣu pānthanivahā viśramya geheṣviva 
Subhv nityaṃ nirjharavārivāritatṛṣastṛpyanti yeṣāṃ phalais
Subhv te nandantu phalantu yāntu ca parāmatyunnatiṃ pādapāḥ 
Subhv he he maṇḍitamārga mārgaviṭapiñjīvyāḥ samāḥ śāśvatīr
Subhv adyāpyāvṛṇu diktaṭāni viṭapaiḥ sālaiścucumbāmbaram 
Subhv mūle viśramaṇāśayaiva luṭhitā yanna tvayā kevalaṃ
Subhv gharmārteḥ parimocitāḥ phalaśatairyāvadvayaṃ tarpitāḥ 
Subhv vṛddhiryasya tarormanorathaśatairāśāvatā prārthitā
Subhv jātosau sarasaḥ pravāsiphaladaḥ sarvāśritāpāśrayaḥ 
Subhv nānādeśasamāgatairaviditairākrāntamanyaiḥ khagais
Subhv taṃ labdhāvasaropi vṛddhaśakunirdūre sthito vīkṣate 
Subhv dāvāgniploṣaduḥkhaṃ kharapavanajalakleśamarkācca tāpaṃ
Subhv mātaṅgākarṣaṇāni vyasanamapi guru prāptavantopi vajrāt 
Subhv dārucchāyāphalāni tvacamapi kusumaṃ mañjarīḥ pallavānvā
Subhv nārthibhyo vārayanti pratidivasamaho sādhu vṛttaṃ tarūṇām 
Subhv haṃsāḥ padmavanāśayā balibhujo gṛdhrāśca māṃsāśayā
Subhv pānthāḥ svāduphalāśayā madhulihaḥ saurabhyagandhāśayā 
Subhv dūrānniṣphalaraktapuṣpanicayairniḥsāra rathyonnate
Subhv re re śalmalipādapa pratidinaṃ ke na tvayā vañcitāḥ 
Subhv bhrātarbhīmamarubhramśramaśamavyāpārapāraṃgamaṃ
Subhv matvā candanapādapaṃ pathika mā viśrāntaye śiśriyaḥ 
Subhv etasyāntikavartibhirghanaviṣajvālāvalībīṣaṇair
Subhv āśvāsya smṛtiśeṣatāṃ viṣadharairnīṃtaḥ kiyantodhvagāḥ 
Subhv uccairyo madhupānalubdhamanasāṃ bhṛṅgāṅganānāṃ gaṇair
Subhv udgīto racitālayaḥ khagakulairdeśāntarādāgataiḥ 
Subhv āsīdyaśva niṣevitodhvagaśatairgrīṣmoṣmatānticchide
Subhv soyaṃ saṃprati durmadena dalitaśchāyātarurdantinā 
Subhv bhuktaṃ svāduphalaṃ kṛtaṃ ca śayanaṃ śākhāgrajaiḥ pallavais
Subhv tvacchāyāpariśītalaṃ ca salilaṃ pītaṃ vinītaḥ klamaḥ 
Subhv viśrāntaṃ suciraṃ tatopi manasā prāptā parā nirvṛtis
Subhv tvaṃ sanmārgatarurvayaṃ ca pathikā bhūyāspunaḥ saṃgamaḥ 
Subhv astyeva bhūbhṛtāṃ mūrdhni divi vā dyotatembudaḥ 
Subhv marudbhirbhujyamānopi sa kimeti rasātalam 
Subhv ambudaḥ kṛtapado nabhastale
Subhv toyapūraparipūritodadhiḥ 
Subhv goṣpadasya bharaṇepyaśaktimān
Subhv ityasatyamabhidīyate katham 
Subhv etadatra pathikaikajīvitaṃ
Subhv paśya śuṣyati kathaṃ mahatsaraḥ 
Subhv dhiṅmudhāmbudhara ruddhasadgatir
Subhv vardhitā kimiha haṭṭavāhinī 
Subhv svārthānapekṣaṃ janatāpaśāntyai
Subhv nityoditāḥ santi payomucomī 
Subhv vivarṣiṇastānavagṛhṇate ye
Subhv santyeva te kepi mahānubhāvāḥ 
Subhv kva dṛṣṭamandhena balāhakena
Subhv ghrātuṃ gavā yanna tṛṇaṃ nighṛṣṭam 
Subhv mahātarurbandhurivādhvagānā
Subhv māyātvavaśyāyakaṇairdaridraḥ 
Subhv uttuṅgaśailaśikharāśrayaṇena kecid
Subhv uddāmavīcivalitāḥ sarito bhavanti 
Subhv anye punarjalakaṇāstṛṇaloṣṭapātā
Subhv dambhomucāṃ payasi na kṣayamānpuvanti 
Subhv yatroṣitosi cirakālamakiṃcanaḥ san
Subhv narṇaḥpratigrahadhanagrahaṇādhamarṇaḥ 
Subhv nirlajja garjasi samudrataṭepi tatra
Subhv dhṛṣṭodhamastava samo ghana naiva dṛṣṭaḥ 
Subhv āsyaṃ nirasya rasitaiḥ suciraṃ vihasya
Subhv gātrāntareṣu ghana varṣasi cātakasya 
Subhv taccañcukoṭikuṭilāyatakaṃdharasya
Subhv prāṇātyayosya bhavataḥ parihāsamātram 
Subhv ākramyoccaiḥ śirasi vasatirbhūbhṛtāmunnatānāṃ
Subhv toyādānāṃ tadapi jaladherlokasaṃtāpaśāntyai 
Subhv dīrghā chāyā prakṛtimahati vyomni cābhogabandho
Subhv he he megha spṛhayati na te kaḥ kiletthaṃ vratāya 
Subhv ākramyoccaiḥ śirasi vasatirbhūbhṛtāmunnatānāṃ
Subhv toyādānaṃ tadapi jaladherlokasaṃtāpaśāntyai 
Subhv dīrghā chāyā prakṛtimahati vyomni cābhogabandho
Subhv he he megha spṛhayati na te kaḥ kiletthaṃ vratāya 
Subhv sādhūtpātaghanaugha sādhu sudhiyāṃ dheyaṃ dharāyāmidaṃ
Subhv konyaḥ kartumalaṃ tavaiva ghaṭate karmedṛśaṃ duṣkaram 
Subhv sarvasyaupayikāni yāni katicitkṣetrāṇi tatrāśaniḥ
Subhv sarvānaupayikeṣu dagdhasikatāraṇyeṣvapāṃ vṛṣṭayaḥ 
Subhv bhekaiḥ koṭaraśāyibhirmṛtamiva kṣmāntargataṃ kacchapaiḥ
Subhv pāṭhīnaiḥ pṛthupaṅkakūṭaluṭhitairyasminmuhurmūrchitam 
Subhv tasmiñchuṣkasarasyakālajaladenāgatya tacceṣṭitaṃ
Subhv yenā kaṇṭhanimagnavanyakariṇāṃ yūthaiḥ payaḥ pīyate 
Subhv yadbhūbhṛto laghuguṇairapi baddhamūlam
Subhv āpāditāni sahasaiva tṛṇaiḥ śirāṃsi 
Subhv ambhomucaḥ pracuravarṣaviśṛṅkhalasya
Subhv tacceṣṭitaṃ duravadhāragaterjalasya 
Subhv kṛchrāddatte viralaviralānvāribindūnpravṛddho
Subhv garjatyekaḥ sarabhasataraṃ paśya tanmātralābhāt 
Subhv nṛtyatyanyopyatulamahimaślāghyabhūmirna jāne
Subhv madhyādābhyāṃ vipulahṛdayaścātakaḥ kiṃ nu meghaḥ 
Subhv gatāste jīmūtāḥ sphuradalikulaśyāmavapuṣaḥ
Subhv śriyā yeṣāṃ loke sthalajalavibhāgopyapahṛtaḥ 
Subhv vṛthā tṛṣṇāndhaḥ kiṃ bhramasi vidhuraścātakaśiśo
Subhv śarajjīmūtoyaṃ kuta iha payobindurapi te 
Subhv paśyāmaḥ kimayaṃ viceṣṭata iti svalpābhrasiddhikriyair
Subhv darpāddūramupekṣitena balavatkarmeritairmantribhiḥ 
Subhv labdhātmaprasareṇa rakṣitumathāśakyena muktvāśaniṃ
Subhv sphītastāvadaho ghanena ripuṇā dagdho girigrāmakaḥ 
Subhv garjitvā bahu saṃnirudhya gaganaṃ pracchādya diṅmaṇḍalaṃ
Subhv saṃpādyoddalitendranīlaśakalaśyāmābhirāmaṃ vapuḥ 
Subhv prāpte vāridharāgamepi salilaṃ tattyaktamambhomucā
Subhv cañcūśrātakapotakasya sakalā siktā na yena svayam 
Subhv atrotpātaghanena mantrivikale śūnyāmbaravyāpinā
Subhv dhṛṣṭasvaprakṛtikriyāsamucite grāme tathā jṛmbhitam 
Subhv rathyākardamavāhināmatiśucisvacchātmanāmantaraṃ
Subhv nāpyajñāyi janairyathaughapayasāṃ strotojalānāmapi 
Subhv re meghāḥ svaśarīradānaguru kiṃ bauddhaṃ yaśo na śrutaṃ
Subhv yaṣmābhiḥ kimu pārijātacaritaṃ nākarṇitaṃ vā kvacit 
Subhv yenaitatsukhalabhyamambu dadatāṃ yuṣmākamudgarjatāṃ
Subhv no lajjāpyabhijāyatetirabhasādvyomnyuddhataṃ dhāvatām 
Subhv sthāne varṣati naiva garjati vṛthā klāntiṃ haratyañjasā
Subhv kṣetrāṇāṃ paritāpajarjararucāṃ kṣemaṃkaraḥ kṣmātale 
Subhv yadyadbhadrakasāndratāṃ hṛdi dadhātyanyatkarotyullasa
Subhv nsanmeghoyamamoghadarśanaghanasnigdhacchavirvardhatām 
Subhv no garjatyamburāśistrijagadadhipatiprārthitārthapradāna
Subhv vyāpārsphītakīrtiḥ sphuradanlaśikhānargharatnaikapūrṇaḥ 
Subhv tattoyastokamātravyapahṛtavikṛtiḥ prākṛtoyaṃ prakṛtyā
Subhv śūnye kṣiptvāmbu garjatyagaṇitanidhano vārivāhaḥ sagarvam 
Subhv na pālayati maryādāṃ velākhyāmambudhistathā 
Subhv tṛṣyatāṃ nopakartavyamitīmāmaparāṃ yathā 
Subhv gavādīnāṃ payonyedyuḥ sadyo vā dadhi jāyate 
Subhv kṣīrodadhestu nādyāpi mahatāṃ vikṛtiḥ kutaḥ 
Subhv yadyapi svacchabhāvena darśayatyudadhirmaṇīn 
Subhv tathāpi jānudaghnoyamiti cetasi mā kṛthāḥ 
Subhv yasyāmbukaṇikāpyāsye na patatyarthīnāṃ kvacit 
Subhv kaṣṭamambhonidhiḥ sopi nadīna iti kathyate 
Subhv yātu nāśaṃ samudrasya mahimā sa bhuvi śrutaḥ 
Subhv vāḍavaḥ kṣutpipāsārto yenaikopi na tarpitaḥ 
Subhv amṛtarasavisaraavitaraṇamaraṇottāritasure sati payodhau 
Subhv kasya sphuranti hṛdaye grīṣmataḍākā bhuvi varākāḥ 
Subhv yadayaṃ śaśiśekharo haro
Subhv harirapyeṣa yadīśitā śriyaḥ 
Subhv amarā api yatsurā amī
Subhv tadimāstasya vibhūtivipruṣaḥ 
Subhv kṣārataiva hi guṇastathāsti te
Subhv yena na vrajati kaścidantikam 
Subhv bhīṣaṇākṛti bibharṣi yādasāṃ
Subhv cakramarṇava kimarthamagrataḥ 
Subhv apāsya lakṣmīharaṇotthavairitā
Subhv macintayitvā ca tadadrimanthanam 
Subhv dadau nivāsaṃ haraye mahodadhir
Subhv vimatsarā dhīradhiyāṃ hi vṛttayaḥ 
Subhv jitendubhāso nayatāṃ maṇinadhas
Subhv tṛṇāni mūrdhnā bibhṛtāṃ jaleśvaraḥ 
Subhv prabhorna kaścitprabhurasti tattvato
Subhv ratnāni ratnāni tṛṇaṃ tṛṇaṃ punaḥ 
Subhv grīṣmaṃ dviṣantu jaladāgamarthayantāṃ
Subhv te saṃkaṭaprakṛtayaḥ kṛpaṇāstaḍāgāḥ 
Subhv abdhestu mugdhaśapharīcaṭulācalendra
Subhv niṣkampakukṣipayaso dvayamapyacintyam 
Subhv grāvāṇo maṇayo harirjalacaro lakṣmīḥ payomānuṣī
Subhv muktaughaḥ sikatā pravālalatikāḥ śevālamambhaḥ sudhā 
Subhv tīre kalpamahīruhāḥ kimaparaṃ nāmāpi ratnākaro
Subhv dūrātkarṇarasāyanaṃ nikaṭatastṛṣnāpi no śāmyati 
Subhv āstāṃ klamāpaharaṇaṃ jaladherjalena
Subhv dūre davāgniparidīpitamānasānām 
Subhv etāvadastu yadi toyakaṇairna jihvā
Subhv dandahyate dviguṇatāṃ ca na yāti tṛṣṇā 
Subhv ratnānyamūni makarālaya māvamaṃsthāḥ
Subhv kallolavellitadṛṣatparuṣaprahāraiḥ 
Subhv kiṃ kaustubhena vihito bhavato na nāma
Subhv yāñcāprasāritakaraḥ puruṣottamopi 
Subhv lajjāmahe vayamaho bhṛśamapyaneke
Subhv sāṃyātrikāḥ salilarāśimamī viśānti 
Subhv skandhādhiropitatadīyataṭopakaṇṭha
Subhv kauleyakāmbudṛtayo yadudīrṇatṛṣṇāḥ 
Subhv ā strīśiśuprathitayaiṣa pipāsitebhyaḥ
Subhv saṃrakṣyatembudhirapeyatayaiva dūrāt 
Subhv dṛṣṭvā karālamakarālikarālitābhiḥ
Subhv kiṃ bhāyayasyaparamūrmiparamparābhiḥ 
Subhv dhigdhigdhigambudhimamī nirapatrapasya
Subhv yasyādhvagā marubhuvīva nitāntatāntāḥ 
Subhv tṛḍdāhaśuṣkagalanirgatadīrghajihvā
Subhv dīnā vivartitadṛśonutaṭaṃ prayānti 
Subhv nirmathyate yadi surāsurasainyasaṃghair
Subhv āpūryate yadi jalairjaladāpagābhiḥ 
Subhv pepīyate ca vaḍavāmukhavahninā cen
Subhv na kṣubhyati sma jaladhirna tanutvameti 
Subhv mainākādibhiradribhirmaghavataḥ saṃtrasya yatrāsyate
Subhv caṇḍārcirbhagavānudeti ca yato yatrāstamabhyeti ca 
Subhv śete kvāpi nilīya yasya jagatāṃ kukṣyekadeśe patir
Subhv gāmbhīryaśriyamasya kastulayituṃ vārāṃ nidherarhati 
Subhv upakṛtavatā śrīratnābhyāṃ hareḥ śaśilekhayā
Subhv manasijaripoḥ pīyūṣeṇāpyaśeṣadivaukasām 
Subhv kathamitarathāḥ tena stheyaṃ yaśobharamantharaṃ
Subhv yadi na mathanāyāsaṃ dhīraḥ saheta payonidhiḥ 
Subhv viṣamabhimukhaṃ muktaṃ raudraṃ diśo daśa saṃśritāḥ
Subhv śaśitarumaṇiprāyaiḥ prāyaḥ pralobhanamāhitam 
Subhv kimiva na kṛtaṃ nanthārambhe śaṭhena payodhinā
Subhv tadapi nipuṇairnāsya kṣāntaṃ surairamṛtaṃ vinā 
Subhv yadiha bhavato gāmbhīryeṇa prayāti mahattayā
Subhv pyanucitaguṇārambhaḥ kālaḥ kimetadanantaram 
Subhv ayi jalanidhe kiṃ kallolairalabdhasamāptibhir
Subhv virama saritāmetattoyaṃ na testi manāgapi 
Subhv samāśrityotsaṅgaṃ vipṛtavadanasyāsya vasataḥ
Subhv kṣaṇenaikasyāntarjvalitavapuṣo yatkṣaṇamapi 
Subhv na tṛṣṇāmaurvāgnerapanayati puṣṭepi vibhave
Subhv nṛśaṃsasyāmbhodhervrajatu vilayaṃ sosya mahimā 
Subhv aho bata saritpateridamanāryarūpaṃ paraṃ
Subhv yadujjvalarucīnmaṇīnsuciracarcitāsthāguṇān 
Subhv jaḍairanupayogibhiḥ parata etya labdhāspadaiḥ
Subhv kṣipatyaniśamūrjitairjhagiti tanmayatvaṃ gataḥ 
Subhv ihaikaścūḍālobhyajani kalaśādyasya sakalaiḥ
Subhv pipāsorambhobhiśculukamapi no bhartumaśakaḥ 
Subhv svamāhātmyaślāghāgurugahanagarjābhirabhitaḥ
Subhv kuṣitvā kliśnāsi śrutikuharamabdhe kimiti naḥ 
Subhv rūkṣaṃ kṣāramapeyamatra salilaṃ labdhvā paraṃ tapyate
Subhv vyālagrāhabhiyāvagāhanamapi svasthena nāsādyate 
Subhv tatkiṃ pāntha payodhināmani marau tṛṣṇāvimūḍho bhavān
Subhv antarnihnutināśitāmalamaṇivrāte mudhā dhāvasi 
Subhv sarvāsāṃ trijagatyapāmiyamasāvādhāratā tāvakī
Subhv prollāsoyamasau tavāmbunilaye seyaṃ mahāsattvatā 
Subhv sevitvā bahubhaṅgabhīṣaṇatanuṃ tvāmeva velācala
Subhv grāvasrotasi pāpa tāpakalaho yatkvāpi nirvāpyate 
Subhv kallolairvikiratvasau girivarānvelāvilāsotthitaiḥ
Subhv śabdairvā badhirīkarotu kakubho dhattāṃ ca vistīrṇatām 
Subhv pānthānāṃ ravitāpataptavapuṣāṃ tṛṣṇātirekacchidaḥ
Subhv kiṃ sāmyaṃ pratanoḥ karotu sarasopyabdhiḥ kṛtāḍamabaraḥ 
Subhv dataṃ yena sudhānidhānamasamaṃ sattvādhikenārthine
Subhv śrīvāsopi mahāmaṇirvidhurasau kalpadrumo gaustathā 
Subhv śāpātkṣārajalastathāpi jaladhiḥ prāptāyaśā ityaho
Subhv lokoyaṃ tṛṇavadguṇaṃ vigaṇayandoṣagrahaikāgradhīḥ 
Subhv hā kaṣṭaṃ taṭavāsinopi viphalaprāgbhāramālokya mām
Subhv anyatraiva vipāsavaḥ pratidinaṃ gacchantyamī jantavaḥ 
Subhv itthaṃ vyarthajalātibhāravahanaprodbhūtakhedādiva
Subhv svāṃ mūrtiṃ vaḍavānale jalanidhirmanye juhotyanvaham 
Subhv maryādāparipālanena mahatāṃ kṣauṇībhṛtāṃ rakṣaṇād
Subhv viśrāntyā madhusūdanasya suciraṃ yatkiṃcidāsāditam 
Subhv gāmbhīryocitamātmano jaladhinā manthavyathāsaṃbhramād
Subhv deveṣvarpayatāmṛtaṃ drutamaho sarvaṃ tadutpuṃsitam 
Subhv āścaryaṃ vaḍavānalaḥ sa bhagavānāścaryamambhonidhir
Subhv yatkarmātiśayaṃ vicintya manasaḥ kampaḥ samutpadyate 
Subhv ekasyāśrayaghasmarasya pibatastṛptirna jātā jalair
Subhv anyasyāpi mahātmano na vapuṣaḥ svalpopi jātaḥ śramaḥ 
Subhv nodvegaṃ yadi yāsi yadyavahitaḥ karṇaṃ dadāsi kṣaṇaṃ
Subhv tvāṃ pṛcchāmi yadambudhe kimapi tanniścitya dehyuttaram 
Subhv nairāśyānuśayātimātraniśitaṃ niḥśvasya yaddṛśyase
Subhv tṛṣyadbhiḥ pathikaiḥ kiyattadadhikaṃ syādaurvadāhādataḥ 
Subhv itaḥ svapiti keśavaḥ kulamitastadīyadviṣām
Subhv itaśca śaraṇārthināṃ śikhariṇāṃ guṇāḥ śerate 
Subhv itaśca vaḍavānalaḥ saha samastasaṃvartakair
Subhv aho vitatamūrjitaṃ bharasahaṃ ca sindhorvapuḥ 
Subhv vaikuṇṭhāyaśriyamabhinavaṃ śītabhānuṃ bhavāya
Subhv prādāduccaiḥśravasamapi vā vajriṇe tatkva gaṇyam 
Subhv tṛṣṇārtāya svamapi munaye yaddadāti sma dehaṃ
Subhv konyastasmādbhavati bhuvaneṣvambudherbodhisattvaḥ 
Subhv ratnojjvalāḥ pravikirallaṃharīḥ samīrair
Subhv abdhiḥ kriyeta yadi ruddhataṭābhimukhyaḥ 
Subhv doṣorthinaḥ sa khalu bhāgyaviparyayāṇāṃ
Subhv dāturmanāgapi na tasya tu dātṛtāyāḥ 
Subhv antarye satataṃ luṭhantyagaṇitāstāneva pāthodharai
Subhv rāttānāpatatastaraṅgavalayairāliṅgya gṛhṇannasau 
Subhv vyaktaṃ mauktikaratnatāṃ jalakaṇānsaṃprāpayatyambudhiḥ
Subhv prāyonyena kṛtādaro laghurapi prāptorcyate svāmibhiḥ 
Subhv svastyastu vidrumalatāsumanomaṇibhyaḥ
Subhv kalyāṇinī bhavatu mauktikaśuktipaṅktiḥ 
Subhv prāptaṃ mayā sakalameva phalaṃ payodher
Subhv yaddāruṇairjalacarairna vidāritosmi 
Subhv ādāya vāri paritaḥ saritāṃ mukhebhyaḥ
Subhv kiṃ tāvadarjitamanena durarṇavena 
Subhv kṣārīkṛtaṃ ca vaḍavādahane hutaṃ ca
Subhv pātālakukṣikuhare viniveśitaṃ ca 
Subhv kālaprāptaṃ mahāratnaṃ yo na gṛhṇātyabuddhimān 
Subhv anyahastagataṃ dṛṣṭvā paścātsa paritapyate 
Subhv bhidyatenupraviśyāntaryo yathārucyupādhinā 
Subhv viśuddhiḥ kīdṛśī tasya jaḍasya sphaṭikāśmanaḥ 
Subhv sphaṭikasya guṇo yosau sa evāyāti doṣatām 
Subhv dhatte svacchatayā chāyāṃ yastāṃ malavatāmapi 
Subhv yena pāṣāṇakhaṇḍasya mūlyamalpaṃ vasuṃdharā 
Subhv anastamitasārasya tejasastadvijṛmbhitam 
Subhv śuṣkatanutṛṇalavāgraṃ gṛhṇāti dhanāśayānyadīyaṃ yaḥ 
Subhv mūḍhāstṛṇamaṇimapi taṃ niyuñjate pādarakṣāyai 
Subhv sadvaṃśajaḥ sādhuguṇaḥ suvṛttaḥ
Subhv saṃtāpabhittulyaguṇopagūḍhaḥ 
Subhv kānto dṛśaḥ paśya tathāpi hāraḥ
Subhv kṣipto bahistuṅgakucadvayena 
Subhv kanakabhūṣaṇasaṃgrahaṇocito
Subhv yadi maṇistrapuṇi pratibadhyate 
Subhv na sa virauti na cāpi hi śobhate
Subhv bhavati yojayiturvacanīyatā 
Subhv marakatasya varaṃ malinātmatā
Subhv tyajati jātu nijāṃ prakṛtiṃ na yaḥ 
Subhv amalatāṃ sphaṭikasya dhigañjasā
Subhv bhajati rūpamupāntagatasya yaḥ 
Subhv asminsakhe nanu maṇitvamahāsubhikṣe
Subhv cintāmaṇe tvamupalo bhava mā maṇirbhūḥ 
Subhv adyedṛśā hi maṇayaḥ prabhavanti loke
Subhv yeṣāṃ tṛṇagrahaṇakauśalameva bhūṣā 
Subhv bhūmau patannapi rajaḥ paridhūsaropi
Subhv jātyandhadurjanajanairavadhīritopi 
Subhv trailokyavandanamahāmahimānamantaś
Subhv cintāmaṇirnahi jahāti kadācideva 
Subhv cintāmaṇe bhuvi na kenacidīśvareṇa
Subhv mūrdhnā dhṛtosi yadi mā sma tato viṣīdaḥ 
Subhv nāstyeva hi tvadadhiropaṇapuṇyabījaṃ
Subhv saubhāgyayogyamiha kasyaciduttamāṅgam 
Subhv cintāmaṇestṛṇamaṇeśca kṛtaṃ vidhātrā
Subhv kenobhayorapi maṇitvamadaḥ samānam 
Subhv naikorthitāni dadadarthijanāya khinno
Subhv gṛhṇañjarattṛṇalavaṃ na tu lajjitonyaḥ 
Subhv manorathaśatairvṛto bhuvananāthacūḍocitas
Subhv tṛṇairalamadhaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛtapadaḥ kvacidgrāvasu 
Subhv vrajatyapi sacetasāṃ viṣayamīdṛśāṃ yo dṛśo
Subhv luṭhatyacalakaṃdare vidhura eṣa cintāmaṇiḥ 
Subhv parāmṛṣati saspṛhaṃ muhurapelavaṃ vīkṣate
Subhv mahatkimapi ratnamityasamasaṃmadaṃ gūhate 
Subhv kutopi parilepavacchavimavāpya kācopale
Subhv vahatyatikadarthanāṃ bata varākakaḥ pāmaraḥ 
Subhv kiraṇanikarairāśācakraṃ ciraṃ paripūrayan
Subhv kimiha gahena bhrātarvyarthaṃ samullasito bhavān 
Subhv ka iha bhavato vettyatyantaṃ nisargamahārghatāṃ
Subhv marakatamaṇe dagdhagrāme hatādarapāmare 
Subhv dūre kasyacideṣa kopyakṛtadhīrnaivāsya vettyantaraṃ
Subhv mānī kopi na yācate mṛgayate kopyalpamalpāśayaḥ 
Subhv itthaṃ prārthitadānadurvyasanino naudāryarekhojjvalā
Subhv jātā naipuṇadustareṣu nikaṣā sthāneṣu cintāmaṇeḥ 
Subhv ye gṛhṇanti haṭhāttṛṇāni maṇayo ye vāpyayaḥpiṇḍikāṃ
Subhv te dṛṣṭāḥ pratidhāma dagdhamaṇayo vicchinnasaṃkhyāściram 
Subhv no jāne kimabhāvataḥ kimathavā daivādiha śrūyate
Subhv nāmāpyatra na tādṛśasya tu maṇe ratnāni gṛhṇāti yaḥ 
Subhv yanmuktāmaṇayombudherudarataḥ kṣiptā mahāvīcibhiḥ
Subhv paryanteṣu luṭhanti nirmalarucā spaṣṭāṭṭahāsā iva 
Subhv tattasyaiva parikṣayājjalanidherdvīpāntarālambināṃ
Subhv ratnānāṃ tu parigrahavyasaninaḥ santyeva sāṃyātrikāḥ 
Subhv māṇikyoyaṃ mahārghaḥ kṣititalamahito dīptimānuccajanmā
Subhv dṛṣṭvainaṃ nūnamārādvyapasaratitarāṃ kāpi daurgatyanītiḥ 
Subhv itthaṃ bhrāntiprapañcairvipadapahṛtaye kenacitsthāpitaḥ sa
Subhv nnante dṛṣṭaḥ sa eva vraṇaśataparuṣaḥ kopi pāṣāṇakhaṇḍaḥ 
Subhv yāmaḥ svasti tavāstu rohaṇagire mattaḥ sthitipracyutā
Subhv vartiṣyanta ime kathaṃ kathamiti svapnepi maivaṃ kṛthāḥ 
Subhv śrīmaṃste maṇayo vayaṃ yadi bhavallabdhapratiṣṭhāstadā
Subhv te śṛṅgāraparāyaṇāḥ kṣitibhujo maulau kariṣyanti naḥ 
Subhv uccairuccaratu ciraṃ cīrī vartmani taruṃ samāruhya 
Subhv digvyāpini śabdaguṇe śaṅkhaḥ saṃbhāvanābhūmiḥ 
Subhv śaṅkhosthiśeṣaḥ sphuṭito mṛto yad
Subhv ucchvāsitenocchvasate nu satyam 
Subhv kiṃ tūccaratyeva na sosya śabdaḥ
Subhv śravyo na yo yo na sadarthaśaṃsī 
Subhv prāṇānvihāya dhavalatvaguṇocitāni
Subhv prāptāni yajjagativaktraviśeṣayogāt 
Subhv śaṅkhairmahāvibhavaśabdavijṛmbhitāni
Subhv tajjīvitaṃ sahṛdayāḥ prabhavanti yeṣām 
Subhv dhīraḥ śrotrasukhāvahopi sadṛśaḥ satyaṃ paraṃ maṅgalaṃ
Subhv kvāpi grāmasurāṅgaṇe sa tu lasansaṃdhyāsu śaṅkhadhvaniḥ 
Subhv mādyanmedurasārameyasaralagrīvāgradīrghībhavan
Subhv nādo nāma kṛtānukāramuditagrāmyāṭṭahāsāhataḥ 
Subhv ratnākarājjanibhuvopyapacāyamānaḥ
Subhv śuṣkāsthiśeṣatanutāmapi lambamānaḥ 
Subhv śvāsaiḥ saphūtkṛtibhirapyupahanyamānaḥ
Subhv śuddhāśayo vadati maṅgalameva śaṅkhaḥ 
Subhv śaṅkhāḥ santi sahasraśo jalanidhervīcicchaṭāghaṭṭitāḥ
Subhv paryanteṣu luṭhanti ye dalaśataiḥ kalmāṣitakṣmātalāḥ 
Subhv ekaḥ kopi sa pāñcajanya udabhūdāścaryabhūtaḥ satāṃ
Subhv yaḥ saṃvartabharakṣamairmadhuripoḥ śvāsānilaiḥ pūryate 
Subhv sarvāśāparipūri huṃkṛtamado janmāpi dugdhodadher
Subhv govindānanacumbi sunadarataraṃ pūrṇendubimbādvapuḥ 
Subhv śrīreṣā sahajā guṇāḥ kimaparaṃ bhaṇyanta ete hi yat
Subhv kauṭilyaṃ hṛdi pāñcajanya bhavatastenātilajjāmahe 
Subhv varamaśrīkataivāstu netaraśrīsamānatā 
Subhv iti kairavakodbhede kamalaṃ mukulāyate 
Subhv lakṣmīsaṃparkarūpoyaṃ doṣaḥ padmasya niścitam 
Subhv yadayaṃ guṇasaṃdohadhāmanīndau parāṅmukhaḥ 
Subhv antaśchidrāṇi bhūyāṃsi kaṇṭakā bahavo bahiḥ 
Subhv kathaṃ kamalanālasya mā bhūvanbhaṅgurā guṇāḥ 
Subhv kiṃ dīrghadīrgheṣu guṇeṣu padma
Subhv siteṣvavacchādanakāraṇaṃ te 
Subhv astyeva tānpaśyati cedanāryā
Subhv trasteva lakṣmīrna padaṃ vidhatte 
Subhv sthalakuśeśaya saṃcinu kaṇṭakān
Subhv prathaya paṅkakulodbhavatāṃ mudā 
Subhv api badhāna dhṛtiṃ jalasaṃgame
Subhv vrajasi yena parāspadatāṃ śriyaḥ 
Subhv akṣeṣviyaṃ vyasanitā hṛdaye yadete
Subhv rāgo ghano madhumadotkaṭamānanaṃ ca 
Subhv padmastathāpi paramāspadameva lakṣmyās
Subhv taddainyameva kila durbhagatā yadebhiḥ 
Subhv padmādayo bahuguṇā api yanniśāsu
Subhv nāśaṃ na yānti viraheṇa divākarasya 
Subhv tatpaṅkasaṃkarajalāśayajanmajāḍya
Subhv jyāyovijṛmbhitamidaṃ trijagatpratītam 
Subhv lakṣmīṃ viśeṣaya kuśeśaya kauśalāṅkāṃ
Subhv jṛmbhā jahīhi calatāṃ ca vimuñca kiṃcit 
Subhv āśāgatānyalikulāni mudaṃ nayeha
Subhv mittre vidhau sati vidhatsa yatheṣṭametat 
Subhv nityaṃ tathā śṛṇu kuśeśaya madvacāṃsi
Subhv snehena yāni bhavataḥ kathayāmi kiṃcit 
Subhv kāntyānayā vimalayā bhramarairguṇairvā
Subhv kiṃ yāsi ramyatamatāmuta kaṇṭakarddheḥ 
Subhv saṃkocamehi bisapuṣpa jahīhi śobhāṃ
Subhv doṣākaroyamadhunā samudeti paśya 
Subhv vakrātmani prabhavati kramaśo vicintya
Subhv pracchannatā guṇavatāṃ svayameva yogyā 
Subhv truṭyadguṇopi bahukaṇṭakatāṃ gatopi
Subhv randhrānvitopi hatakardamasaṃbhavopi 
Subhv bhṛṅgopabhogyavibhavopi tathāpi padmo
Subhv mitrodaye vikasanaṃ labhate sadaiva 
Subhv kāmaṃ bhavantu madhulampaṭaṣaṭpadaugha
Subhv saṃghaṭṭaghuṃghumaghanadhvanayobjakhaṇḍāḥ 
Subhv gāyannatiśrutisukhaṃ vidhireva yatra
Subhv bhṛṅgaḥ sa kopi dharaṇidharanābhipadmaḥ 
Subhv tāpāpahe sahṛdaye rucire prabuddhe
Subhv mitrānurāganirate dhṛtasadguṇaughe 
Subhv svāṅgapradānaparitoṣitaṣaṭpadesmin
Subhv yuktaṃ taveha kamale kamale sthitiryat 
Subhv na paṅkādudbhūtirna jaḍasahavāsavyasanitā
Subhv vapurdigdhaṃ kāntyā sthalanalina ratnadyutimuṣā 
Subhv vyadhāsyaddurvedhā hṛdayalaghimānaṃ yadi na te
Subhv tvamevaikaṃ lakṣmyāḥ paramamabhaviṣyaḥ padamiha 
Subhv utpannā bahavastaleṣu sarasāmambhoruhāṇāṃ cayā
Subhv ye yāminyadhipānukāriramaṇīvaktropamānaṃ gatāḥ 
Subhv nābhau bhaumariporajāyata mahāpadmaḥ sa kopyekako
Subhv yastrailokyasamudbhavaprabhaviturjanmāvanitvaṃ gataḥ 
Subhv puṣyenyatrāvakāśo nipuṇamapahṛtaḥ saurabhālobhanābhiḥ
Subhv svābhogentaḥpraveśopyaśithilaniviḍaḥ kośabhāvānna dattaḥ 
Subhv nītvā nairāśyamitthaṃ galitagatirasau mugdhabuddhiḥ pradoṣe
Subhv padmena śrīmatāpi prasabhamubhayato bhraṃśitaḥ paśya bhṛṅgaḥ 
Subhv bhrātaḥ paṅkaja saṃkocaḥ kaṃcitkālaṃ viṣahyatām 
Subhv saiva prabhāte śobhā te bhāte dinakare bhavet 
Subhv adhogatiṃ ca saṃprāpya bisāḥ paṅkakalaṅkitāḥ 
Subhv guṇino nirguṇairdāśaiḥ kṛṣṭāḥ svāṅkuradarśitāḥ 
Subhv tadaṅkurāṇi padmāni guṇairyuktāni mānibhiḥ 
Subhv śirasā dhāryamāṇāni mīlitāni jaḍātmanā 
Subhv marau nāstyeva salilaṃ kṛchrādyadyapi labhyate 
Subhv tatkaṭu stokamuṣṇaṃ ca na karoti vitṛṣṇatām 
Subhv caṭulacātakacañcupuṭātpata
Subhv ñjalakaṇopi maroratigocaraḥ 
Subhv sa punaradya ghanāgamabandhunā
Subhv jaladhareṇa jalairaparaḥ kṛtaḥ 
Subhv kiṃ pāntha nirmathanasiddhyupayogivastu
Subhv saṃbhāraśālini marau sugṛhītanāmni 
Subhv saṃdṛśyatetiviparītamidaṃ hi tatra
Subhv kūposti tatra ca jalaṃ yadayatnalabhyam 
Subhv asminmarau kimaparaṃ vacasāmavācyaṃ
Subhv mā muñca pāntha muhurāśritavatsalo bhūḥ 
Subhv etattvayā jalalavāmiṣalālasena
Subhv dṛṣṭaṃ jvalatparikaraṃ sikatāvitānam 
Subhv satpādapānvipulapallavapuṣpabhāra
Subhv saṃpatparītavapuṣaḥ phalabhāranabhrān 
Subhv yo muñjuśiñjitaśakuntaśatāśritoru
Subhv śākhānmarau mṛgayate na tatosti mugdhaḥ 
Subhv jalatarutṛṇaśūnyaḥ śrāmyatāmadhvagānāṃ
Subhv kimapi kila batāhaṃ nopakartuṃ samarthaḥ 
Subhv iti na paramabhīkṣṇaṃ nānuśete na yāvac
Subhv chaṭhamaruranṛtāmbhaḥprāptaye tānprayuṅkte 
Subhv gatamatijavādbhrāntaṃ bhrāntaṃ samutkaṣitā ca bhūś
Subhv cirataramatho niḥśvasyātho sadainyamavasthitam 
Subhv kimiva na kṛtaṃ pānthenetthaṃ tathāpi śaṭho maruḥ
Subhv prakṛtivirasaḥ kaṣṭaṃ yāto manāgapi nārdratām 
Subhv itaḥ kākānīkaṃ pratibhayamitaḥ kauśikakṛtā
Subhv ditomī gṛdhrādyāḥ kulamidamitaḥ kaṅkavayasām 
Subhv śmaśānasthānesminnakhilaguṇavandhye hatatarāv
Subhv api dvitrāḥ kecinna khalu kalavācaḥ śakunayaḥ 
Subhv kimasi vimatiḥ kiṃ vobmādī kṣaṇādabhilakṣyase
Subhv punarapi punaḥ prekṣāpūrvā na kācana te kriyā 
Subhv svayamajalakāṃ jānānopi praviśya marusthalīṃ
Subhv śiśiramadhuraṃ vāri prāptuṃ yadadhvaga vāñchasi 
Subhv parārthe yaḥ pīḍāmanubhavati bhaṅgepi madhuro
Subhv yadīyaḥ sarveṣāmiha khalu vikāropyabhimataḥ 
Subhv na saṃprāpto vṛddhiṃ yadi sa bhṛśamakṣetrapatitaḥ
Subhv kimikṣordoṣosau na punaraguṇāyā marubhavaḥ 
Subhv tāpaḥ svātmani saṃśritadrumalatādoṣodhvagairvarjanaṃ
Subhv satyaṃ tīvratayā tṛṣastava maro kosāvanarthodayaḥ 
Subhv nanvarthaḥ sumahānayaṃ jalalavasvāmyasmayodgarjinaḥ
Subhv saṃnahyanti yatastavopakṛtaye dhārādharāḥ prākṛtāḥ 
Subhv evaṃ codvidhinā kṛtosyupakṛtau kasyāṃcidapyakṣamaḥ
Subhv kāmaṃ mopakṛthāstatastava maro vācyaṃ na dhīro bhava 
Subhv kiṃ tvārānmṛgatṛṣṇayopajanayannambhomucāṃ vañcanāṃ
Subhv premṇā karṣasi tarṣamūrchitadhiyopyanyānataḥ śocyase 
Subhv āmrāḥ kiṃ phalabhāranabhraśiraso ramyāḥ kimūṣmacchidaḥ
Subhv sacchāyāḥ kadalīdrumāḥ surabhayaḥ kiṃ puṣpitāścampakāḥ 
Subhv etāstā niravagrahograkarabhollīḍhāvarūḍhāḥ punaḥ
Subhv śamyo bhrāmyasi mūḍha nirmaruti kiṃ mithyaiva martuṃ marau 
Subhv jalāntarāṇi śvabhreṣu tiṣṭhantu kvāpi yāntu vā 
Subhv surasindhupravāhasya sṛtau ratnākarovadhiḥ 
Subhv kvāntaḥ śūnyo naḍaḥ kvekṣustathāpi sudṛśākṛtī 
Subhv vivekaśūnyamanasāṃ vipralambhāya nirmitau 
Subhv nāsya bhāragrahe śaktirna ca vāhaguṇaḥ kṛṣau 
Subhv devāgārabalīvardastathāpyaśnāti śobhanam 
Subhv nakraḥ svasthānamāsādya gajendramapi karṣati 
Subhv sa eva pracyutaḥ sthānācchunāpi paribhūyate 
Subhv varamunnatalāṅgūlātsaṭādhūnanabhīṣaṇāt 
Subhv siṃhātpādaprahāropi na sṛgālādhirohaṇam 
Subhv gandhaikasāro viphalaḥ sevyaścandanapādapaḥ 
Subhv bhujaṃgāḥ pavanāhārāḥ sevakāḥ sadṛśo vidhiḥ 
Subhv kva gato mṛgo na jīvatyanudinamaśnaṃstṛṇāni vividhāni 
Subhv svayamāhatagajabhoktuḥ siṃhasya tu durlabhā vṛttiḥ 
Subhv vakramaśayyāsaṃsthitamantaḥkoṭaramanekadurgranthi 
Subhv praguṇīkartuṃ śakto durdāru na viśvakarmāpi 
Subhv na tadanukṛtaṃ manāgapi na vā jalaṃ sucirasevitaiḥ śītam 
Subhv andhīkṛte kudīpaiḥ pratyuta dhūmena me nayane 
Subhv utsannamāpaṇamamuṃ drakṣyāmo nirmalaiḥ kadā nayanaiḥ 
Subhv cintāmaṇikācakaṇau viparītaguṇāguṇau yatra 
Subhv ujjvalacampakamukulāśaṅkitayā yaḥ pradīpakaṃ spṛśati 
Subhv kajjalakalaṅkadāhaṃ muktvānyattasya kiṃ ghaṭatām 
Subhv śikharī citaśikharaśikhaḥ sphuradaurvaśikhākadambakombunidhiḥ 
Subhv kasyāpi laṅghanīyau na tu nagarāvakaranikaroyam 
Subhv phaṇamaṇibhāsuraguratarasamarthabahumastake śeṣe 
Subhv kaḥ kṣitibharamudvoḍhuṃ prārthayate kṛpaṇakaṇikīṭān 
Subhv yatnādapi kaḥ paśyecchikhināmāhāraniḥsaraṇamārgam 
Subhv yadi jaladaninadamuditāsta eva mūḍhā na nṛtyeyuḥ 
Subhv śaradi samagraniśākarakaraśatahatatimirasaṃcayā rajanī 
Subhv jaladāntaritārkāmapi divasacchāyāṃ na pūrayati 
Subhv mṛdusubhagaparikararucopyanucitamidamekameva madanasya 
Subhv yadanena kṛtaḥ ketau makaro daṃṣṭrākarālamukhaḥ 
Subhv hemakāra sudhiyo namostu te
Subhv dustareṣu bahuśaḥ parīkṣitum 
Subhv kāñcanābharaṇamaśmanā samaṃ
Subhv yattvayaitadadhuropyate tulām 
Subhv vṛtte eva sa ghaṭondhakūpa yas
Subhv tvatprasādamapanetumakṣamaḥ 
Subhv mudritaṃ tvadhamaceṣṭitaṃ tvayā
Subhv tanmukhāmbukaṇikāḥ pratīcchatā 
Subhv śatapadī sati pādaśate kṣamā
Subhv yadi na goṣpadamapyativartitum 
Subhv kimiyatā dvipadasya hanūmato
Subhv jaladhivikramaṇe vivadāmahe 
Subhv na guruvaṃśaparigrahaśauṇḍatā
Subhv na ca mahāguṇasaṃgrahaṇādaraḥ 
Subhv phalavidhānakathāpi na mārgaṇe
Subhv kimiha lubdhakabāla gṛhedhunā 
Subhv tṛṇamaṇermanujasya ca tadvataḥ
Subhv kimubhayorvipulāśayatocyate 
Subhv tanu tṛṇāgralavāvayavairyayor
Subhv avasite grahaṇa pratipādane 
Subhv bhrātaḥ suvarṇamayarūpakatāracitrā
Subhv laṃkārayatnaghaṭanāsu suvarṇakāra 
Subhv dūrīkuru śramamihādya suvarṇapātre
Subhv durvarṇayojayiturasti mahārghalābhaḥ 
Subhv tanutṛṇāgradhṛtena hṛtaściraṃ
Subhv ka iha yena na mauktikaśaṅkayā 
Subhv sa jalabindurato viparītadṛg
Subhv jagadidaṃ vayamatra sacetanāḥ 
Subhv re dandaśūka tadayuktamapīśvarastvāṃ
Subhv vāllabhyato nayati nūpuradhāma satyam 
Subhv āvarjitālikulasatkṛtimūrchitāni
Subhv kiṃ śiñjitāni bhavataḥ kṣama eṣa kartum 
Subhv suvarṇakāra śravaṇocitāni
Subhv vastūni vikretumihāgatosi 
Subhv adyāpi nāśrāvi yadatra pallyāṃ
Subhv pallīpatirnūnamaviddhakarṇaḥ 
Subhv tānunnatānkṣitibhṛto nanu rūpayāmaḥ
Subhv pakṣakṣayavyatikare mathitaṃ tadojaḥ 
Subhv yuktaṃ kimaurvaśikhinaḥ parikopitasya
Subhv tejasvinopyudadhinirmathanaṃ visoḍhum 
Subhv citraṃ kiyadyadayamambudhirambudaugha
Subhv sindhupravāhaparipūrṇatayā mahīyān 
Subhv tvaṃ tvarthināmupakaroṣi yadalpakūpa
Subhv niṣpīḍya kukṣikuharaṃ hi mahattvametat 
Subhv dhigvāḍavaṃ dahanamarthitayā vipakṣa
Subhv mabhyeti yaḥ svajaṭharapratipūraṇāya 
Subhv dhigvārirāśimapi yastu tathāvidhasya
Subhv śatrorjalairapi na pūrayabhilāṣam 
Subhv śāvānkulāyakagatānparipātukāmā
Subhv nadyāḥ pragṛhya laghu pakṣapuṭena toyam 
Subhv dāvānalaṃ kila siṣeca muhuḥ kopotī
Subhv snigdho jano na khalu cintayate svapīḍām 
Subhv kākaḥ svabhāvacapalaḥ pariśuddhavṛttir
Subhv labdhvā baliṃ svajanamāhvayate parāṃśca 
Subhv carmāsthimāṃsavati hastikalevarepi
Subhv śvā dveṣṭi hanti ca parānkṛpaṇasvabhāvaḥ 
Subhv ādāyi vāri yata eva jahāti bhūyas
Subhv tatraiva yaḥ sa jaladaḥ prathamo jaḍānām 
Subhv vāntaṃ pratīpsati tadeva tadeva yastu
Subhv strotaḥ patiḥ sa nirapatrapasārthavāhaḥ 
Subhv budhyāmahe na bahudhāpi vikalpamānāḥ
Subhv kairnāmabhirvyapadiśāma mahāmatīṃstān 
Subhv yeṣāmaśeṣabhuvanābharaṇasya hemnas
Subhv tattvaṃ vivektumupalāḥ paramaṃ pramāṇam 
Subhv na mlānitānyakhiladhāmavatāṃ mukhāni
Subhv nāstaṃ tamo na ca kṛto bhuvanopakāraḥ 
Subhv sūryātmajohamiti kena guṇena lokān
Subhv pratyāpayiṣyasi śane śapathaṃ vinā tvam 
Subhv saṃrakṣituṃ kṛṣimakāri kṛṣīvalena
Subhv paśyātmanaḥ pratikṛtistṛṇapūruṣoyam 
Subhv stabdhasya niṣkriyatayāstabhiyosya nūna
Subhv matsyanti gomṛgaganāḥ punareva sasyam 
Subhv kasyānimeṣavitate nayane divauko
Subhv lokādṛte jagati te api vai gṛhītvā 
Subhv piṇḍe prasāritamukhena time kimetad
Subhv dṛṣṭaṃ na bāliśa viśadbaḍiśaṃ tvayāntaḥ 
Subhv ā janmanaḥ kuśalamaṇvapi te kujanman
Subhv pāṃso tvayā yadi kṛtaṃ vada tattvametat 
Subhv utthāpitosyanalasārathinā yadarthaṃ
Subhv duṣṭena tatkuru kalaṅkaya viśvametat 
Subhv puṃstvādapi pravicaledyapi yadyadhopi
Subhv yāyādyapi praṇayanena mahānapi syāt 
Subhv abhyuddharettadapi viśvamitīdṛśīyaṃ
Subhv kenāpi dikprakaṭitā puruṣottamena 
Subhv svalpāśayaḥ svakulaśilpavikalpameva
Subhv yaḥ kalpayanskhalati kācavaṇikpiśācaḥ 
Subhv grastaḥ sa kaustubhamaṇīndrasapatnaratna
Subhv niryatnagumphapaṭuvaikaṭikerṣyayāntaḥ 
Subhv devī kva durgatiharā bhaginī bhavānī
Subhv devo haraḥ kva bhaginīpatirārtabandhuḥ 
Subhv ambhonidhau kva śaraṇāgatavṛttidainyaṃ
Subhv maināka nākathayitavyamidaṃ tvayā naḥ 
Subhv tuṅgātmatāstaśikharasya vṛthaiva bhānor
Subhv nālambinī bhavati yāstamaye prapitsoḥ 
Subhv ślāghyaḥ sa tāmarasanālaguṇopi daitya
Subhv bhītyā yametya marutāṃ patirālalambe 
Subhv gṛhaṃ śmaśānaṃ gajacarma cāmbaraṃ
Subhv vilepanaṃ bhasma vṛṣaśca vāhanam 
Subhv kubera he vittapate na lajjase
Subhv priyasya te sakhyuriyaṃ daridratā 
Subhv naikatra śaktiviratiḥ kvacidasti sarva
Subhv bhāvāḥ svabhāvapariniṣṭhitatāratamyāḥ 
Subhv ākalpamaurvadahanena nipīyamāna
Subhv mambhodhimekaculakena papāvagastyaḥ 
Subhv viṣṇurbibharti bhagavānakhilāṃ dharitrīṃ
Subhv taṃ pannagastamapi tatsahitaṃ payodhiḥ 
Subhv kumbhodbhavastamapibatkhalu helayaiva
Subhv satyaṃ na kaścidavadhirmahatāṃ mahimnaḥ 
Subhv āropitaḥ pṛthunitambataṭe taruṇyā
Subhv kaṇṭhe ca bāhulatayā niviḍaṃ gṛhītaḥ 
Subhv utuṅgapīnakucanirbharapīḍitoyaṃ
Subhv kumbhaḥ karīṣadahanasya phalāni bhuṅkte 
Subhv ābaddhakṛtrimasaṭāvalitāṃsabhitti
Subhv rāropyate mṛgapateḥ padavīṃ yadi śvā 
Subhv mattebhakumbhataṭapāṭanalampaṭasya
Subhv nādaṃ kariṣyati kathaṃ hariṇādhipasya 
Subhv mukhamapi pariśiṣṭaṃ yasya tejaḥprasūtiṃ
Subhv kharakiraṇamathenduṃ grāsapātrīkaroti 
Subhv yadi kila vapurasya prābhaviṣyatsamagraṃ
Subhv kimiva kimiva rāhurnākariṣyattadānīm 
Subhv yatpuṣpapallavaphalāhitasāmyamohair
Subhv na jñāyate śuka tava sthitirasthitirvā 
Subhv taddāḍimaṃ tyajasi naiva phalāśayā tvam
Subhv arthāturo na gaṇayatyapakarṣadoṣam 
Subhv varamiha ravitāpaiḥ kiṃ na śīrṇāsi gulme
Subhv kimu davadahanairvā sarvadāhaṃ na dagdhā 
Subhv yadahṛdayajanaughairvṛntaparṇānabhijñair
Subhv itarakusumamadhye mālati prombhitāsi 
Subhv kimidamucitaṃ śuddheḥ spaṣṭaṃ sapakṣasamunnateḥ
Subhv phalapariṇateryuktaṃ prāptuṃ guṇapraṇayasya te 
Subhv kṣaṇamupagataḥ karṇopāntaṃ parasya puraḥ sthitān
Subhv viśikha nipatankrūraṃ dūrānnṛśaṃsa nihaṃsi yat 
Subhv sa hemālaṃkāraḥ kṣitipatanalagnena rajasā
Subhv tathā dainyaṃ nīto narapatiśiraḥślāghyavibhavaḥ 
Subhv yathā loṣṭabhrāntivyavahitavivekavyatikaro
Subhv vilokyainaṃ lokaḥ pariharati pādakṣatibhayāt 
Subhv āhūteṣu vihaṃgameṣu maśako nāyānpurovāryate
Subhv madhye vā dhuri vā vasaṃstṛṇamaṇirdhatte maṇīnāṃ rucam 
Subhv khadyotopi na kampate pracalituṃ madhyepi tejasvināṃ
