Subhv dhiksāmānyamacetanaṃ prabhumivānāmṛṣṭatattvāntaram 
Subhv evaṃ cetsarasasvabhāvaparatā jāḍyaṃ kimetādṛśaṃ
Subhv yadyastyeva nisargataḥ saralatā kiṃ granthimattedṛśī 
Subhv mūlaṃ cecchuvi paṅkajaśrutiriyaṃ kasmādguṇā yadyamī
Subhv kiṃ chidrāṇi sakhe mṛṇāla bhavatastattvaṃ na manyāmahe 
Subhv tvaṃ bhogī yadi kuṇḍalī yadi bhavāṃstvaṃ cedbhujaṃgaḥ sakhe
Subhv dhatse cenmukuṭaṃ saratnamuraga svastyastu te kiṃ tataḥ 
Subhv asthāne yadi kañcukaṃ tyajasi tannāsmākamatra spṛhā
Subhv kiṃ tu krūraviṣolkayā dahasi yadbhrātaḥ ka eṣa grahaḥ 
Subhv maulau sanmaṇayo gṛhaṃ giriguhā tyāgaḥ kilātmatvaco
Subhv niryatnopanataiśca vṛttiranilairekatra caryedṛśī 
Subhv anyatrānṛju vartma vāgvitasanā dṛṣṭau viṣaṃ dṛśyate
Subhv yādṛktāmanu dīpako jvalati kiṃ bhoginsakhe kinvidam 
Subhv bhūyāṃsyasya mukhāni nāma viditaivāste mahāsattvatā
Subhv kadrvāḥ prākprasavoyamatra kupite cintyaṃ yathedaṃ jagat 
Subhv trailokyādbhutamīdṛśaṃ tu caritaṃ śoṣasya yenāsya sā
Subhv pronmṛjyeva nivartitā viṣadharajñānepi durvarṇikā 
Subhv kiṃ tena hemagiriṇā rajatādriṇā vā
Subhv yasyāśrayeṇa taravastaravasta eva 
Subhv manyāmahe malayameva yadāśritāni
Subhv śāhoṭanimbakuṭajānyapi candanāni 
Subhv yāndigdhvaiva kṛtā viṣeṇa kusṛtiryeṣāṃ kiyadgaṇyate
Subhv lokaṃ hantumanāgasaṃ dvirasanā randhreṣu ye jāgrati 
Subhv vyālāstepi dadhatyamī sadasatormūḍhā maṇīnmūrdhabhir
Subhv naucityādguṇaśālināṃ kvacidapi bhraṃśostyalaṃ cintayā 
Subhv tatpratyastratayā dhṛto na tu kṛtaḥ samyaksvatantro bhayāt
Subhv svasthastānpratighātayediti yathākāmaṃ na saṃpoṣitaḥ 
Subhv saṃśuṣyanvṛṣadaṃśa eṣa kurutāṃ mūkaḥ sthitopyatra kiṃ
Subhv gehe kiṃ bahunādhunā gṛhapateścaurāścarantyākhavaḥ 
Subhv svātmīyānna dadāsi cetphaṇamaṇīnmā dāḥ parārthaṃ parair
Subhv yatkiṃcinnihitaṃ ruṇatsi kimidaṃ nidhyādi duṣṭāśayā 
Subhv etattāvadalaṃ bhavantamaparaṃ pṛcchāmi kasmādahe
Subhv phūtkārairviṣavahnivegagurubhirdandahyasemuṃ janam 
Subhv niḥsārāḥ sutarāṃ laghuprakṛtayo yogyā na kārye kvacic
Subhv chuṣyantodya jarattṛṇādyavayavāḥ prāptāḥ svatantreṣu ye 
Subhv antaḥsāraparāṅmukheṇa dhigaho te mārutenāmunā
Subhv paśyātyantacalena vartma mahatāmākāśamāropitāḥ 
Subhv ye jātyā laghavaḥ sadaiva gaṇanāṃ yātā na ye kutracit
Subhv padbhyāmeva vimarditāḥ pratidinaṃ bhūmau nilīnāściram 
Subhv utkṣiptāścapalāśayena marutā paśyāntarikṣe sakhe
Subhv tuṅgānāmupari sthitaṃ kṣitibhṛtāṃ kurvantyamī pāṃsavaḥ 
Subhv anīrṣyāḥ śrotāro mama vacasi cedvacmi tadahaṃ
Subhv svapakṣādbhetavyaṃ bahu na tu vipakṣātprabhavataḥ 
Subhv tamasyākrāntāśe kiyadapi hi tejovayavinaḥ
Subhv svaśaktyā bhāsante divasakṛti satyeva na punaḥ 
Subhv sāṃmukhyaṃ vastujātaṃ nayati nanu cidīśasya yaddarśanāḍhyaṃ
Subhv netradvandvaṃ kilaitadvimalamiti tatonyāṅgasaṅgaṃ vihāya 
Subhv ghrāṇaṃ vaṃśābhirāmaṃ parimalanirataṃ cakṣuṣormadhyabhāge
Subhv nityaṃ līnaṃ na cāsminmṛgasi nayanayoḥ śvāsamāmuñca khinne 
Subhv etattasya mukhātkiyatkamalinīpattre kaṇaṃ pāthaso
Subhv yanmuktāphalamityamaṃsta sa jaḍaḥ śṛṇvanyadasmādapi 
Subhv aṅgulyagralaghukriyāpravilayinyādīyamāne śanais
Subhv tatroḍḍīya gate hahetyanudinaṃ nidrāti nāntaḥśucā 
Subhv āstetraiva sarasyaho bata kiyānsaṃtoṣapakṣagraho
Subhv haṃsasyāsya manāṅna dhāvati matiḥ śrīdhāmni padme kvacit 
Subhv suptodyāpi vibudhyate na taditastāvatpratīkṣāmahe
Subhv velāmityuṣasi priyā madhulihaḥ soḍhuṃ tu eva kṣamāḥ 
Subhv vātāhāratayā jagadviṣadharairāśvāsya niḥśeṣitaṃ
Subhv te grastāḥ punarabhratoyakaṇikātīvravratairbarhibhiḥ 
Subhv tepi krūracamūrucarmavasanairnītāḥ kṣayaṃ lubdhakair
Subhv dambhasya sphuritaṃ vidannapi jano jālmo guṇānīhate 
Subhv nāmāpyanyatarornimīlitamabhūttattāvadunmīlitaṃ
Subhv prasthāne skhalataḥ svavartmani vidheranyairgṛhītaḥ karaḥ 
Subhv lokaścāyamadṛṣṭadarśanadaśādṛgvaiśasāduddhṛto
Subhv yuktaṃ kāṣṭhika lūnavānyadasitāmāmrālimākālikīm 
Subhv ūḍhā yena mahādhuraḥ suviṣame mārge sadaikākinā
Subhv soḍho yena kadācideva na nije goṣṭhenyaśauṇḍadhvaniḥ 
Subhv āsīdyaśca gavāṃ gaṇasya tilakastasyaiva saṃpratyaho
Subhv dhikkaṣṭaṃ dhavalasya jātajaraso goḥ paṇyamuddhoṣyate 
Subhv bhekena kvaṇatā saroṣaparuṣaṃ yatkṛṣṇasarpānane
Subhv dātuṃ karṇacapeṭamujjhitabhiyā hastaḥ samullāsitaḥ 
Subhv yaccādhomukhamakṣiṇī pidadhatā nāgena tatra sthitaṃ
Subhv tatsarvaṃ viṣamantriṇo bhagavataḥ kasyāpi līlāyitam 
Subhv nityaṃ tīrthe nivāsaḥ prakṛtiratitarāṃ snigdhamugdhasvabhāvā
Subhv vṛttirdaivāddhi vaktre gagananipatitairnirmalairvārileśaiḥ 
Subhv itthaṃ sarvaṃ vilokya prakaṭamiha time mugdhalokena loke
Subhv sādhutvaṃ darśitaṃ te bahirabahiramī kaṇṭakāḥ kena dṛṣṭāḥ 
Subhv mṛtyorāsyamivātataṃ dhanuramī cāśīviṣābhāḥ śarāḥ
Subhv śikṣā sāpi jitārjunā pratibhayaṃ sarvāṅganimnā gatiḥ 
Subhv antaḥ krauryamaho śaṭhasya madhuraṃ hā hāri geyaṃ mukhe
Subhv vyādhasyāsya yathā bhaviṣyati tathā manye vanaṃ nirmṛgam 
Subhv dhigvyomno mahimānametu dalaśaḥ proccaistadīyaṃ padaṃ
Subhv nindyāṃ daivagatiṃ prayātvabhavanistasyāstu śūnyasya vā 
Subhv yenotkṣiptakarasya naṣṭamahasaḥ śrāntasya saṃtāpino
Subhv mitrasyāpi nirāśrayasya na kṛtaṃ dhṛtyai karālambanam 
Subhv digdāhaikarate vanāntakara te jvālā na me rocate
Subhv dugdhaṃ svāśrayamudyatasya bhavato necchanti vṛddhiṃ janāḥ 
Subhv mūlānyasya mahībhṛto dalayituṃ durvedhasā nirmitaḥ
Subhv ko vā na tvayi śaṅkate khala jagatkhedāvahe dāva he 
Subhv kṣutkṣāmeṇa kathaṃ kathaṃcidaniśaṃ gātraṃ kṛśaṃ bibhratā
Subhv bhrāntaṃ yena gṛhe gṛhe gṛhavatāmucchiṣṭapiṇḍārthinā 
Subhv asthnaḥ khaṇḍamavāpya daivapatitaṃ śūnyāṃ trilokīmimāṃ
Subhv manvāno dhigaho sa eva saramāputrodya siṃhāyate 
Subhv śuṣkasnāyuvasāvasekamalinaṃ nirmāṃsamapyasthi goḥ
Subhv śvā labdhā paritoṣameti na tu tattasya kṣudhaḥ śāntaye 
Subhv siṃho jambukamaṅkamāgatamapi tyaktvā nihanti dvipaṃ
Subhv sarvaḥ kṛchragatopi vāñchati janaḥ sattvānurūpaṃ phalam 
Subhv kāluṣyaṃ payasāṃ vilokya śanakairuḍḍīya haṃsā gatā
Subhv dhārājarjarakesarāsphuṭarucaḥ padmā nimignā jale 
Subhv sā sarvartusukhāvatārapadavī channā tṛṇairnūtanaiḥ
Subhv kaṣṭaṃ tādṛgapi svabhāvavimalaṃ vṛdchyaiva naṣṭaṃ saraḥ 
Subhv ye saṃtoṣasukhaprabuddhamanasasteṣāmabhinno mṛdo
Subhv yepyete dhanalobhasaṃkuladhiyasteṣāṃ tu dūre nṛṇām 
Subhv itthaṃ kasya kṛte kṛtaḥ sa vidhinā tādṛkpadaṃ saṃpadāṃ
Subhv svātmanyeva samāptahemamahimā merurna me rocate 
Subhv dravyāṇāmadharottaravyatikaro bhagnāśayānāmadho
Subhv bījānāṃ nayanaṃ svayaṃ ca nijavacchidrakriyānveṣaṇam 
Subhv vyūhābandhavidhāyibhirgatabhayairmugdhaprasuptārbhakaṃ
Subhv śūnyaṃ prāpya nivāsamākhubhiraho kiṃ kiṃ na yadyatkṛtam 
Subhv anyonyasya layaṃ bhayādiva mahābhūteṣu yāteṣvalaṃ
Subhv kalpānte parameka eva sa taruḥ skandhoccayairjṛmbhate 
Subhv vinyasya trijaganti kukṣikuhare devena yasyāsyate
Subhv śākhāgre śiśuneva sevitajalakrīḍāvilāsālasam 
trivikramasya
Subhv trailokyopakṛtiprasaktamanaso devasya śaṃbhoḥ priyā
Subhv jātā śailakule varairabhimatairānandayantī surān 
Subhv mlecchānāmapi vāñchitārpaṇaparā svasyāspadasyāmbikā
Subhv vindhyasyonnatimātanoti na nijāṃ daivasya kīdṛgbalam 
bhā amṛtadattasya
Subhv kiṃ tvaṃ hālika mūḍhadhīrhataphalaṃ mā mā kṛthā lāṅgalaṃ
Subhv kṣetraṃ naiva bhavatyadhaḥ kaṭhinatā naivātra dṛṣṭā tvayā 
Subhv ullekhopi na jāyatetra virama kleśaḥ phalaṃ kevalaṃ
Subhv nirbījā bahavo gatāśca satataṃ dṛṣṭāḥ śrutā vā na kim kasyāpi
Subhv koyaṃ bhrāntiprakārastava pavana ghanāvaskarasthānajātaṃ
Subhv tejasvivrātasevye nabhasi nayasi yatpāṃsupūraṃ pratiṣṭhām 
Subhv yasminnutthāpyamāne jananayanapathopadravastāvadāstāṃ
Subhv kenopāyena sahyo vapuṣi malinatādoṣa eṣa tvayaiva 
bhā amṛtadattasya
Subhv jātaḥ kūrmaḥ sa ekaḥ pṛthubhuvanabharāyārpitaṃ yena pṛṣṭhaṃ
Subhv ślāghyaṃ janma dhruvasya bhramati niyamitaṃ yatra tejasvicakram 
Subhv saṃjātavyarthapakṣāḥ parahitakaraṇe nopariṣṭānna cādho
Subhv brahmāṇḍodumbarāntarmaśakavadapare jantavo jātanaṣṭāḥ kasyāpi
Subhv kaṭu raṭasi kimevaṃ karṇayoḥ kuñjarāre
Subhv raviditanijabuddhe kiṃ na vijñātamasti 
Subhv śiratarakaradaṃṣṭrāṭaṅkanirbhinnakumbhaṃ
Subhv maśaka galakarandhre hastiyūthaṃ mamajja kasyāpi
Subhv udrarjankuṭilastaṭāśrayatarupronmūlanoḍḍāmaro
Subhv mā garvīḥ saritaḥ pravāha jaladhiṃ prakṣobhayāmīti bhoḥ 
Subhv svāṃ sattāṃ yadi vāñchasi bhrama maruṣvevāḥsva tatraiva vā
Subhv dūre vāḍavavahniratra tu mahāsattvairviśanpīyase 
Subhv sthairyaṃ tuṅgaśirā jagatsthitikṛte velāmahībhṛcchrito
Subhv dūrātpreraṇayā kalāvata imaṃ krāntuṃ jalānāṃ pate 
Subhv mithyā vāñchasi kiṃ tatastava paraṃ syādratnasattvakṣayo
Subhv nūnaṃ ghaṭṭanamāpya pādatalagastvasyaiva cānte luṭheḥ 
Subhv āndolayasyavirataṃ gaganārkamaṅke
Subhv tārāgaṇaṃ ca śaśinaṃ ca tathetarāṇi 
Subhv tejāṃsi bhāsurataḍitprabhṛtīni sādho
Subhv citraṃ tathāpi na jahāsi yadāndhyamantaḥ 
Subhv ayaṃ sa bhuvanatrayaprathitasaṃyamaḥ śaṃkaro
Subhv bibharti vapuṣādhunā virahakātaraḥ kāminīm 
Subhv anena kila nirjitā vayamiti priyāyāḥ karaṃ
Subhv kareṇa paripīḍayañjayati jātahāsaḥ smaraḥ 
Subhv bhrūśārṅgākṛṣṭamuktāḥ kuvalayamadhupavyomalakṣmīmuṣo ye
Subhv kṣīvā ye kṛṣṇaśārā narahṛdayabhidastārakakrūraśalyāḥ 
Subhv te dīrghāpāṅgapuṅkhāḥ smitaviṣaviṣamāḥ pakṣmalāḥ strīkaṭākṣāḥ
Subhv pāyāsurvotivīryāstribhuvanajayinaḥ pañcabāṇasya bāṇāḥ 
Subhv gaccha gacchasi cetkānta panthānaḥ santu te śivāḥ 
Subhv mamāpi janma tatraiva bhūyādyatra gato bhavān
